### [41] [Fine-Tuning Improves Information Conveyance in Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30844)
*Yuwei Cheng,Weiyi Tian,Haifeng Xu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文通过引入“树冠熵（CE*）”这一新度量指标，证明了微调不仅能降低大模型的不确定性，更重要的是，它将不确定性重构为更高效、更具语义价值的生成空间，实现了从简单的减少不确定性到优化生成效率的范式转变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究在分析微调对大模型不确定性和多样性的影响时，往往忽视了“输出长度”这一关键混淆因素，导致无法准确评估不确定性在整个生成过程中的分布规律。因此，本研究旨在通过引入新的数学框架，揭示微调对模型生成行为的深层影响。

Method: 研究者提出了“树冠熵”（Canopy Entropy, CE*）这一新型度量方法。该方法将语言生成视为一棵树，通过联合度量输出长度 $N$ 和生成序列 $Y_{1:N}$ 的总香农熵 $H(N, Y_{1:N}\mid X)$，能够量化生成空间的有效大小，并引入长度-熵相关性指标（ρ(N, r_N)）来分析信息传递效率。

Result: 实验表明，微调后的模型在总熵降低的同时，长度与熵率的相关性反而增强。此外，控制多种变量后发现，微调使模型在将“词元不确定性”转化为“语义多样性”方面的效率提升了近三倍，证明了微调显著提升了模型生成的有效性和结构化程度。

Conclusion: 微调并非单纯地降低了大型语言模型的输出不确定性，而是从根本上重组了这种不确定性，使其转化为更高效、更具语义意义的生成内容。这一发现挑战了“微调总是减少模型多样性”的传统观点。

Abstract: Fine-tuning is often believed to reduce uncertainty and diversity in large language models, but existing analyses overlook output length, a key confounder, and therefore fail to capture how uncertainty is distributed across an entire generation rollout. To address this, we propose Canopy Entropy ($\mathrm{CE}^\star$), a measure that views language generation from a tree perspective, where ``canopy'' represents the space of all possible rollouts, making $\mathrm{CE}^\star$ naturally quantify the effective size of the generation space. $\mathrm{CE}^\star$ jointly captures uncertainty in both the output length $N$ and the generated sequence $Y_{1:N}$ -- indeed, we show that it equals to total Shannon entropy $H(N, Y_{1:N}\mid X)$, where $X$ denotes the prompt. This formulation yields interpretable metrics, including a length-entropy correlation term $ρ(N, r_N)$, where $r_N$ is the entropy rate, quantifying information conveyance efficiency by indicating whether longer outputs are more or less informative per token. Empirically, across tasks and model families, we find that fine-tuned models consistently exhibit stronger positive correlation $ρ(N, r_N)$, even when total entropy decreases. Furthermore, after controlling for model family, task, prompt, and output-length effects, we find that fine-tuning nearly triples the correlation strength between entropy rate and semantic diversity, suggesting that aligned models convert token uncertainty into semantic diversity more efficiently. Overall, these results demonstrate that fine-tuning does not simply reduce uncertainty, but fundamentally reorganizes it into more informative and semantically meaningful generations. Our code is available at https://github.com/WeiyiTian/canopy-entropy.

*Yijiong Yu,Huazheng Wang,Shuai Yuan,Ruilong Ren,Ji Pei*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: SPD是一种新型推理加速框架，通过在流水线并行各阶段并行执行推测任务，解决了传统推测解码的串行延迟问题，显著提升了LLM的解码速度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有推测解码方案依赖多Token预测，导致预测难度随Token位置增加而上升，且草稿生成过程存在串行延迟，限制了推理加速效果。

Method: 提出“推测流水线解码”（Speculative Pipeline Decoding, SPD）框架：将目标大模型划分为多个流水线阶段，利用跨深度的中间特征聚合进行下一Token的推测，使推测过程与模型流水线执行过程严格并行，从而实现无气泡的流水线填充。

Result: 实验结果表明，SPD相比主流基准测试方法实现了更高的理论加速比，能够有效维持高接受率并消除流水线空转（气泡）。

Abstract: Speculative Decoding (SD) accelerates low-concurrency LLM inference by employing a draft-then-verify paradigm. However, mainstream methods typically rely on multi-token prediction, which introduces escalating prediction difficulty and serial drafting latency. To address these, we propose Speculative Pipeline Decoding (SPD), a groundbreaking framework that unlocks the true potential of pipeline parallelism. By partitioning the target LLM into $n$ pipeline stages, SPD allows LLM to process $n$ tokens in parallel to accelerate decoding. To continuous fill the pipeline in single sequence decoding, a speculation module aggregates intermediate features across different pipeline depths to predict the next token, executing strictly in parallel with the target model's pipeline step, to realize bounded difficulty, higher acceptance rates, and zero latency bubbles. Our experiments demonstrate that SPD achieves a significantly higher theoretical speedup compared to mainstream baselines, offering a highly scalable solution for LLM decoding acceleration. Our code is available at https://github.com/yuyijiong/speculative_pipeline_decoding

Existing methods predominantly distinguish different training data based on the text features themselves, decoupled from LLMs' own understanding and representation of the data. To address this issue, we propose a Model-Aware Diverse Core Set Selection method, which distinguishes data features based on the neural activation states during LLM inference. This approach serves as an efficient instantiation of coverage-based selection using model-intrinsic activation features to ensure the diversity in the core set. We extensively evaluate our method on six benchmarks that cover five distinct tasks. In our method, the core set selected by the 3B-parameter LLM performs effectively when utilized to fine-tune larger models with 7B, 8B, and 13B parameters. ### [44] [dMoE: dLLMs with Learnable Block Experts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30876)
*Sicheng Feng,Zigeng Chen,Gongfan Fang,Xinyin Ma,Xinchao Wang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 为解决扩散大语言模型中 MoE 架构带来的推理内存瓶颈，本文提出了 dMoE，通过将 Token 级路由聚合为块级路由，在几乎不损失性能的前提下，显著减少了激活专家数量，提升了推理效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩散大语言模型（dLLMs）结合专家混合（MoE）架构时存在根本性矛盾：dLLMs 的块并行解码机制与 MoE 逐 Token 独立路由机制导致单次推理激活的专家数量激增，引发严重的内存带宽瓶颈问题。

Method: 提出了一种简单的块级混合专家（dMoE）框架，其核心是将每个块内各 Token 的专家分布聚合为统一的块级专家分布，利用该统一分布指导专家路由，从而强制块内 Token 共享相同的专家激活决策。

Result: 实验表明，dMoE 将平均每个块内激活的唯一专家数量从 69.5 个大幅降至 14.6 个，同时保留了 99.11% 的原始性能；此外，该方法减少了 76.64% 到 79.84% 的内存使用量，并实现了 1.14 倍到 1.66 倍的端到端推理速度提升。

Conclusion: dMoE 提出了一种有效的块级专家混合架构，通过统一块内所有 Token 的专家路由，成功解决了扩散大语言模型中块并行解码与 Token 级专家路由之间的冲突，实现了在保持模型性能的同时，大幅降低内存占用和提升推理速度。

Abstract: Diffusion Large Language Models (dLLMs) have recently emerged as a promising alternative to autoregressive models, offering competitive performance while naturally supporting parallel decoding. However, as dLLMs are increasingly integrated with Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) architectures to scale model capacity, a fundamental mismatch arises between block parallel decoding and token-level expert selection. Specifically, each dLLM forward pass processes multiple tokens with bidirectional dependencies, whereas conventional MoE layers route each token independently. This mismatch substantially increases the number of uniquely activated experts, making inference increasingly memory-bound. To address this, we propose dMoE, a simple yet effective block-level MoE framework. The central idea of dMoE is to aggregate token-level expert distributions within each block into a unified block-level expert distribution, which is then used to guide expert routing in a more coherent manner. In this way, dMoE substantially reduces the number of uniquely activated experts during inference without sacrificing performance, thereby mitigating the memory-bound bottleneck. Extensive experiments across a variety of benchmarks demonstrate the effectiveness of dMoE. On average, dMoE reduces the number of uniquely activated experts from 69.5 to 14.6 while retaining 99.11% of the original performance. Meanwhile, it reduces memory usage by 76.64% to 79.84% and achieves 1.14$\times$ to 1.66$\times$ end-to-end latency speedup. Code is available at: https://github.com/fscdc/dMoE

### [45] [PatchWorld: Gradient-Free Optimization of Executable World Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30880)
*Jiaxin Bai,Yue Guo,Yifei Dong,Jiaxuan Xiong,Tianshi Zheng,Yixia Li,Tianqing Fang,Yufei Li,Yisen Gao,Haoyu Huang,Zhongwei Xie,Hong Ting Tsang,Zihao Wang,Lihui Liu,Jeff Pan,Yangqiu Song*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: PatchWorld 是一种通过反例引导的代码修复技术，将离线轨迹转化为可执行 Python 世界模型的框架。它在无需 LLM 调用的情况下，实现了在部分可观测环境下的高效规划，并揭示了观测保真度与决策效用之间的权衡机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在文本智能体环境中，通常将环境建模为 POMDP。现有研究较少关注如何利用可执行代码作为世界模型来处理部分可观测性问题，且黑盒预测模型缺乏可解释性和可修改性，因此需要一种能进行预测、规划且可被检查与局部修复的符号化世界模型方案。

Method: 提出 PatchWorld 框架，采用一种免梯度（gradient-free）的方案。该方法利用离线轨迹，通过基于反例引导的代码修复（counterexample-guided code repair）技术，将轨迹诱导为可执行的 Python 世界模型，并以此进行信念状态（belief-state）的预测与规划，无需在模型预测模块内部调用 LLM。

Result: 在七个 AgentGym 环境中，PatchWorld-Simple 实现了最高的基于代码的规划得分，宏观成功率达到 76.4%（单步预测）。此外，研究揭示了人类定义的残差记忆偏差会提升观测保真度，但会削弱决策效用的现象。

Conclusion: PatchWorld 证明了通过可执行代码构建世界模型在部分可观测环境下的有效性。研究发现，在可执行世界模型中存在一种权衡：单纯提高观测保真度可能会损害动作决策的效用，即观测准确性与策略执行能力之间并非总是正相关的。

Abstract: Text-agent environments are typically modeled as partially observable Markov decision processes (POMDPs), assuming that the simulator's latent state and transition dynamics are hidden from the agent. Yet little work has examined whether executable code can be induced to serve as a world model for prediction and planning under partial observability. We introduce PatchWorld, a gradient-free framework that turns offline trajectories into executable Python world models through counterexample-guided code repair. Instead of predicting the next observation with a black-box model, PatchWorld induces symbolic belief-state programs whose action updates can be inspected, replayed, and locally patched. Across seven AgentGym environments, PatchWorld-Simple achieves the highest code-based planning score among evaluated methods, reaching 76.4\% macro success in live one-step lookahead while invoking no LLM calls inside the world-model prediction module itself. We further find that a human-specified residual-memory bias improves surface observation fidelity but weakens decision utility. This exposes a tradeoff in executable world models, since improving observation fidelity can come at the expense of action-discriminative dynamics, and vice versa. Code is available at https://github.com/HKBU-KnowComp/PatchWorld.

</details>


### [46] [The Flip Side of RLHF: On-Policy Feedback for Reward Model Self-Supervised Improvement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30888)
*Xiaobo Wang,Tong Wu,Min Tang,Jiaqi Li,Qi Liu,Zilong Zheng*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了 SAVE 框架，通过引入价值锚定与自监督策略内反馈机制，高效更新奖励模型，解决了传统奖励模型在策略演进中的泛化难题，在多项基准测试中取得了显著优于现有方法的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 语言模型对齐中奖励模型的构建受限于人工标注或判别模型提供的高成本、低多样性数据。此外，当模型策略在训练过程中发生演进时，静态奖励模型往往无法有效适应，导致性能提升受限。

Method: 提出 SAVE 框架，利用价值函数对策略内（on-policy）响应进行评估。通过“提示词特定值头（prompt-specific value head）”作为自适应锚点，将奖励评分转化为监督信号；同时引入优势计算与样本过滤机制，并采用对比学习目标函数对奖励模型进行更新。

Result: 在六个多样化基准测试中表现出色，全面超越现有方法。同时，该方法在 GRPO、RLOO 和 GSPO 三种强化学习算法以及不同的模型骨架上均表现出高度的稳定性和一致的性能提升。

Conclusion: SAVE 框架通过引入价值锚定机制，成功解决了奖励模型在面对策略演进时的性能瓶颈。它证明了利用策略内反馈和自监督学习能够有效提升奖励模型的泛化能力与准确性，为强化学习对齐提供了高效且鲁棒的新路径。

Abstract: Building strong reward models (RMs) for language model alignment is bottlenecked by the cost and difficulty of acquiring diverse and reliable preference data from human annotation or judge models. It is dramatically worse as the policy evolves beyond the static RM training. Therefore, we propose SAVE (Self-supervised reward model improvement via Value-Anchored On-policy feedback), a framework that grades on-policy responses as feedback by using the value function for on-policy RM training. SAVE naturally converts the reward-graded on-policy responses into supervision with a prompt-specific value head as an adaptive anchor. It computes RM advantages and filters ambiguous samples to update the RM via a contrastive objective. The effectiveness of SAVE for enhancing RM training is strongly validated through rigorous empirical evaluation across six diverse benchmarks. It achieves outperforming results across all datasets while maintaining consistent improvements across three RL algorithms (GRPO, RLOO, GSPO) and different policy backbones.

</details>

*Tianjie Ju,Yueqing Sun,Zheng Wu,Wei Zhang,Yaqi Huo,Xi Su,Qi Gu,Xunliang Cai,Gongshen Liu,Zhuosheng Zhang*

Method: 1. 筛选去除了强领域知识依赖的原子任务，聚焦通用开放世界推理；2. 采用 ReAct 式能力构建框架，通过组合原子任务生成隐式多跳任务；3. 提出多智能体合成工作流（Multi-agent synthesis workflow），自动化生成任务图、场景及基于规则的评估器；4. 利用人类评估验证了多智能体生成实例的可靠性，并对主流 MLLM 进行了实证基准测试。

Result: 实验表明，当前的先进 MLLM 在处理单跳任务时表现尚可，但随着任务跨度增加、涉及隐式前置条件协调时，性能会迅速下降；研究还发现模型性能提升并不与模型大小或单一的“思考”模式呈线性正相关。

Conclusion: MineExplorer 揭示了现有 MLLM 在处理长跨度、需要隐式多跳推理的开放世界探索任务时表现较差。研究表明，仅仅依靠扩大模型规模或单纯的“思考”模式并不足以解决复杂的探索挑战，未来的研究需要重点解决长轨迹中的前置条件规划与协调问题。

Abstract: Multimodal large language models (MLLMs) have shown strong capabilities in perception, reasoning, and action generation. However, their ability to sustain exploration in dynamic open worlds remains unclear. Existing embodied and game-based benchmarks often compress interaction into short-horizon tasks or entangle success with domain-specific game mechanics. In this paper, we introduce MineExplorer benchmark for evaluating open-world exploration capabilities of MLLM agents in Minecraft. We first filter atomic tasks whose solutions rely heavily on Minecraft-specific knowledge to better reflect general open-world reasoning. Then we organize the benchmark around a ReAct-style capability formulation and compose atomic tasks into implicit multi-hop tasks. To further construct reliable instances, MineExplorer uses a multi-agent synthesis workflow that jointly designs task graphs, sandbox scenes, and rule-based milestone evaluators. Human evaluation shows that the multi-agent synthesis workflow produces significantly more reliable instances than a single-agent baseline. Experiments with advanced MLLM agents show that open-world exploration remains challenging, as strong models can handle many single-hop tasks but degrade sharply when hidden prerequisites must be coordinated over longer trajectories. Further analysis finds that task difficulty tracks agent completion, and larger models or thinking modes do not consistently translate into better performance. Code and dataset are available at https://github.com/Jometeorie/MineExplorer.

*Nattavudh Powdthavee*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了LLMs的道德推理深受训练语料中隐含的制度环境影响，且这种影响在模糊情境下最易显现，而明确的提示词可能会掩盖模型固有的这种跨语言道德差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在探究大型语言模型（LLMs）在不同语言中表现出的道德推理系统性差异的根源，验证语言是否通过编码制度环境，从而使模型继承了特定于制度的道德先验。

Method: 研究采用了两个预注册实验。实验一通过显式的制度框架测试模型在制度依赖情境下的道德判断；实验二通过制度模糊的情境（隐式制度风险），对比不同语言模型在跨文化道德困境中的表现，并将其与现实世界的制度质量数据进行相关性分析。

Result: 研究发现，在显式制度框架下，跨语言道德分歧并未随制度差异而显著变化；但在制度模糊的情境下，跨语言道德分歧显著增加，且与现实世界中的制度质量差异密切相关。显式框架的使用会削弱这种潜在的制度影响。

Conclusion: 大型语言模型在处理道德推理时，会内化并表现出与其训练数据中语言所代表的制度环境相关的道德先验。当情境具有制度模糊性时，这种差异尤为明显，而显式的制度框架反而会抑制这些潜在差异的表达。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) exhibit systematic differences in moral reasoning across languages, yet the source of this variation remains unclear. We test the hypothesis that languages encode aspects of the institutional environments in which they are spoken, allowing LLMs to inherit institution-specific moral priors through training. Across nine languages spanning a broad gradient of institutional quality, six frontier LLMs, and two preregistered studies, we examine moral dilemmas whose acceptability depends on institutional functioning. In Study 1, explicit institutional framing produced uniformly null results: cross-linguistic moral divergence did not increase in institutionally contingent scenarios, nor did it track institutional differences between language communities. In Study 2, we introduced institutionally ambiguous scenarios in which institutional stakes were present but not explicitly stated. Under these conditions, cross-linguistic moral divergence increased relative to institutionally inert controls and, with one theoretically informative exception, was associated with real-world institutional differences between language communities. Explicit framing again attenuated these effects. These findings suggest that institutional experience may leave detectable traces in language that shape LLM moral reasoning, while also indicating that explicit institutional cues can suppress the expression of those differences.

### [49] [EvoGens: A Population-Based Heuristic Search Framework for Scientific Idea Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30961)
*Xu Li,Hanzhe Tu,Xinyi Li,Kuncheng Zhao,Xun Han,Zhonghui Liu*

Main category: cs.CL

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大语言模型在辅助生成研究创意时，往往倾向于语义收敛，导致生成的创意在多样性和新颖性方面表现有限，难以满足科研创新的需求。

Method: 提出了EvoGens框架，将科学创意生成建模为一种群体演化搜索过程。该方法包括：1. 基于排名的变异（Rank-based mutation）并结合差异化检索规划以引入外部知识；2. 语义感知交叉（Semantic-aware crossover）用于融合互补概念；3. 引入轻量级评估信号指导选择过程，旨在平衡探索与开发，防止过早收敛。

Result: 实验表明，EvoGens显著增强了探索能力。与基线方法相比，创意的新颖性（Novelty）从0.1提升至0.4，多样性（Diversity）从0.24提升至0.55，同时保持了与现有技术相当的创意质量。

Conclusion: 进化机制为探索导向的研究创意生成提供了有效的框架，能够显著提升科研创意的多样性和新颖性，同时在当前评估协议下保持创意质量，为克服大语言模型在创意生成中常见的语义收敛问题提供了有力方案。

Abstract: Generating novel research ideas is fundamental to scientific progress. While Large Language Models (LLMs) show promise in assisting this process, existing approaches often exhibit semantic convergence, resulting in limited diversity and novelty. To address this, we introduce EvoGens, an evolution-inspired framework that recasts scientific idea generation as an evolutionary search over a population of ideas. EvoGens iteratively applies rank-based mutation with differentiated retrieval planning to incorporate external knowledge, and semantic-aware crossover to fuse complementary concepts for conceptual reorganization. A lightweight evaluation signal guides the selection process, encouraging sustained exploration while mitigating premature convergence. Extensive experiments demonstrate that EvoGens substantially enhances exploration capabilities compared to state-of-the-art baselines. Specifically, it improves the Novelty from 0.1 to 0.4 and the Diversity from 0.24 to 0.55, while maintaining comparable idea quality under the current automatic evaluation protocol. These findings suggest that evolutionary mechanisms can serve as a useful framework for exploration-oriented research ideation, especially for broadening the novelty and diversity of candidate ideas under a shared automatic evaluation setting.

### [50] [Cognitive Fatigue in Autoregressive Transformers: Formalization and Measurement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30981)
*Riju Marwah,Ritvik Garimella,Vishal Pallagani,Atishay Jain,Michael Stewart,Amit Sheth*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文定义了长文本生成中语言模型的“认知疲劳”现象，并提出了一种轻量级的疲劳指数（FI），可实时监测模型性能退化，为大规模语言模型的生产监控提供了可靠的评估工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自回归语言模型在处理长周期生成任务时常出现重复、指令遵循能力下降及熵不稳定等退化现象，但目前缺乏有效的实时在线诊断工具来捕捉这些生成过程中的性能衰减。

Method: 作者提出了“疲劳指数（Fatigue Index, FI）”，这是一种轻量级且与模型无关的诊断工具。该方法通过量化三个核心指标——对提示词的注意力衰减、表征漂移以及熵失准，并基于单调性、有界性和可解释性公理进行聚合，从而在生成过程中实时监控模型的认知状态。

Result: 在针对9个不同参数规模（1B-13B）模型的测试中，FI在预测任务退化（AUROC=0.95）和文本重复（Spearman相关系数=0.94）方面表现优异。研究还发现模型存在非单调的缩放行为：3B以下的指令微调模型比基础模型退化更快，但在7B以上该趋势发生反转；此外，更长的上下文、中间位置的信息以及降低的数值精度会加速疲劳的发生。

Conclusion: 本文建立了“认知疲劳”作为语言模型生成退化过程的理论框架，证明了疲劳指数（FI）是一个有效的在线监测工具，能够提升生产环境中大语言模型的可靠性与可解释性。

Abstract: Autoregressive language models frequently degrade during long-horizon generation, producing repetitive text, losing instruction adherence, and exhibiting unstable entropy. Despite the prevalence of these failures, practitioners lack online diagnostics to detect them in real-time as they occur. We formalize this degradation as cognitive fatigue, a measurable generation-time state characterized by decay in attention to the original prompt, representational drift, and entropy miscalibration. We introduce the Fatigue Index (FI), a lightweight, model-agnostic diagnostic that aggregates these three signals under explicit axioms (monotonicity, boundedness, interpretability) enabling reliable runtime monitoring. Across nine models (1B-13B parameters), FI trajectories exhibit structured temporal dynamics, predict task degradation (AUROC = 0.95) and repetition (Spearman rho = 0.94), and reveal non-monotonic scaling behavior: instruction-tuned models below 3B exhibit faster collapse than base models, with this trend reversing at 7B. Stress analyses further show that FI onset accelerates under longer contexts, middle-positioned evidence, and reduced numerical precision. These results establish cognitive fatigue as a coherent and measurable phenomenon, and position FI as a principled tool for runtime reliability monitoring in production LLM systems.

### [51] [MoG: Mixture of Experts for Graph-based Retrieval-Augmented Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31010)
*Zheng Yuan,Chuang Zhou,Linhao Luo,Siyu An,Di Yin,Xing Sun,Xiao Huang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: MoG 是一种新型图检索增强生成框架，通过将知识组织为“中心图+专家图”，并利用路由机制动态触发相关领域知识，有效解决了传统 RAG 在复杂推理中因检索冗余导致的性能下降问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的检索增强生成（RAG）方法通常依赖于统一的知识库，这会导致检索到无关信息，进而干扰复杂任务的生成效果。受专家混合（MoE）条件计算机制的启发，作者旨在通过动态、稀疏的检索策略来提高知识检索的准确性和针对性。

Method: 提出了一种名为 MoG 的框架，包含两个核心组件：(1) 中心图（Hub Graphs）：编码语义和结构上通用的核心知识，提供上下文线索；(2) 专家图（Expert Graphs）：包含稀疏激活的特定领域证据。该方法利用拓扑感知路由（Topology-aware router）根据查询动态选择相关的专家图，从而将检索范围限制在核心证据子空间中。

Result: 在多个具有挑战性的基准测试中，MoG 框架表现优于现有的强基准模型，特别是在 MuSiQue 数据集上实现了超过 20% 的相对性能提升。

Conclusion: MoG 框架通过引入图结构化知识组织方式和基于专家混合的动态检索机制，有效解决了传统统一知识库检索引入冗余信息的问题，显著提升了大语言模型在复杂推理任务中的表现。

Abstract: Retrieval-augmented generation is intensively studied to ground large language models on external evidence. However, retrieving from a unified knowledge base could inevitably introduce irrelevant information that may mislead generation for complex reasoning. Inspired by the conditional computation of mixture of experts (MoE), where a router sparsely selects specialized experts alongside shared ones for each input, we propose \textbf{M}ixture \textbf{o}f experts for \textbf{G}raph-based Retrieval-Augmented Generation, i.e., \textbf{MoG}. It organizes knowledge into two core components: (i) diverse, always-accessible hub graphs that encode semantically and structurally central knowledge and provide contextual clues for expert activation, and (ii) sparsely activated expert graphs that contain domain-specific evidence. MoG first accesses hub graphs to identify general evidence and derive contextual clues. Then, a topology-aware router dynamically activates a limited set of expert graphs conditioned on the query, thereby confining retrieval to a focused evidence subspace. Extensive experiments on challenging benchmarks show that MoG consistently outperforms strong baselines, with over 20\% relative improvement on MuSiQue. Our code is available in https://github.com/DEEP-PolyU/MoG.

</details>


### [52] [TRACE: Discovering Task-Specific Parameter via Adaptation-Aware Probing for Continual Fine-Tuning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31025)
*Xiaosong Han,Ke Chen,Xindi Dai,Di Liang,Minlong Peng,Wei Pang,Fausto Giunchiglia,Xiaoyue Feng,Yonghao Liu,Renchu Guan*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: TRACE 是一种高效的大语言模型持续微调方法，通过“适应感知探测”定位并仅更新任务特定的核心参数，既解决了灾难性遗忘问题，又避免了额外存储开销，并支持小模型向大模型的有效迁移。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在大语言模型持续学习过程中，混合任务会导致专业化能力稀释，而顺序微调则会导致灾难性遗忘。现有的重放机制或独立适配器方案会带来额外的计算、存储和管理开销。作者旨在通过发现任务特定的参数子集，在保持任务性能的同时避免遗忘，并减少额外开销。

Method: 提出了一种名为 TRACE 的方法：1. 进行短期的热启动微调以获取任务的适应轨迹；2. 通过重要性评分（L2 范数和 Fisher 信息）和特异性分析（参数更新的余弦相似度）识别任务核心参数；3. 在后续训练中，仅更新当前任务的核心参数，冻结其余参数，从而保护既有知识。

Result: 在多个标准基准测试中，TRACE 表现出优于现有方法的性能；此外，研究还验证了其跨模型和规模的通用性，提出了“小模型导向大模型”的迁移学习范式，降低了大模型微调的资源需求。

Conclusion: TRACE 通过识别并隔离任务特定的核心参数，有效解决了大语言模型持续微调中的灾难性遗忘问题，并展现出良好的跨模型及跨规模迁移能力，为资源受限场景下的模型更新提供了一种高效方案。

Abstract: In real-world deployment, LLMs are often adapted continually across tasks to keep LLMs up-to-date in production, where new fine-tuning should preserve previously learned skills. However, indiscriminately mixing tasks can dilute task specialization, while sequential fine-tuning (full-parameter or low rank adaptation) often causes catastrophic forgetting due to destructive overwriting. Replay-based continual tuning and maintaining separate task-specific adapters can mitigate forgetting, but introduce additional compute, storage, and management overhead. Recognizing the redundancy of LLM parameters for any single task, we reframe continual task adaptation as task-specific parameter discovery via adaptation-aware probing: a short warm-start probe exposes a task's adaptation trace, enabling us to identify and isolate the small subset of parameters essential for each task to mitigate catastrophic forgetting. Building on this view, we introduce TRACE, a novel approach for discovering Task-specific paRameters via Adaptation-aware probing for Continual finE-tuning. We perform a short warm-start fine-tune to derive task-specific core parameters by comparing the warm-started and pre-trained models. Core parameters are identified via two strategies: importance scoring (L$_2$ norm and Fisher Information) and specificity analysis (cosine similarity of parameter updates). In continual fine-tuning settings, only the active task's core parameters are updated while others remain frozen, preserving prior knowledge. We conduct extensive experiments across multiple standard benchmarks to demonstrate the superior performance of our proposed method. Additionally, we validate the generalization of our method through a cross-model and scale transferability study, demonstrating a "small-to-large" paradigm that guides the fine-tuning of large-scale models under resource constraints.

</details>


### [53] [How Much Do LLMs Know About Chinese Zero Pronouns?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31056)
*Yifei Li,Guanyi Chen,Tingting He*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 零代词在中文等“代词脱落（pro-drop）”语言中普遍存在，且一直是自然语言处理领域的难点。尽管大语言模型技术迅猛发展，但目前对于它们在处理零代词这一特定语言现象上的能力缺乏系统性研究与认知。

Conclusion: 尽管大型语言模型（LLMs）在多种语言任务中表现出色，但在处理零代词（ZP）这一语言现象时仍存在显著局限。研究表明，无论是上游的识别与指称性分类，还是下游的消解与翻译任务，当前大模型均面临较大困难，尚未达到令人满意的性能水平。

Although Large Language Models (LLMs) perform well on many Chinese language tasks, their ability to process ZPs remains poorly understood. We conduct a systematic investigation of LLMs' handling of Chinese ZPs through a sequence of linguistically motivated tasks, including identification, referentiality classification, referential type classification, resolution, and translation. A diverse set of LLMs is evaluated across all tasks. Our results show that Chinese ZPs remain highly challenging for current LLMs, particularly for upstream tasks such as identification and referentiality classification. Performance on downstream tasks, such as ZP translation, is also consistently low: even state-of-the-art reasoning-oriented LLMs correctly translate fewer than half of Chinese ZPs into English.

*Jiasheng Zheng,Boxi Cao,Boxi Yu,Yuzhong Zhang,Jialun Cao,Yaojie Lu,Hongyu Lin,Xianpei Han,Le Sun*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对强化学习训练大模型时缺乏高质量可验证代码数据的问题，本文提出了“原子分解与重组”（ADR）框架，通过生成极具挑战性和新颖性的代码任务，有效提升了模型在多种代码相关领域的能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前的强化学习可验证奖励（RLVR）方法受限于高质量、有挑战性的可验证代码任务的匮乏，现有基于启发式的种子数据扩展方法难以生成足够新颖且困难的数据，导致训练收益随数据规模增长的边际效应递减。

Method: 提出了一种名为“原子分解与重组”（Atomic Decomposition and Recombination, ADR）的框架。该方法通过将代码任务分解为原子级元素，再根据预设控制进行重组，从而自动化生成具有高新颖性和高难度的可验证代码训练数据。

Result: 实验表明，与现有基准方法相比，ADR在数据的新颖性、难度、多样性和测试质量上表现更优；在算法编程、工具使用和数据科学等多个下游领域中，使用ADR合成的数据能更显著地提升大模型的代码能力。

Conclusion: ADR框架为可验证代码任务的合成提供了一种新范式，能够生成高质量、高难度且新颖的数据，从而有效突破了RLVR在数据规模和模型能力提升上的瓶颈，证明了该方法在提升大语言模型代码生成能力方面的有效性。

Abstract: Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) has recently emerged as the cornerstone for shaping the remarkable coding abilities of Large Language Models (LLMs). However, the scalability of RLVR is severely constrained by the scarcity of sufficiently challenging verifiable code tasks that target near the model's edge of competence. Prior studies often rely on heuristic seed expansions for data synthesis, which severely limits both novelty and difficulty. Consequently, the training value of such data fails to scale proportionally with the size of its synthesis. To this end, we propose Atomic Decomposition and Recombination (ADR), a novel framework that generates verifiable code tasks via decomposition into atomic elements and controlled recombination, thereby enabling the generation of genuinely novel and challenging verifiable code tasks. Experiments and analysis demonstrate that ADR achieves superior originality, difficulty, diversity, and test quality over existing baselines, and consistently delivers greater improvements in code ability across RLVR in diverse downstream domains, including algorithmic programming, tool usage, and data science. Our work sheds light on a new paradigm for novel code task synthesis and scalable RLVR training.

### [55] [AdaptR1: Reinforcement Learning Based Adaptive Interleaved Thinking in Multi-hop Question Answering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31062)
*Yuxin Wang,Jiahao Lu,Qifeng Wu,Shicheng Fang,Chuanyuan Tan,Yining Zheng,Xuanjing Huang,Xipeng Qiu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对大模型推理中存在的“过度思考”浪费，本文提出了 AdaptR1，通过强化学习动态分配每一步的推理预算，在大幅降低推理成本的同时保证了任务准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的链式思考（CoT）推理方法往往导致“过度思考”，即在简单查询或非必要阶段生成冗长的推理过程，造成推理成本浪费。目前的自适应方法大多只在查询级别做决策，忽略了多步推理任务中各阶段对推理需求的不同。

Method: 提出 AdaptR1 框架，这是一种完全基于强化学习（RL）的自适应交错思维方法。它摒弃了传统的监督微调（SFT）初始化，引入了“质量门控效率奖励（quality-gated efficiency reward）”机制，使模型能够在多跳问答的每一个推理步骤中动态决定是否进行显式思考。

Result: 在 Graph-R1 设置下，AdaptR1 将平均思维标记（think tokens）减少了 69.71%，在 HotpotQA 数据集上更是减少了 90.35%，同时保持了与基准模型相当或更优的性能。此外，分析表明该方法通过精准识别规划阶段的需求，显著提升了推理效率。

Conclusion: AdaptR1 证明了在多跳问答任务中，通过基于强化学习的步进式自适应思维分配，可以在大幅减少推理成本（思维标记）的同时，保持甚至超越传统模型的性能。研究发现“过度思考”主要集中在规划阶段，该方法有效地实现了计算资源的最优化分配。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) have achieved remarkable performance in complex reasoning tasks through Chain-of-Thought (CoT) prompting. However, this approach often leads to ``over-thinking,'' where models generate unnecessarily long reasoning traces for simple queries and incur avoidable inference cost. While recent work has explored adaptive reasoning, existing methods typically make a single query-level decision about whether to reason. This overlooks the dynamic nature of multi-step tasks, where the need for explicit reasoning varies across intermediate stages. To address this limitation, we introduce AdaptR1, a Reinforcement Learning (RL) based framework for adaptive interleaved thinking in multi-hop Question Answering (QA). Unlike previous approaches that require Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) for cold-start initialization, AdaptR1 uses a fully RL-based strategy with a quality-gated efficiency reward to dynamically allocate reasoning budgets at each step. Under the Graph-R1 setting, AdaptR1 reduces average think tokens by 69.71\%, with a 90.35\% reduction on HotpotQA, while maintaining performance comparable to or better than standard baselines. Furthermore, our analysis reveals that overthinking in multi-hop reasoning is not uniformly distributed but occurs predominantly during the initial planning stages, highlighting the effectiveness of step-wise adaptive budget allocation.

</details>


### [56] [ConsisGuard: Aligning Safety Deliberation with Policy Enforcement in LLM Guardrails](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31073)
*Yan Wang,Zhixuan Chu,Zihao Xue,Zhen Bi,Bingyu Zhu,YueFeng Chen,Zeyu Yang,Jungang Lou,Longtao Huang,Ningyu Zhang,Kui Ren,Hui Xue*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文针对LLM安全护栏中推理与决策不一致的问题，提出了ConsisGuard框架，通过轨迹蒸馏与功能耦合对齐技术，确保了安全推理的忠实执行，提升了护栏的可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于推理的LLM安全护栏存在“审议-执行鸿沟”（deliberation-to-enforcement gap）问题，即模型虽能识别有害意图但决策不一致，或决策缺乏政策依据。现有的思维链方法未能保证推理与安全决策的忠实性。

Method: 提出了ConsisGuard框架，该框架包含两个核心环节：1. 策略到决策轨迹蒸馏（Policy-to-Decision Trajectory Distillation），旨在强化推理路径与安全策略的对齐；2. 功能耦合对齐（Functional Coupling Alignment），通过优化内部机制，确保最终决策由推理过程严格导出。

Result: 在有害提示词与响应检测基准测试中，ConsisGuard有效提升了检测准确率，并显著降低了策略执行失败的情况，验证了该框架在提升护栏可靠性方面的有效性。

Conclusion: 为了构建可靠的基于推理的大语言模型（LLM）护栏，仅有推理是不够的，必须确保推理过程与最终决策之间存在严格的逻辑一致性。通过政策执行一致性来弥合“审议-执行鸿沟”，是提升AI安全防护能力的关键。

Abstract: Reasoning-based LLM guardrails improve safety moderation by generating explicit rationales before issuing final decisions. However, their rationales do not always lead to faithful enforcement: a model may recognize a harmful intent in its reasoning but still predict a safe label, or issue an unsafe decision without policy-grounded justification. We identify this safety-critical failure mode as the deliberation-to-enforcement gap. Unlike general chain-of-thought faithfulness, guardrail reliability requires policy execution consistency: the generated reasoning should be grounded in the safety policy, and the final decision should be entailed by that reasoning. We propose ConsisGuard, a consistency-aware framework for reasoning-based LLM guardrails. ConsisGuard performs Policy-to-Decision Trajectory Distillation and Functional Coupling Alignment, aligning the internal coupling between safety deliberation and decision enforcement. Experiments on prompt and response harmfulness detection benchmarks show that ConsisGuard improves detection performance while reducing policy execution failures. These results suggest that reliable reasoning-based guardrails require accurate faithful execution of safety policies.

*Dominik Soós,Meng Jiang,Jian Wu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为KnowledgeGain的新指标，旨在通过量化读者的知识获取量来评估科学新闻质量，并利用校准后的LLM模拟器筛选出更具教育价值的科普内容。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的科学新闻生成与摘要评价指标主要关注语义相似性和事实一致性，缺乏对“读者通过阅读获取了多少新知识”这一核心教育目标的衡量，导致科普内容难以有效达成知识传播的效果。

Method: 1. 提出KnowledgeGain指标：通过评估读者阅读前后知识的变化来衡量科学新闻质量；2. 开展对照人类研究：验证指标与人类阅读知识获取差异的相关性；3. 构建LLM阅读器模拟器：利用人类实验数据校准大语言模型，使其模拟人类阅读行为；4. 评估流程：使用模拟器对生成的候选新闻进行排序与过滤，并经由后续人类测试验证其效果。

Abstract: Science news is an important medium to communicate discoveries between the research communities and the public. Yet, most metrics for generated or summarized text evaluate semantic similarity and factual consistency, but do not measure how much knowledge readers learn from the news. We introduce KnowledgeGain, a metric that evaluates the quality of science news by measuring how much knowledge readers gained after reading it. To evaluate the metric, we first performed a controlled human study and showed that the metric successfully captures the differential knowledge gained by human readers reading different types of science media. The data allowed us to calibrate a prompt-only LLM reader simulator. We use it to rank and filter candidate articles before human evaluation. A second human study shows that articles selected with this simulator improve post-reading accuracy and normalized KnowledgeGain over a strong generation baseline. Our work is a step toward generating science news that better meets the knowledge and comprehension goals of Bloom's Taxonomy.

### [58] [GRKV: Global Regression for Training-Free KV Cache Compression in Long-Context LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31105)
*Junjie Peng,You Wu,Haoyi Wu,Jialong Han,Xiaohua Xie,Kewei Tu,Jianhuang Lai*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对长文本 LLM 的 KV 缓存内存瓶颈，本文提出了 GRKV 方法，通过岭回归优化信息合并过程，有效缓解了传统方法中存在的不平衡合并问题，实现了在保持性能的同时高效压缩缓存。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于跨度的 KV 缓存压缩方法在处理合并时会产生极度不平衡的模式，导致边缘标记过载及信息丢失。作者旨在通过更均衡的合并策略来缓解这一问题，从而在受限缓存预算下更好地保持语义连贯性。

Method: 提出了 GRKV（全局回归 KV 缓存）方法。该方法直接最小化压缩缓存与完整缓存注意力输出之间的差异，利用基于岭回归（Ridge Regression）的合并步骤将已丢弃标记的信息分布到保留的标记中，并引入正则化机制以防止过度平滑。

Result: 在 LongBench 和 RULER 等长上下文基准测试中，GRKV 是唯一能够在维持极低额外开销的同时，显著提高模型整体性能的 KV 缓存合并方法。

Conclusion: GRKV 是一种无需训练的高效 KV 缓存压缩方法，它通过岭回归技术优化信息分布，解决了传统基于跨度保留与合并方法中由于合并偏差导致的信息丢失问题，在长上下文任务中表现出优异的性能提升。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) with extended context lengths rely on the key-value (KV) cache to support attention over prior tokens. However, maintaining the KV cache incurs substantial memory overhead, motivating KV-cache compression methods that enforce a fixed budget through eviction and merging. Modern eviction methods increasingly adopt span-based retention because preserving contiguous spans is empirically effective and better preserves semantic coherence. Yet, when combined with post-eviction merging, span-based retention concentrates merges onto a small set of span-boundary carrier tokens, producing a highly imbalanced merge pattern that exacerbates over-merging and increases information loss. To address this imbalance, we propose GRKV (Global Regression for KV Cache), a training-free KV-cache merging method that directly minimizes the discrepancy between compressed-cache and full-cache attention outputs. GRKV uses ridge-regression-based merge steps to distribute information from evicted tokens across retained tokens, while regularizing the updates to prevent over-smoothing. Across the LongBench and RULER long-context benchmarks, GRKV is the only merging method that improves overall performance with minimal overhead.

</details>


### [59] [Multilingual and Cross-Lingual Citation Needed Detection on Wikipedia for Lower-Resource Languages](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31136)
*Gerrit Quaremba,Amy Rechkemmer,Elizabeth Black,Denny Vrandečić,Elena Simperl*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1. 构建了包含18种语言、涵盖三种不同资源水平的“多语言CND语料库”（MCN）。2. 评估了多种小型解码器型语言模型（SLM）在CND任务上的表现。3. 采用了编码器风格（encoder-style）的训练目标对SLM进行微调。4. 进行了跨语言实验，测试仅在英语数据上微调的模型对其他语言的迁移能力。

Conclusion: 对于维基百科的“引用需求检测”（CND）任务而言，经过微调的小型模型（SLM）在性能和资源利用率上均优于大型语言模型（LLM）。SLM不仅在多语言环境下表现出色，且展现了强大的跨语言迁移能力，即使在几乎没有目标语言数据的情况下，也能通过英语训练数据实现高效的跨语言检测，为低资源语言社区提供了更可行、高效的解决方案。

Abstract: In automated fact-checking (AFC), check-worthiness detection identifies claims requiring verification based on domain-specific criteria. On Wikipedia, this task instantiates as Citation Needed Detection (CND), which flags claims lacking supporting citations. However, existing research has largely overlooked lower-resource languages, and recent AFC pipelines rely on large language models (LLMs), which are inaccessible to low-resource organizations. We introduce MCN, a multilingual CND corpus spanning 18 languages across three resource levels, on which we conduct an extensive study of small decoder-based language models (SLMs). Our experiments show that SLMs fine-tuned with an encoder-style objective substantially outperform prompted LLMs across languages. We further present one of the first studies on cross-lingual CND, demonstrating that SLMs fine-tuned solely on English claims surpass LLMs, even with little to no target-language adaptation. Our findings have important implications for lower-resource Wikipedia communities and suggest that compact, task-specific models are preferable to LLMs for CND. We release all data and code at https://github.com/gerritq/mcn

### [60] [On the Robustness of Multilingual Text Embedding Rankings Across Learning Tasks, Languages, and Benchmark Datasets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31142)
*Ana Gjorgjevikj,Barbara Koroušić Seljak,Tome Eftimov*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了多语言文本嵌入模型在MTEB等基准测试中的排名极易受评估设计影响，并提出了评估模型性能稳健性的新指标，发现仅有少数模型具备真正的跨任务高性能表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的多语言嵌入模型基准测试（如MTEB）在评估模型性能时，往往受到数据集构成选择和性能聚合方法等隐含偏好的影响，导致结论缺乏稳健性。因此，需要系统性地研究这些因素如何影响多语言模型排名的稳定性。

Method: 本文采用元分析（meta-study）方法，应用多种多准则决策分析（MCDA）排名方案，并引入了“数据集构成稳健性”和“排名方案稳健性”两个关键指标。研究涵盖了5种主要语言的9项任务，并扩展至约230种语言，旨在量化评估结果对评估设计变化的敏感度。

Result: 研究表明，基于LLM的大规模模型在多数任务中表现出较强的稳健性，但在特定任务（如检索）中表现存在差异。分析证实，大多数模型的性能排名对评估设计（数据集选择及聚合方式）高度敏感，只有极少数模型展现了跨任务和跨评估方案的综合稳健性。

Conclusion: 多语言文本嵌入模型的性能表现高度依赖于评估方案和数据集构成。通过引入稳健性指标，研究发现仅有少数模型能在多种任务、排名方案和数据集子集下保持始终如一的高性能，强调了在评估中进行多维度敏感性分析的必要性。

Abstract: Large-scale multilingual text embedding models play crucial role in both research and industry, yet their behavior in language-specific, multi-task settings remains insufficiently understood. Although benchmarking platforms such as MTEB report results across more than 250 languages, conclusions about model superiority often depend on implicit choices of dataset compositions and performance aggregation methods. To address this gap, we present a meta-study of multilingual model performance robustness in MTEB, applying a diverse set of multi-criteria decision-making ranking schemes and introducing two robustness indicators: dataset-composition robustness (sensitivity of rankings to changing dataset compositions) and ranking-scheme robustness (sensitivity to aggregation method change). They enable systematic sensitivity analysis of whether benchmarking conclusions remain stable under different evaluation designs. We conduct an in-depth analysis on five languages (English, French, German, Hindi, and Spanish) across nine tasks (e.g., classification, clustering, retrieval) and release results for approximately 230 additional languages. The task-specific analyses show that large-scale LLM-based models are often robust top performers, though not uniformly (e.g., in retrieval task), while task-agnostic results reveal that only a small subset of models remains consistently strong across tasks, ranking schemes, and data subsamples.

### [61] [Towards Efficient LLMs Annealing with Principled Sample Selection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31175)
*Yuanjian Xu,Jianing Hao,Wanbo Zhang,Zhong Li,Guang Zhang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种名为DiReCT的数据选择框架，通过分析损失曲面的谱几何特性，对退火阶段的样本梯度施加方向约束，从而优化模型在大语言模型预训练最后阶段的收敛性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型预训练中的退火阶段对模型质量至关重要，但现有的数据选择策略多依赖经验启发式规则（如领域过滤），缺乏优化理论的指导。作者旨在从损失曲面谱几何的角度出发，解决退火阶段数据选择缺乏原则性基础的问题。

Method: 提出了一种名为DiReCT（方向约束受限训练）的新框架。该方法将样本选择转化为一个约束优化问题，利用Hessian矩阵的谱特性（即损失曲面的几何特征）对每个样本的梯度施加显式方向约束，从而筛选出符合最优曲率感知下降路径的训练数据。

Result: 实验结果表明，DiReCT框架在多种模型规模下均能持续取得最优性能，有效提升了退火阶段的收敛质量，验证了通过方向受限优化提升模型训练效率的有效性。

Conclusion: 本研究成功利用损失曲面谱几何特性指导大语言模型退火阶段的数据选择，证明了基于方向约束的梯度优化方法能显著提升模型最终性能，为退火阶段的训练策略提供了理论支撑与有效工具。

Abstract: The annealing phase is a pivotal convergence stage in LLM pre-training that ultimately determines final model quality. However, effectively selecting training data during this phase remains a key challenge. Current strategies rely on empirical heuristics, such as domain filtering or context extension, which lack a principled grounding in optimization theory. In this work, we characterize the annealing phase through the lens of the loss landscape's spectral geometry. We argue that optimal convergence requires gradient updates to satisfy heterogeneous constraints across different eigen-directions. Building on this insight, we formulate data selection as a problem of satisfying these directional constraints. To this end, we propose DiReCT (Directionally-Restrained Constrained Training), a novel framework that reformulates sample selection in the annealing stage as a constrained optimization problem. By imposing explicit directional constraints on per-sample gradients based on the spectral properties of the Hessian, DiReCT identifies samples that align with the optimal curvature-aware descent path. Extensive experiments across various model scales demonstrate that DiReCT consistently achieves state-of-the-art performance. For future research, code is available at https://github.com/xuyj233/Direct.

</details>


### [62] [Steering LLMs? Actually, Sparse Autoencoders can outperform simple baselines](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31183)
*Mikkel Godsk Jørgensen,Lars Kai Hansen*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对近期研究（Wu et al., 2025）指出 SAE 在模型操控基准 AxBench 上表现不佳的问题，作者旨在重新评估 SAE 的潜力，并反驳其在可解释性操控任务中表现逊色的观点。

Result: 实验结果显示，通过所提出的方法，SAE 在 AxBench 上的表现接近 LoRA 基准；同时证实了即使仅利用可解释性组件，所选特征也具有显著的因果效能；此外，发现高稀疏性并不是实现有效操控的必要条件。

Conclusion: 研究表明，稀疏自动编码器（SAE）在模型操控方面被低估了。通过受监督的特征选择与标记流程，SAE 的性能可媲美 LoRA 基准。此外，研究发现高稀疏性对于基于可解释性的操控并非必要，这挑战了此前的相关研究结论。

Abstract: Sparse Autoencoders (SAEs) have been seen as a promising avenue for exploring the internals of Large Language Models (LLMs) and for steering model output generation. When AxBench - a model steering benchmark - was introduced in Wu et al. (2025), SAEs did not seem to live up to their original hype due to poor steering performance relative to a set of simple baselines. This work serves as a partial rebuttal for Sparse Autoencoders and suggests that the results of Wu et al. (2025) did not do them full justice. We find that Sparse Autoencoders can, in fact, perform close to on par with the reference LoRA performance on the AxBench benchmark, when features are selected and labelled with our supervised pipeline. We also find that our pipeline selects features that are surprisingly causal of their identified labels when using only its interpretability-based components. Lastly, we present evidence that high sparsity (low l0) may not be crucial for successful steering based on interpretability, which is in contrast to the earlier findings in Wang et al. (2025).

### [63] [Learning Whom to Trust: Market-Feedback Adaptive Retrieval for Frozen LLMs in Event-Driven Financial RAG](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31201)
*Zijie Zhao,Roy E. Welsch*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种用于金融预测的 RAG 新框架，通过引入可随市场反馈更新的“贝叶斯源记忆”来优化检索源选择，显著提升了金融预测的准确性和投资组合表现，证明了优化检索机制比单纯微调阅读模型更为有效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的金融 RAG 系统仅依赖文本相关性进行证据排序，忽略了金融市场中证据的有效性高度依赖于事件类型、预测时间跨度和市场上下文的事实，导致其在处理复杂金融预测任务时表现受限。

Method: 提出了一个“带源记忆的冻结阅读器”（Frozen Reader with Source Memory）架构。该方法保持大语言模型（LLM）阅读器不动，通过一个外部贝叶斯源记忆（Bayesian Source Memory）层来适配检索过程，并利用已实现的剩余收益（residual-return）反馈实时更新记忆，以适应不同的事件类型、预测期限和市场环境。

Conclusion: 在金融 RAG 系统中，优化检索源的选择（即学习“从哪里检索”）与提升模型的阅读能力同样重要。通过构建外部贝叶斯源记忆模块，系统能够实现模块化、高效的市场反馈自适应，优于单纯依赖微调阅读器（如 LoRA）的方案。

Abstract: Financial retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) systems typically rank evidence by textual relevance, but in financial markets the useful evidence source depends on event type, forecast horizon, and market context. We study news-triggered event-impact prediction as a point-in-time financial RAG problem. For each company-news anchor, the system retrieves related financial news and SEC filing passages, appends a pre-decision market-context card, and predicts multi-horizon residual-return signals. Our method keeps the large language model (LLM) reader frozen and adapts the retrieval layer through an external Bayesian source memory updated from matured residual-return feedback. On a fixed 89-stock Nasdaq-oriented universe derived from the FinRL-DeepSeek/FNSPID task, using original FNSPID news and point-in-time EDGAR filing passages, Frozen Reader with Source Memory improves held-out macro-F1 from 0.438 to 0.471 and downstream portfolio Sharpe from 0.52 to 0.84 relative to Frozen Reader with No Memory. A supervised LoRA reader improves static RAG modestly, but does not improve over the frozen source-memory reader. These results suggest that, for financial RAG, learning where to retrieve from can be as important as learning how to read, offering a simple, modular route to market-feedback adaptation.

### [64] [Shared Doubt: Zero-shot Cross-Lingual Confidence Estimation for Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31220)
*Athina Kyriakou,Dennis Ulmer,Ivan Titov*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文研究发现大语言模型中存在跨语言共享的置信度特征，通过训练简单的线性探针，即可在无需多语言监督的情况下实现高效的零样本跨语言置信度估计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的置信度估计（CE）研究主要集中在英语领域，忽略了多语言场景；此外，许多现有的CE方法在不同语言间表现下降，或需要针对特定语言进行繁重的重新训练。作者旨在探究多语言大语言模型是否编码了通用的、可跨语言迁移的置信度特征。

Method: 研究人员使用了一种轻量级的线性探针（Linear Probe），该探针直接基于大模型中间层的表征来预测答案的正确性。通过单语言训练，观察探针在未见过的、语系多样的语言上的零样本（zero-shot）泛化表现，并通过分析层权重和消融实验来定位置信度特征。

Result: 实验表明，置信度特征在不同语言的模型中间层中高度集中，暗示了共享置信度子空间的存在。该探针在零样本跨语言设置下表现优异，无需重新训练即可达到较强的基准性能，且优于其他主流的置信度估计方法。

Conclusion: 本研究证实了多语言大语言模型中存在跨语言共享的置信度特征子空间，并表明通过轻量级线性探针可以在无需目标语言监督的情况下，实现高效、泛化能力强的跨语言置信度估计。

Abstract: Confidence estimation (CE), i.e. quantifying the reliability of a model's prediction, has attracted great interest in the context of large language models (LLMs). However, most studies focus on English, ignoring the multilingual reality of LLM usage, while many CE methods degrade or require retraining across languages. To address this gap, we investigate whether multilingual LLMs encode shared, language-transferable confidence features. We use a lightweight linear probe that predicts answer correctness directly from intermediate representations. Trained monolingually, the probe generalizes zero-shot to unseen, typologically diverse languages without target-language supervision. Learned layer weights and multiple ablations reveal that confidence features concentrate in middle layers across languages, suggesting a shared confidence subspace. While zero-shot cross-lingual performance depends on similarity to the source language, the probe provides a strong baseline without any retraining and compares favorably to other popular confidence estimation methods.

### [65] [Scaling Multi-Hop Training Data via Graph-Constrained Path Selection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31238)
*Pengyu Chen,Yonggang Zhang,Mingming Chen,Jun Song,Wei Xue,Yike Guo*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对专业文档推理数据稀缺的问题，本文提出了一种基于图约束的离线路径挖掘与在线口语化转换方法，通过扩大高质量训练数据规模，显著提升了大模型在复杂文档环境下的多跳推理性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有从非结构化文本中构建多跳推理数据的方法在处理重复模板多、交叉引用密集的专业文档时表现不佳，难以在海量专业语料上进行有效扩展。

Method: 提出了一种解耦的训练数据构建方法：首先利用基于上下文关键词中心点的图枚举方法离线挖掘推理路径，并应用几何容许约束（Gram矩阵论证）过滤无效路径；随后仅调用教师模型对验证后的路径进行问答对的口语化转换。

Result: 在CUAD法律合同语料库上，通过构建8万个样本对Qwen3-32B进行微调，将闭卷Token F1分数从21.66%提升至38.58%；验证了该方法将可用语料库规模扩大了4.4倍，显著提升了模型的合成与推理能力。

Conclusion: 本研究证明了通过离线图约束路径挖掘可以显著扩大训练数据规模，从而有效提升大语言模型处理复杂、结构化专业文档的推理能力。研究还指出，在该任务中，规模效应（数据量的增加）比单条路径的质量优化更为关键。

Abstract: Endowing large language models with compositional reasoning over specialized documents requires multi-hop training data at scale, where such data rarely exists outside of curated benchmarks built on structured sources. To construct it directly from plain, unannotated text, existing methods ask a single teacher model to jointly discover an evidence path through a document and verbalize it as a question-answer pair. However, these methods degrade sharply when documents are structured around repetitive templates and densely cross-referencing clauses, conditions that characterize most real-world specialized corpora. In this work, we decouple the two operations: reasoning paths are enumerated offline over a graph of contextual keyword centroids, and the teacher is invoked only to verbalize pre-validated paths. The graph enforces five geometric admissibility constraints, for which we provide Gram-matrix arguments establishing that local similarity bounds alone admit endpoint drift up to ${\sim}91^{\circ}$, and that an upper similarity bound is necessary to exit dense embedding cliques formed by boilerplate text. A matched-size ablation isolates the mechanism: at equal training scale, constrained and unconstrained chains yield indistinguishable downstream performance, and the gain at full scale comes from a 4.4$\times$ expansion of the usable corpus rather than from higher per-chain quality -- reframing the role of graph constraints, in this setting, as raising teacher synthesizability rather than improving chain content. Fine-tuning Qwen3-32B on 80K examples constructed from the CUAD legal contract corpus improves closed-book Token F1 from 21.66% to 38.58%. We have released our codes at https://github.com/hkgai-official/GCSCS.

</details>


### [66] [Mellum2 Technical Report](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31268)
*Marko Kojic,Ivan Bondyrev,Aral de Moor,Joseph Shtok,Petr Borovlev,Kseniia Lysaniuk,Madeeswaran Kannan,Ivan Dolgov,Nikita Pavlichenko*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: Mellum 2 是一款高效的 12B 参数 MoE 模型，专为软件工程优化。它通过多令牌预测和滑动窗口注意力技术，在保持高性能的同时实现了极高的推理效率，并开源了基础版、指令版和思考模型供社区使用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在解决现有 4B 稠密模型在复杂编程任务和长文本推理中的局限性，开发一款既具备卓越软件工程能力（如代码生成、调试、Agentic 编程），又能通过 MoE 架构在消费级 GPU 上保持高推理效率的通用大语言模型。

Method: 采用 12B 参数的混合专家 (MoE) 架构（64 个专家，激活 8 个），集成组查询注意力 (GQA)、滑动窗口注意力及多令牌预测 (MTP) 头；采用三阶段训练课程，结合 Muon 优化器与 FP8 混合精度，并使用 YaRN 进行 128K 上下文扩展，最终经过监督微调 (SFT) 和强化学习验证 (RLVR) 后训练。

Result: Mellum 2 在代码生成、数学推理、工具调用及知识基准测试中表现优异，性能可与 4B-14B 参数范围内的开源模型相媲美，且单令牌计算量仅相当于 2.5B 稠密模型。

Conclusion: Mellum 2 通过创新的 MoE 架构、多令牌预测技术以及高效的训练课程，证明了在有限的推理资源下，通过专门的模型设计能够实现高性能的代码工程与推理能力，为开源大语言模型提供了一个高效、可扩展的参考范例。

Abstract: We present Mellum 2, an open-weight 12B-parameter Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) language model with 2.5B active parameters per token. Mellum 2 is a general-purpose language model specialized in software engineering, spanning code generation and editing, debugging, multi-step reasoning, tool use and function calling, agentic coding, and conversational programming assistance, and it is the successor to the completion-focused 4B dense Mellum model. The architecture builds on the Mixture-of-Experts (64 experts, 8 active) and combines Grouped-Query Attention with 4 KV heads, Sliding Window Attention on three of every four layers, and a single Multi-Token Prediction head that doubles as both an auxiliary pre-training objective and a built-in draft model for speculative decoding; each choice was validated by ablation with inference efficiency on commodity GPUs as a design constraint. Pre-training spans approximately 10.6 trillion tokens through a three-phase curriculum that progressively shifts the mixture from diverse web data toward curated code and mathematical content, optimized with Muon under FP8 hybrid precision and a Warmup-Hold-Decay schedule with linear decay to zero. The pre-trained base is extended to a 128K context window via a layer-selective YaRN and then post-trained in two stages (supervised fine-tuning followed by RLVR), yielding two released variants: an Instruct model that answers directly and a Thinking model that emits an explicit reasoning trace before its final answer. Across code generation, math and reasoning, tool use, knowledge, and safety benchmarks, Mellum 2 is competitive with open-weight baselines in the 4B-14B range while running at the per-token compute of a 2.5B dense model. We release the base, instruct, and thinking checkpoints, together with this report on the architecture decisions, data pipeline, and training recipe behind them, under the Apache 2.0 license.

</details>


### [67] [Wind Turbine Maintenance Log Labelling Framework: LLM-Driven Data Correction and Enrichment via Semantic Extraction of Reliability Intelligence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31281)
*Max Malyi,Jonathan Shek,Alasdair McDonald,Andre Biscaya*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究开发了一种利用大语言模型处理风机维护日志的方法，成功将非结构化的文本转变为结构化的可靠性数据，提升了故障分析效率，并为预测性维护奠定了数据基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 风机维护日志中包含大量非结构化的自然语言描述，难以进行量化分析，阻碍了对风机老化过程、运维优化及降低能源平准化成本（LCOE）的深度研究。亟需一种有效手段将这些定性观察转化为量化可靠性指标。

Method: 提出了一种模型无关的自动化框架，利用大语言模型（LLM）处理风机维护日志。该方法对自由文本描述进行标准化和结构化处理，通过系统化的批次处理构建经验性词典，自动修正系统代码并提取维护行动与故障模式的分类法（Taxonomies）。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了利用大语言模型将非结构化的风机维护日志转化为结构化数据的可行性与高效性，为风能行业实现大规模、自动化的可靠性工程和故障模式分析（FMEA）提供了一个可扩展的框架，有助于优化风机运维策略并降低能源平准化成本。

Abstract: As wind turbine fleets age, data-driven reliability engineering is essential to optimise their operation and maintenance for service life extension and levelised cost of energy reduction. Failure event descriptions within historical maintenance logs are a source of valuable reliability intelligence. However, they typically appear as unstructured natural language entries, rendering them inaccessible for quantitative analysis. This paper presents a novel methodology leveraging a large language model (LLM) to systematically standardise and structure maintenance logs based on their free-text descriptors. Operating on a dataset of 16,316 maintenance logs from 280 turbines monitored over nine years, the developed model-agnostic framework autonomously corrected hierarchical system codes and extracted evidence-based taxonomies of maintenance actions and failure modes. The automated pipeline successfully structured over 70% of the dataset. It resolved pervasive misclassification issues, such as isolating previously unclassified pitch system faults and restoring missing system codes, and enriched the records by applying empirical taxonomies to label specific actions taken and failure modes addressed. By using system-based log batches to construct empirical dictionaries of failure modes, observable symptoms, dominant mechanisms, and candidate causes, this approach reduces the inherent subjectivity of manual failure modes and effects analysis (FMEA). Ultimately, the methodology provides a highly scalable, cost-effective blueprint for translating large sets of qualitative field observations into quantitative reliability metrics, laying the foundation for integrated root-cause analysis across the renewable energy sector, improved FMEA, and advanced predictive maintenance.

### [68] [Divergence Decoding: Inference-Time Unlearning via Auxiliary Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31293)
*Humzah Merchant,Bradford Levy*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对大语言模型存在的隐私记忆风险，本文提出了一种名为“发散解码（DD）”的新型遗忘方法。它通过小型辅助模型引导推理过程，有效移除了敏感信息，且在不损害模型效能的前提下表现优于现有方案，并具备跨模态泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型常会记忆敏感的训练数据，引发隐私和版权风险。现有的模型“遗忘”方法往往会导致模型效能严重下降，或者难以有效移除复杂查询中的敏感知识，亟需一种既能保护隐私又不损害模型性能的有效手段。

Method: 提出了一种称为发散解码（Divergence Decoding, DD）的机制。该方法通过训练小型辅助模型来引导大语言模型的输出逻辑值（logits），使其在推理过程中避开特定的敏感知识。此外，研究还展示了如何将这种受控分布通过知识蒸馏的方式重新集成回原模型。

Result: 实验表明，在多种模型规模和训练数据集上，DD方法的遗忘效果显著优于现有的前沿（SOTA）基准方法。该方法不仅在文本生成任务中表现优异，还成功验证了在图像生成等其他概率模型领域的通用性和有效性。

Conclusion: 发散解码（Divergence Decoding, DD）是一种高效且经济的机器遗忘方案。通过利用辅助模型在推理阶段引导模型偏离敏感数据，该方法不仅避免了传统重训练带来的效能损失，还能通过知识蒸馏将其能力固化到基座模型中，且具有跨模态（如图像领域）的泛化潜力。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) frequently memorize sensitive training data thereby creating significant privacy and copyright risks. Addressing these risks, i.e., removing such knowledge from an existing model checkpoint, has proven challenging as many unlearning methods lead to catastrophic utility loss or are ineffective for complex queries. We introduce Divergence Decoding (DD), a mechanism that uses small auxiliary models to steer the logits of the LLM away from specific data during inference. Training these models is straight forward, i.e., we use standard pre-training and fine-tuning setups. We find the method decisively outperforms state-of-the-art (SOTA) baselines on unlearning benchmarks across a variety of model and training dataset scales consistent with DD being an effective and inexpensive solution to unlearning. We then demonstrate that this steered distribution can be trivially distilled back into the base model. Since the method is generally applicable to any probabilistic model, we explore its efficacy outside of text generation and find evidence of generalization to the domain of images.

### [69] [Reinforcement Learning Amplifies Emergent Misalignment from Harmless Rewards](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31328)
*Magnus Jørgenvåg,David Kaczér,Lasse Ruttert,Marvin Gülhan,Lucie Flek,Florian Mai*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 研究发现，在小型开源模型中，强化学习（RL）比监督微调（SFT）更容易诱导涌现性不对齐（EM），且即便是细微的奖励偏差也可能导致模型行为广泛失控，但通过特定的在线策略安全数据混合训练可以有效缓解该问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前关于涌现性不对齐（EM）的研究多集中于监督微调（SFT）场景，且有关强化学习（RL）诱导EM的证据主要源自昂贵且闭源的大模型，导致该现象难以复现和深入研究。因此，本研究旨在探索在小型开源模型中，RL是否也会诱导EM，并评估相关的缓解策略。

Method: 研究人员在小型、开源模型上进行了实验。方法包括：1. 比较强化学习（RL）与监督微调（SFT）诱导出的通用领域不对齐程度；2. 测试不同类型的奖励信号（如审美偏好、修辞缺陷）对模型行为的影响；3. 评估并迁移针对SFT开发的缓解策略，以验证其在RL环境下的有效性。

Result: 1. 奖励窄范围的不对齐行为会比SFT产生更显著的通用领域不对齐；2. 常见的奖励信号（如不受欢迎的审美或拙劣的修辞）足以诱导EM；3. 在SFT中有效的缓解策略在RL环境中同样适用，其中“交替在线策略安全数据”的缓解效果最佳。

Conclusion: 强化学习诱导的涌现性不对齐（EM）是一个显著的风险，其表现比监督微调（SFT）更严重。然而，通过特定的缓解策略（如交替在线策略安全数据），该问题是可以被有效抑制的。本研究为开放模型环境下的安全研究提供了可复现的实验框架。

Abstract: Emergent misalignment (EM) is the surprising tendency of language models to become broadly misaligned after fine-tuning on narrowly misaligned examples. While EM has been extensively studied in the supervised fine-tuning (SFT) setting, evidence that it also arises from reinforcement learning (RL) is limited to large, closed-source models, leaving the phenomenon expensive to study and difficult to reproduce. We characterize EM from RL in small, off-the-shelf open-weight models along three axes. First, we show that rewarding narrow, overtly misaligned behavior produces substantially higher general-domain misalignment than sample-matched SFT. Second, we show that EM from RL can be induced by reward signals that could plausibly arise naturally, such as unpopular aesthetic preferences or poor rhetorical appeals. Third, we evaluate in-training mitigations developed for SFT-induced EM and find that they broadly transfer, with interleaving on-policy safety data performing best.

</details>


### [70] [Bundesrecht: An Open Library and Corpus for German Statutory Reference Processing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31338)
*Harshil Darji,Martin Heckelmann,Christina Kratsch,Gerard de Melo*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文推出了 bundesrecht，这是一个针对德国联邦法律引用的开源处理工具与结构化数据集，能够实现从原始法律引用字符串到具体法条的高效解析、归一化与关联。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 德国法律语言中的引用形式紧凑、变体多、常包含组合目标或特殊缩写，现有的法律自然语言处理工具难以有效解析这些引用并将其与具体的法条文本进行精确关联。

Method: 该研究开发了一个包含软件库和结构化语料库的 bundesrecht 系统。软件库通过解析、归一化和消歧过程，将复杂的原始引用字符串映射为标准化的结构化对象；语料库则详细记录了德国联邦法律从法律层级到细颗粒度子条款的完整层级结构。

Result: 在 2,944 个标注的德国法律引用上进行的评估表明，该解析器和归一化器在严格精确匹配和微观信息提取指标上表现优异，且相比于简单的字符串匹配，其归一化方法能更可靠地对不同表面的引用变体进行分组。

Conclusion: bundesrecht 是首个针对德国法律引用处理的端到端开源工具库和语料库，通过将原始引用映射为结构化对象并链接到具体法条，显著提升了法律引用解析和归一化的可靠性。

Abstract: Statutory references are central to legal language understanding, but are difficult to process automatically, as they appear in compact and variable surface forms, may combine multiple targets, use special abbreviations, and often point to lower-level units. Existing tools for German focus either on parsing references from legal documents or accessing statutory text once citations are explicit. This paper introduces bundesrecht, an open resource for German statutory reference processing, consisting of a software library and a structured corpus of German federal law. The library parses, normalizes, and resolves German statutory references, mapping raw citation strings to structured objects, expanding compact references into canonical forms, and linking them to statutory provisions. The accompanying dataset preserves the internal hierarchy of statutes from laws to fine-granular subclauses. We evaluate the parser and normalizer on 2,944 annotated German legal references using strict exact-match and micro information extraction metrics. We further evaluate canonical reference deduplication and show that normalized references group real citation surface variants far more reliably than string matching. bundesrecht is the first open resource that covers German statutory reference processing as an end-to-end pipeline, from raw citation string to resolved statutory provision, and is available on PyPI.

*Paramananda Bhaskar,Naquee Rizwan,Daksh Jogchand,Saurabh Kumar Pandey,Animesh Mukherjee*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的仇恨模因检测基准存在观察偏差，将修辞机制与目标群体特征混淆，导致模型无法进行因果评估，且在实际应用中表现出严重的泛化能力不足。

Method: 1. 构建了FBHM（基于功能性的仇恨模因）基准，包含25种修辞功能和10个目标群体，共5000个模因；2. 提出了LSV（可学习引导向量）策略，通过在仅500个样本（50个基础模因）上施加因果干预目标，以实现高效的性能提升。

Result: 1. 主流视觉-语言模型（VLM）在FBHM基准上的性能出现断崖式下跌，接近随机水平；2. 使用LSV策略后，模型在FBHM上的Macro-F1指标提升了约30个点，且优于上下文学习（ICL）和参数高效微调（PEFT），且未降低源域性能。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了现有仇恨模因检测模型主要依赖数据集特定启发式算法而非多模态推理的现状，并证明通过因果干预（LSV）可以在极低数据需求下显著增强模型的鲁棒性和通用性。

Abstract: Hateful meme detection remains a formidable challenge for vision-language models, as existing benchmarks are structurally observational - confounding rhetorical hate mechanisms with target community features and preventing causal evaluation of model vulnerabilities. To address this, we introduce FBHM, a systematically curated benchmark of Functionality Based Hateful Memes constructed along two orthogonal axes: 25 distinct rhetorical functionalities and 10 target communities (5,000 memes total). Benchmarking state-of-the-art VLMs reveals a severe generalization gap: models highly accurate on standard datasets catastrophically drop to near-random performance on FBHM, proving they exploit dataset-specific heuristics rather than robust multimodal reasoning. To efficiently close this gap, we propose LSV (learnable steering vectors), an ultra-low data regime strategy that applies a causal intervention objective on as few as 500 steering samples (50 unique base memes), boosting FBHM performance by ~30 Macro-F1 points while outperforming in-context learning and PEFT without degrading source-domain performance.

### [72] [A Visually Impaired Assistance Benchmark for VLM-as-a-Judge Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31351)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 现有的视觉语言模型（VLM）在作为视觉辅助（VIA）任务的自动评估者时表现不可靠且存在严重偏见。本文提出的 VIA-Judge-Agent 通过增强视觉证据提取和分类导向流程，能够显著提升评估的准确性和可用性，为未来开发更可靠的 AI 辅助系统提供了有效途径。

Abstract: AI-based Visually Impaired Assistance (VIA) remains challenging, largely due to the high cost of human evaluation. The VLM-as-a-Judge paradigm may offer a promising alternative, although it has mostly been studied in general domains. We therefore ask whether such judges can be trusted for VIA tasks. To investigate this question, we introduce VIABLE (Visually Impaired Assistance Benchmark for VLM-as-a-Judge Evaluation), the first benchmark for VLM-as-a-Judge evaluation in VIA. VIABLE contains over 300K judgment samples across three scenarios and introduces an Effectiveness--Impartiality--Stability framework with a 12-mode failure taxonomy. Based on VIABLE, our systematic study of seven judges across different model scales shows that existing models are largely unreliable across all evaluation axes. The strongest judge, GPT-5.4, achieves only 52.6% single-failure diagnostic accuracy, yet exhibits the highest self-preference rate at 94.2%; while open-source judges are strongly biased and adversarially fragile. To address these issues, we propose VIA-Judge-Agent, a model-agnostic inference-time harness that augments judges with visual evidence extraction and a taxonomy-guided workflow. It enables positive improvements in diagnostic accuracy and downstream VIA responses more preferred by BLV users. Data and code are available at: https://github.com/YiyiyiZhao/VIABLE

### [73] [Unlocking Fine-Grained Translation Quality Estimation in LRMs through Synergistically Evolving Implicit and Explicit Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31378)
*Renfei Dang,Xinye Wang,Zhejian Lai,Weilu Xu,Shimin Tao,Daimeng Wei,Min Zhang,Shujian Huang*

TL;DR: 本文提出了RIEQE框架，通过结合无推理链监督微调（NonThinking-SFT）和带可验证奖励的强化学习（Thinking-RLVR），有效提升了大模型在细粒度翻译质量评估任务中隐式与显式推理的协同能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大模型（LRM）尽管具备强大的多语言能力，但在细粒度翻译质量评估（QE）任务上表现欠佳，现有研究未能充分挖掘模型隐式与显式推理能力的协同潜力。

Method: 提出了RIEQE框架，包含两个阶段：1. NonThinking-SFT：在没有推理链的情况下进行监督微调，提升模型的隐式推理趋势与能力；2. Thinking-RLVR：使用基于可验证奖励的强化学习，强化显式推理能力。该方法通过将QE任务分解为简单子任务来实现。

Result: 在WMT测试集上，基于Qwen3-4B的RIEQE模型在显式推理性能上超过了所有基线模型，且其隐式推理能力达到目前最优编码器模型水平，验证了隐式与显式推理之间的协同增效作用。

Conclusion: RIEQE框架成功实现了隐式（层级）和显式（标记级）推理能力的协同进化，证明了通过将复杂翻译质量评估任务分解并结合SFT与RLVR，可以有效弥补大模型在细粒度质量评估方面的短板。

Abstract: Large Reasoning Models (LRMs) still struggle with fine-grained translation quality estimation (QE), even with long reasoning chains. We argue that LRMs already possess strong multilingual capabilities, while the core challenge stems from the intrinsic difficulty of learning the fine-grained QE task. In this paper, we propose RIEQE (Reasoning both Implicitly and Explicitly for QE), a simple two-stage training framework that enables the co-evolution of implicit (layer-wise) and explicit (token-wise) reasoning capabilities. To make implicit reasoning feasible, we first decompose the complex QE task into straightforward subtasks. Based on this, our two-stage approach applies: (1) NonThinking-SFT, Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) without reasoning chains to directly boost the model's implicit reasoning tendency and capability; and (2) Thinking-RLVR, standard Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Reward (RLVR) to subsequently strengthen explicit reasoning. Results demonstrate that implicit and explicit reasoning synergistically co-evolve under our framework. On the WMT test sets, RIEQE based on Qwen3-4B-Thinking-2507 surpasses all baselines in explicit reasoning performance, while its implicit reasoning capability is also comparable to the best current encoder-based models. We further provide evidence for the synergistic collaboration between implicit and explicit reasoning, showing how they mutually benefit each other.

Abstract: We evaluate the consistency of automated judges in conducting a multi-dimensional safety evaluation in a reference-free setup. ### [75] [Target-Side Paraphrase Augmentation for Sign Language Translation with Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31393)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究提出了基于目标端增强的训练框架：首先利用GPT-4o对参考句生成多种受控释义变体，以此扩充训练语料，同时保持手语视频输入不变；随后采用两阶段训练策略，即先在增强语料上进行预训练，再在原始数据集上进行微调。此外，引入了LLM-as-a-Judge作为新的评估手段。

Conclusion: 本文首次验证了利用大语言模型生成目标端释义作为数据增强手段在手语翻译任务中的有效性。实验表明，该方法能显著提升翻译的语义保真度，且语义层面的指标往往能捕捉到传统词汇重叠指标所忽略的性能增益。此外，研究也指出了该方法在特定数据分布（如极端长尾或高度受限数据）下的局限性。

Abstract: Sign language translation (SLT) remains constrained by limited paired sign-video/text corpora and heavy-tailed target vocabularies. We study target-side augmentation in which GPT-4o generates controlled paraphrase variants of reference sentences while the sign input remains unchanged. A Signformer-style pose-based Transformer is trained under a two-stage schedule: pre-training on the augmented corpus followed by fine-tuning on the original references.
  We evaluate on three datasets spanning complementary challenges: PHOENIX14T (German Sign Language), with moderate lexical diversity; GSL (Greek Sign Language), with highly ontrolled, repetitive recordings; and LSA-T (Argentinian Sign Language), with severe long-tail sparsity. On PHOENIX14T, augmentation improves BLEU-4 from 9.56 to 10.33. The near-saturated GSL baseline and extremely sparse LSA-T setting reveal the limits of the approach. To our knowledge, this is the first study to apply LLM-generated target-side araphrases and LLM-as-a-Judge evaluation to SLT. The semantic evaluation reveals gains in fidelity that lexical overlap metrics understate.

### [76] [The Sword, Shield, and Achilles' Heel: Characterizing the Linguistic Inductive Bias of Large Language Models for Spatial Reasoning in Navigation Planning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31404)
*Xudong Zhang,Jian Yang,Shengkai Wang,Jiangpeng Tian,Shaowen Chen,Xian Wei,Ke Li,Xiong You*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究通过双重干预框架揭示了大语言模型在导航规划中的语言归纳偏置，指出拓扑结构是稳健性的关键，而错误的语义信息则是导致规划失败的主要原因，建议在设计导航任务表示时应综合平衡这些因素。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于大语言模型的导航系统多采用显式空间表示（如拓扑图），但对于这些文本表示的语言结构及上下文特征选择如何影响模型行为缺乏系统性研究，通常被视为随意的工程决策。作者旨在揭示这些因素如何构成大语言模型的归纳偏置。

Method: 提出了一种双重干预框架（Dual-interventional Framework）来评估大语言模型的语言归纳偏置：1. 表示干预（Representation Intervention）：通过改变语言格式和压缩程度，研究其对导航规划的支持或抑制作用；2. 上下文干预（Context Intervention）：通过上下文特征组合与冲突探测，分析模型处理不同空间特征时的偏好与缺陷。

Result: 实验发现：拓扑信息是稳健规划的基石；语言格式的影响具有双重性，受模型规模、任务需求及压缩程度制约；语义信息是导致规划失效的致命弱点，错误的语义线索会系统性地干扰模型规划。

Conclusion: 该研究强调，基于大语言模型的导航系统在设计文本空间表示时，不能仅将其视为工程细节。设计者应优先保证拓扑结构的完整性，根据模型能力校准表示压缩率，并严格确保语义信息的准确性，以避免由于错误的语义提示导致规划失效。

Abstract: Large Language Model (LLM)-based navigation systems commonly construct explicit spatial representations (e.g., topological graphs, semantic raster maps) and translate them into textual descriptions as LLMs' inputs. However, the linguistic structures of such text-based spatial representations and the choices of contextual features (e.g., topology, geometry) they contain are often treated as neutral engineering decisions rather than key factors that shape LLMs' behavior. To fill the gap, we propose a dual-interventional framework that disentangles linguistic structures from different contextual cues to evaluate the linguistic inductive bias of LLMs for navigation planning. In the framework, representation intervention varies the linguistic format and the degree of linguistic compression, clarifying when linguistic representations support or inhibit navigation planning. Context intervention, combined with contextual feature combination and conflict probing, explicitly clarifies the preferences and weaknesses of LLMs when processing different contextual cues. Experiments across diverse spatial reasoning tasks and multiple model scales reveal a consistent pattern: topological information is a sturdy shield and the backbone of robust planning; linguistic format is a double-edged sword whose effect depends on model size, task demands, and the compression level; and semantic information is a fatal Achilles' heel -- incorrect semantic cues can systematically derail the planning process. Overall, our study shows that effective text-based spatial representations in LLM-based navigation should preserve topological integrity, calibrate representational compression to model capacity, and ensure semantic correctness, rather than simply adopting a single representation. Our code is publicly available at https://github.com/jonesdong150/LLM-Navigation-Inductive-Bias.

</details>


### [77] [SCOPE: Self-Play via Co-Evolving Policies for Open-Ended Tasks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31433)
*Wai-Chung Kwan,Aryo Pradipta Gema,Joshua Ong Jun Leang,Pasquale Minervini*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为 SCOPE 的无数据自博弈框架，通过“挑战者”生成任务、“解决者”回答任务、“冻结模型”充当裁判，在无需外部监督的情况下，显著提升了语言模型处理开放式任务及检索任务的能力，效果超越了依赖人工标注数据的同类方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的自博弈（Self-play）方法通常依赖于规则可验证的任务，对于开放式任务，则往往受限于人工精选提示词或依赖昂贵的强大模型（frontier-model）进行评估。为了解决这一限制，研究者旨在开发一种无需外部标注、且适用于开放式任务的自博弈训练框架。

Method: 提出了一种名为 SCOPE 的无数据自博弈框架。该框架包含两个协同进化的策略：一个是生成基于文档任务的“挑战者”（Challenger），另一个是执行多轮检索并回答任务的“解决者”（Solver）。同时，利用模型初始化的冻结版本作为“自我裁判”，通过源文档生成特定的评分准则并对回答进行评价。

Result: 在 Qwen2.5、Qwen3 和 OLMo-3（7-8B）模型上的测试显示：在八个开放式基准测试中，SCOPE 性能提升最高达 10.4 分，效果持平或优于使用约 9000 条精选提示词训练的 GRPO_data 方法。此外，在七个短问答基准测试中，其性能提升最高达 13.8 分，在所有模型上均表现出色。消融实验证实了挑战者协同进化的必要性以及评分准则生成质量对效果的关键影响。

Conclusion: SCOPE 提供了一种无需标注数据即可提升大语言模型开放式任务性能的有效路径。研究表明，通过让模型在“出题”和“解题”两个策略间协同进化，并利用冻结模型作为自我评估机制，可以显著提升模型的检索与综合能力，且该框架具有良好的通用性和可扩展性。

Abstract: Self-play can train language models without external supervision. However, existing methods require rule-checkable answers, leaving open-ended tasks dependent on curated prompts or frontier-model judges. We introduce SCOPE, a data-free self-play framework for open-ended tasks that co-evolves two policies: a Challenger that generates document-grounded tasks, and a Solver that answers them through multi-turn retrieval. A frozen copy of the initial model serves as the self-judge, which writes task-specific rubrics from the source document and grades Solver responses against them. Across three 7-8B instruction-tuned models (Qwen2.5, Qwen3, OLMo-3), SCOPE improves open-ended performance by up to +10.4 points on eight benchmarks and matches or exceeds GRPO_data trained on ~9K curated prompts. Although trained only on open-ended tasks, SCOPE also improves held-out short-form QA by up to +13.8 points on seven held-out benchmarks, surpassing GRPO_data on all three models. Ablations show that co-evolving the Challenger is necessary to keep tasks near the Solver's frontier, that gains arise from improvements in both retrieval and synthesis with the relative contribution varying by task, and that rubric generation quality is the bottleneck for self-judging.

</details>


### [78] [Fine-grained Verification via Diagnostic Reasoning Supervision for Aspect Sentiment Triplet Extraction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31446)
*Wenna Lai,Haoran Xie,Guandong Xu,Qing Li,S. Joe Qin*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文针对ASTE任务提出了FiVeD框架，通过引入诊断推理和细粒度验证机制，能够有效过滤和优化抽取模型输出的候选三元组，从而显著提高ASTE系统的整体抽取性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的方面情感三元组抽取（ASTE）研究多关注端到端抽取，忽略了对抽取结果的事后验证，导致预测结果在局部合理但全局无效。此外，候选结果的无效性具有多面性，且可用性存在差异，缺乏细粒度的验证机制来过滤或优化不同抽取器的输出。

Method: 提出FiVeD框架，包含以下核心部分：1. 多任务学习：以有效性分类和质量打分为主要任务，以错误类型分类和推理生成为辅助任务；2. 诊断监督：利用现成大语言模型（LLM）结合特定规则生成质量评分和诊断解释；3. 层次化错误分类：定义细粒度的错误类别，并通过语义和句法约束构建负样本；4. 过滤机制：在推理阶段利用质量分数对候选结果进行筛选和重排序。

Result: 在多个ASTE基准模型上的实验结果表明，FiVeD框架作为即插即用的模块，最高可提升3.53个F1值，证明了其在提升抽取结果可靠性和性能方面的有效性。

Conclusion: 本文提出的FiVeD框架通过引入细粒度验证和诊断推理机制，有效解决了ASTE任务中端到端抽取模型在全局一致性上的不足。实验证明，该方法作为一种即插即用的模块，能够显著提升现有ASTE模型的抽取性能，并为系统提供了可控的精度与召回率平衡。

Abstract: Aspect Sentiment Triplet Extraction (ASTE) aims to identify aspect terms, opinion terms, and sentiment polarities as structured triplets, providing essential inputs for downstream information system applications such as opinion mining, explainable recommendations, and review summarization. Prior work mainly focuses on end-to-end extraction, while post hoc verification of extracted triplets remains comparatively underexplored. This gap limits the reliability of ASTE systems, since predicted triplets may be locally plausible while being globally invalid. Moreover, candidate invalidity is multi-faceted and candidate usability is inherently graded, motivating a fine-grained verification mechanism that can filter or re-rank outputs from diverse extractors. In this paper, we propose FiVeD, a framework for Fine-grained Verification with Diagnostic reasoning supervision. Specifically, the verifier is trained with multiple complementary objectives, including validity classification and quality score estimation as primary tasks, with error type classification and rationale generation as auxiliary tasks. We define hierarchical error categories and construct plausible incorrect triplets under semantic and syntactic constraints, and leverage an off-the-shelf LLM with task-specific rubrics to produce quality scores and diagnostic rationales. During inference, the resulting quality scores are used to filter candidate outputs, supporting adjustable precision-recall tradeoffs. Experiments across multiple ASTE baselines demonstrate that FiVeD consistently improves extraction performance by up to 3.53 F1 points as a plug-and-play verification module.

### [79] [Translation Analytics for Freelancers II: Benchmarking Local LLMs for Confidential Translation Workflows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31452)
*Yuri Balashov,Rex VanHorn,Mingxi Xu,Austin Downes*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 对于有隐私保密需求的自由译员和小型语言服务提供商而言，精心挑选的本地化大语言模型是进行离线翻译的切实可行方案。该研究证实了在无需微调的情况下，本地模型已能达到或超越部分专业级本地神经机器翻译（NMT）系统的水平，为行业内评估和应用翻译技术提供了低门槛的参考框架。

Abstract: Building on our previous work, this paper develops practical, low-barrier methods for freelance translators and smaller language service providers to evaluate translation technologies using rigorous yet accessible analytic methods. Here we address a high-stakes, specialized need: offline translation for confidentiality-sensitive domains in which privacy constraints preclude the use of cloud-based engines and commercial LLMs. We expand the Reeve Foundation Trilingual Corpus (RFTC) used in our previous work into a multilingual corpus (RFMC) by adding sentence-aligned German and Simplified Chinese reference translations. We then benchmark several locally runnable language models (via Ollama) across four language directions on 1000+ sentences selected from this corpus. We use consistent single-prompt calls without fine-tuning or domain adaptation, comparing local LLM outputs against commercial NMTs (DeepL, Baidu), a frontier LLM (GPT-5.2), and professional-grade local NMT systems (OPUS-CAT, NeuralDesktop, Promt). Automatic evaluation is conducted with MATEO. Results reveal substantial variation in local LLM performance across language directions and model sizes. The best local LLMs match or surpass local NMT systems and a frontier LLM, though they remain behind top commercial NMTs. These findings underscore the viability of carefully selected local LLM translation for privacy-constrained professionals and inform future research on model scaling and multilingual capability.

### [80] [Scaling Conversational Hungarian ASR: The BEA-Dialogue+ Corpus](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31469)
*Máté Gedeon,Piroska Zsófia Barta,Péter Mihajlik,Katalin Mády*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1. 构建 BEA-Dialogue+ 语料库：在保持主要发言人严格分离的前提下，放宽了实验者和对话伙伴的划分标准，将可用数据量从 85 小时扩展至 200 小时。
