Result: 1. 实验表明，对于未经过微调的模型，更大的数据集（BEA-Dialogue+）反而带来了更大的挑战。
2. 应用 SOT 微调后，模型在 WER（字错误率）、CER（字符错误率）、cpWER 和 cpCER 等指标上均表现出持续的性能改进。
3. BEA-Dialogue+ 成功将语料库规模提升至 200 小时，为对话转录系统的训练和评估提供了更丰富的资源。

Conclusion: BEA-Dialogue+ 为匈牙利语对话自动语音识别（ASR）提供了一个更大且更具挑战性的基准测试集。研究证明，通过放宽数据划分限制以增加训练数据量，并结合 SOT（串行输出训练）微调技术，可以显著提升模型在对话场景下的识别性能。

Abstract: Conversational automatic speech recognition in Hungarian is constrained by the limited amount of publicly available dialogue-style training data. The BEA-Dialogue corpus addresses this need, but its strictly speaker-disjoint train/dev/eval split reduces the usable material to only 85 hours. In this paper, we introduce BEA-Dialogue+, an expanded version of the corpus that relaxes the split criterion for experimenters and dialogue partners while preserving complete separation of the primary speakers. This results in 200 hours of transcribed natural conversations and enables a controlled study of the trade-off between additional training data and speaker overlap across the splits. We evaluate several Whisper- and FastConformer-based models on both corpus versions, including Serialized Output Training (SOT)-based fine-tuning for dialogue transcription. Our results show that the larger corpus is more challenging for models without fine-tuning, whereas SOT-based adaptation yields consistent improvements in WER, CER, cpWER, and cpCER. Overall, BEA-Dialogue+ provides a substantially larger yet still demanding benchmark for Hungarian dialogue ASR, and a practical resource for training and evaluating dialogue transcription systems.

### [81] [Language Models Can Resolve Reference Compositionally, But It's Not Their Native Strength: The Case of the Personal Relation Task](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31480)
*Bart Evelo,Meaghan Fowlie,Denis Paperno*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 研究对比了人类与大语言模型（LLM）在理解语言逻辑结构（内涵）与识别世界指代对象（外延）方面的能力，发现二者存在显著的结构性能力差异，揭示了LLM因缺乏指涉基础而难以实现完全的人类水平语义理解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在探讨大语言模型是否真正具备组合式的语言理解能力。作者区分了语义解释的两个维度：指代现实世界实体的能力（外延）和以结构化方式表示语义的能力（内涵），并试图通过对比人类与模型的表现来揭示模型在处理这两类任务时的机制差异。

Method: 研究采用“个人关系任务”（Personal Relation Task），要求人类和LLM在已知人物关系集合中解释短语（如“Amber的父母的朋友”）。通过对比两种任务：1. 内涵任务（Intensional task）：要求将短语转化为逻辑公式（如 friend(parent(amber))）；2. 外延任务（Extensional task）：要求识别出具体指代的对象。研究对比了二者在这些任务上的表现差异。

Result: 实验发现人类与LLM展现出相反的能力偏好：人类在外延任务上表现更好，而LLM在内涵任务（逻辑结构推导）上表现更佳。这揭示了LLM虽然擅长处理符号结构，但缺乏将语义与现实世界对象关联的指涉基础。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，尽管大语言模型（LLM）在结构化语义表示（内涵任务）方面表现出色，但由于缺乏现实世界的指涉基础（referential grounding），它们在理解语言如何映射到现实世界（外延任务）方面与人类存在根本差异。这意味着单纯的语言建模不足以完全复制人类的语言理解能力。

Abstract: Do neural models, such as Large Language Models, genuinely acquire compositional abilities for interpretation of natural language? When we talk about semantic interpretation, we can distinguish two complementary aspects: establishing what an expression refers to in the world (which we call the Extensional task) and representing its sense in a structured way (which we call the Intensional task). We evaluate LLMs and humans on both tasks in the setting of the Personal Relation Task (Paperno 2022) in which, given a universe of people and their relationships with each other, one is asked to interpret a noun phrase such as "Amber's parent's friend". Here, for the Intensional task, the answer is the formula "friend(parent(amber))", and for the Extensional task, the person. We find that humans and LLMs show opposite strengths: humans perform better on Extensional than Intensional tasks, and LLMs vice versa. Our methodology brings greater nuance to the understanding of compositional abilities in modern machine learning models. Our results support the notion that the lack of referential grounding in LLM training is a crucial missing component in mimicking human-like language understanding.

</details>


### [82] [BenHalluEval: A Multi-Task Hallucination Evaluation Framework for Large Language Models on Bengali](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31483)
*Shefayat E Shams Adib,Ahmed Alfey Sani,Ekramul Alam Esham,Ajwad Abrar,Ishmam Tashdeed,Md Taukir Azam Chowdhury*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文填补了孟加拉语 LLM 幻觉评估的空白，提出了 BenHalluEval 框架和 BenHalluScore 指标，研究发现现有的提示策略难以解决低资源语言中的模型幻觉问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 孟加拉语虽是全球第六大语言，但目前缺乏针对大型语言模型（LLM）的系统性幻觉评估机制。现有研究多集中于高资源语言，忽略了低资源语言在幻觉检测上的特殊性和复杂性。

Method: 1. 构建 BenHalluEval 框架，涵盖生成式问答、代码混杂问答、摘要和推理四项任务；2. 利用 GPT-4 生成包含 12,000 个幻觉候选项的数据集，覆盖 12 种幻觉类型；3. 采用双轨协议（Track A 测误报率，Track B 测幻觉检出率）评估七种 LLM；4. 提出 BenHalluScore 指标，用于联合惩罚两种失效模式并避免均匀响应偏差。

Result: 研究发现不同模型和任务间的幻觉校准存在巨大差异（BenHalluScore 分数跨度为 7.72% 至 55.42%）；思维链（CoT）提示策略能改变响应分布，但不能持续提升模型对幻觉的辨别能力。

Conclusion: BenHalluEval 是首个专门针对孟加拉语的幻觉评估基准。研究证明，单一的评估维度或单纯依靠提示工程（如思维链）在低资源语言场景下不足以有效缓解幻觉问题，必须采用双轨校准机制来全面评估模型。

Abstract: Despite Bengali being the sixth most spoken language in the world, no prior work has systematically evaluated hallucination in large language models (LLMs) for Bengali. We introduce BenHalluEval, a fine-grained hallucination evaluation framework for Bengali covering four tasks: Generative Question Answering (GQA), Bangla-English Code-Mixed QA, Summarization, and Reasoning. We construct 12,000 hallucinated candidates using GPT-5.4 across twelve task-specific hallucination types, drawn from three existing Bengali datasets, and evaluate seven LLMs spanning reasoning-oriented, multilingual, and Bengali-centric categories under a dual-track protocol that independently measures false-positive rate on ground-truth instances (Track A) and hallucination detection rate on hallucinated candidates (Track B). To jointly penalise both failure modes and prevent inflated scores from uniform response bias, we propose BenHalluScore, a dual-track calibration metric that ranges from 7.72% to 55.42% across models and tasks, revealing substantial variation in hallucination calibration. Chain-of-thought prompting, applied as a mitigation strategy, shifts response distributions without consistently improving hallucination discrimination. BenHalluEval establishes the first dedicated hallucination benchmark for Bengali and highlights the inadequacy of single-track and prompting-only evaluation approaches for low-resource language settings. The dataset and code are available at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/BanglaHalluEval-EB77.

</details>


### [83] [Are Full Rollouts Necessary for On-Policy Distillation?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31490)
*Yaocheng Zhang,Jiajun Chai,Songjun Tu,Yuqian Fu,Xiaohan Wang,Wei Lin,Guojun Yin,Qichao Zhang,Yuanheng Zhu,Dongbin Zhao*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文针对在线策略蒸馏（OPD）中完整滚动轨迹带来的计算负担和反馈噪声问题，提出了通过动态控制滚动视野（POPD和TOPD）来提升训练效率的方法，实现了在保持推理性能的同时大幅减少计算成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准的在线策略蒸馏（OPD）在训练中通常生成完整的滚动轨迹，这不仅计算成本高昂，且在训练初期可能因引入不可靠的教师反馈而导致性能下降；研究旨在突破完整滚动轨迹对训练效率的限制。

Method: 提出了两种视野控制策略：1. 渐进式策略蒸馏（POPD）：在训练过程中逐步增加滚动视野的长度；2. 截断式策略蒸馏（TOPD）：仅在可靠的截断滚动视野上执行蒸馏。

Result: 实验表明，POPD将训练效率提升了高达3倍；TOPD在仅使用10%滚动视野的情况下即可达到与标准OPD相当的性能，显著降低了运行时间和内存需求。

Conclusion: 通过控制策略中滚动视野（rollout horizon）的长度，研究证明了无需完整轨迹即可进行有效的策略蒸馏。该方法不仅大幅降低了计算成本和内存占用，还提升了长程推理任务中的训练效率，为策略蒸馏提供了一种轻量且高效的优化范式。

Abstract: On-policy distillation (OPD) provides dense teacher feedback along rollouts generated by the student and has emerged as a promising post-training paradigm for long-horizon reasoning. However, standard OPD typically generates full rollouts during training, which is computationally expensive and may expose the student to unreliable teacher feedback at late rollout positions, especially during early training. We identify the rollout horizon as a key bottleneck in OPD that substantially impacts training efficiency. Unlike Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR), OPD does not require a complete trajectory or a final answer reward to provide learning signals. This observation suggests that full rollouts may not always be necessary for effective OPD. Motivated by this insight, we propose two simple horizon-control strategies: Progressive OPD (POPD), which gradually expands the rollout horizon during training, and Truncated OPD (TOPD), which permanently performs distillation on reliable truncated rollouts. Experiments on mathematical reasoning show that POPD improves the training efficiency of OPD by up to 3$\times$, while TOPD matches OPD performance using only 10\% of the rollout horizon, leading to substantial wall-clock and memory reductions. These results demonstrate that controlling the rollout horizon offers a simple and practical path to more efficient OPD.

</details>


### [84] [Consolidating Rewarded Perturbations for LLM Post-Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31494)
*Zheyu Zhang,Shuo Yang,Gjergji Kasneci*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: CoRP 是一种新型梯度无关优化算法，通过挖掘模型权重更新的低秩结构，将多个受奖励驱动的扰动模型合并为一个单一模型，在极大地降低推理成本的同时，实现了优于传统集成方法的性能提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于权重空间的优化方法（如 RandOpt）通常需要在推理时进行 K 次前向传播（集成），这带来了极高的计算成本且难以扩展至自由生成任务。研究者旨在探究是否可以将这些奖励模型集成到一个单一的、可部署的模型中，以消除推理时的性能开销，同时保留梯度无关优化的优势。

Method: 研究团队提出了 CoRP（Consolidating Rewarded Perturbations）算法。该方法首先通过采样多个高斯扰动模型来收集信息，利用 split-half 分析揭示了权重空间的低秩结构。随后，CoRP 通过奖励加权聚合、兼容性感知重加权以及留出验证门控（held-out validation gate）机制，将多个扰动模型合并为一个单一的可部署模型，整个过程无需通过大语言模型进行反向传播。

Result: 在覆盖数学、代码和创意写作等五个任务、五种不同规模（0.5B 至 8B）的模型上，CoRP 表现优异：相比基准模型，平均性能提升了 8.1 分；在仅使用 RandOpt 十分之一个扰动预算的情况下，CoRP 的单次推理性能比 RandOpt 提升了 6.5 分，并能恢复 50 次前向传播多数投票集成方法中超过一半的增益。

Conclusion: CoRP 证明了可以通过合并多个奖励模型扰动来蒸馏出一个单一的高性能模型，从而在保持低推理成本的同时实现与大型集成模型相当的性能提升。该研究揭示了语言模型微调后的低秩结构，为梯度无关的优化提供了一种高效的替代方案。

Abstract: Post-training of language models is commonly framed as a sample-score-update loop implemented by gradient descent. A recent line of work, exemplified by RandOpt, relocates this loop to weight space, sampling Gaussian perturbations around a pretrained model and ensembling the top-K rewarded specialists at inference. While competitive with PPO and GRPO under matched training compute, this prediction-level ensemble incurs K forward passes per test example and does not extend cleanly to free-form generation. We ask whether the rewarded population can instead be folded into a single deployable model, replacing the inference-time ensemble with one consolidated update. A split-half analysis over 25 model-task pairs reveals reproducible low-rank structure in every case. We turn this geometry into CoRP (Consolidating Rewarded Perturbations), a gradient-free operator that combines reward-weighted aggregation, compatibility-aware reweighting, and a held-out validation gate, with no gradient flowing through the language model. Across five language models from 0.5B to 8B and five tasks covering math, code, and creative writing, CoRP improves the base model by 8.1 points on average. Using one tenth of RandOpt's perturbation budget, CoRP exceeds single-inference RandOpt by 6.5 points and recovers more than half of the gain of the 50-pass majority-vote ensemble, at one forward pass per test example.

</details>


### [85] [Reliable Multilingual Orthopedic Decision Support from Clinical Narratives: Language-Aware Adaptation and Verification-Guided Deferral](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31512)
*Danish Ali,Li Xiaojian,Sundas Iqbal,Farrukh Zaidi*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文提出了IndicBERT-HPA模型及其配套的选择性验证框架，有效解决了医疗资源匮乏地区多语言骨科临床文本分类的难题，通过任务微调和确定性弃权机制显著提升了临床决策支持系统的可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在医疗资源匮乏地区，骨科临床叙述存在专业术语复杂、多脚本混杂、数据缺失、标签不平衡以及语言特定记录模式等挑战，导致多语言临床决策支持面临巨大困难。现有方法难以在多语言环境下保持高性能与高可靠性，因此需要构建一个能有效处理这些问题的框架。

Method: 本研究构建了一个面向可靠性的多语言骨科临床文本分类框架。核心方法包括：1. 开发了“IndicBERT-HPA”模型，通过为IndicBERT添加语言感知骨科适配器（adapter heads）来实现多语言表示学习；2. 进行了全面的对比评估，涵盖多种Transformer架构、微调基准及零样本指令微调的大语言模型；3. 引入了一个确定性选择性验证层，结合了置信度门控、证据一致性检查和语言风险筛选机制，以实现临床决策的自动弃权（deferral）。

Conclusion: 研究表明，面向可靠性的多语言临床决策支持系统是可行的。通过引入领域自适应编码器（IndicBERT-HPA）和确定性选择性验证层，可以在低资源语言环境下显著提升骨科临床文本分类的性能和可靠性。该方法证明了在临床任务中，专门微调的任务适配模型比通用大语言模型更具效能，且通过引入显式拒绝机制，能有效平衡临床应用中的准确性与覆盖率。

Abstract: Multilingual orthopedic decision support remains challenging in low-resource healthcare settings, where clinical narratives contain specialized terminology, mixed scripts, incomplete evidence, label imbalance and language-dependent documentation patterns. This article presents a reliability-oriented framework for classifying free-text orthopedic notes in English, Hindi and Punjabi. We compare task-aligned multilingual transformer encoders, a task-fine-tuned DistilBERT baseline, zero-shot instruction-tuned large language models (LLMs) and a domain-adaptive encoder, IndicBERT-HPA. IndicBERT-HPA augments IndicBERT with language-aware orthopedic adapter heads to support clinically relevant multilingual representation learning. Evaluation extends beyond aggregate accuracy to per-class performance, ROC-AUC, AUPRC, expected calibration error, cross-language stability and robustness under controlled balanced and natural-prevalence distributions. The evaluated zero-shot LLMs remain substantially less effective than task-adapted encoders for closed-set classification, with language-dependent instability. Under natural clinical prevalence, IndicBERT-HPA achieves the strongest overall performance, reaching an averaged Macro-F1 of 0.8792, Macro-AUROC of 0.894 and AUPRC of 0.902. We further implement a deterministic selective-verification layer combining confidence gating, evidence-consistency checking and language-risk screening. On a randomly selected held-out 5,000-record subset, it achieves 84.4% selective accuracy and 0.76 selective Macro-F1 at 72.3% coverage, compared with 71.5% accuracy and 0.65 Macro-F1 for accept-all prediction. These results support reliability-oriented multilingual clinical decision support with explicit deferral.

### [86] [If LLMs Have Human-Like Attributes, Then So Does Age of Empires II](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31514)
*Adrian de Wynter*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文挑战了当前大语言模型研究中常见的拟人化假设，指出所谓的“智能”或“理解”并非模型独有，而是与环境基底相关的表面现象。作者建议用“非唯一性”的零假设替代拟人假设，以构建更严谨的实验度量标准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前关于大语言模型（LLM）的研究中，存在将道德、理解力等通用拟人化属性强加于模型的普遍趋势。作者旨在指出这些结论可能存在误导性，因为这些属性并非LLM所独有，且过度拟人化会导致研究缺乏客观的度量标准，从而陷入逻辑上的循环或无意义的推论。

Method: 本文采用了理论分析与实验演示相结合的方法。首先，通过将《帝国时代II》训练成一个功能完备且图灵完备的系统，演示了即使是简单的计算基底也能表现出与复杂系统类似的“拟人化”行为。随后，通过逻辑推导证明了在脱离特定基底的情况下讨论通用拟人属性会导致循环论证，并提出了一种基于“非唯一性”的实验设计零假设。

Result: 研究表明，拟人化属性在不同基底（如电子游戏、乐高积木或现实地理区域）中具有非唯一性，其呈现特征高度依赖于观察者的解释。此外，作者证明了《帝国时代II》在功能上和计算上是图灵完备的，进一步支持了“任何足够复杂的基底都可能表现出类似LLM的表面特征”这一观点。

Conclusion: LLM所谓的拟人化属性并非其独有，而是取决于观察者的解释及所处的环境（基底）。作者主张在研究中应放弃预设的拟人化假设，转而采用“非唯一性”的零假设，以避免循环论证，并推动科学界建立更客观、明确的度量标准。

Abstract: Much research has been carried out on large language models (LLMs) and LLM-powered agentic workflows. However, many works within the field state emergence of, ascribe to, or assume, generalised anthropomorphic attributes to them (e.g., morality or understanding of natural language). Our goal is not to argue in favour or against the existence of these attributes, but to point out that these conclusions could be incorrect. For this we build and train a simple neural network on the videogame Age of Empires II, and note that any entity in a sufficiently-powerful substrate, such as LEGO or the Greater Boston Area, could also present such attributes. Hence, the purported anthropomorphic attributes of LLMs are empirically non-unique: although some properties (e.g., responses to prompts) could remain constant, others, such as the interpretation of their perceived behaviour, might change with the substrate. Thus, any empirically-grounded discussion requires explicit measurement criteria; otherwise the interpretation is left to the representation. We then show that assuming that these attributes exist or not in a system, independent of the substrate and in a generalised way, leads to either circular or uninformative conclusions, regardless of the experimenter's viewpoint on the subject. Finally we propose a 'null' assumption, where one assumes LLM non-uniqueness instead of assuming anthropomorphic attributes to set up an experiment, along with examples of it. We also discuss potential objections to our work, briefly survey the field, and prove that \textit{Age of Empires II} is functionally- and Turing-complete.

### [87] [Semantic Triplet Restoration: A Novel Protocol for Hierarchical Table Understanding in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31550)
*Yibin Zhao,Fangxin Shang,Dingrui Yang,Yuqi Wang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种名为STR的表格数据表示方法，通过将表格转换为轻量级的语义三元组而非繁杂的标记语言，提升了表格问答效率与模型推理性能，有效节省了计算资源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有表格问答系统常将表格转化为HTML或Markdown格式，这类布局导向的序列化方式会引入大量标记开销，且增加了大型语言模型在解析复杂单元格合并及层级表头时的推理难度。

Method: 提出“语义三元组还原”（Semantic Triplet Restoration, STR）协议，将表格单元格重写为<项路径, 特征路径, 值>的原子事实；同时设计了TripletQL，一种轻量级的查询感知路由机制，用于为特定问题筛选最相关的三元组子集。

Result: 在四个中英文表格问答基准测试中，STR在匹配或超越基于HTML基线模型性能的同时，显著减少了输入Token数量，特别是在小型模型和长表格上下文中表现出明显的优势。

Conclusion: STR通过将复杂的表格结构显式转化为原子事实三元组，有效解决了现有基于标记语言（如HTML/Markdown）的表格表示方法在处理复杂布局和上下文长度限制上的痛点。这种方法不仅提升了模型在表格问答任务上的性能，还显著降低了计算成本，尤其适用于轻量级模型和长上下文场景。

Abstract: Table question answering requires models to recover semantic relations encoded implicitly by two-dimensional layout, merged cells, and hierarchical headers. Current pipelines typically use HTML or Markdown as intermediate table representations, but these layout-oriented serializations introduce markup overhead and require large language models to infer header-cell alignments from row and column spans. We propose Semantic Triplet Restoration (STR), a protocol that rewrites each cell as an atomic fact <item path, feature path, value>, where the item path specifies the row-wise entity, the feature path specifies the hierarchical attribute, and the value contains the cell content. We also present TripletQL, a lightweight query-aware router that uses STR to select an appropriate rendering or filtered subset of triplets for each question. Across four Chinese and English table-QA benchmarks, STR matches or improves upon HTML-based baselines while reducing input tokens. The relative benefit grows for smaller language models and longer table contexts, suggesting that explicit semantic representations are especially useful under constrained inference budgets. Code and data are available at https://github.com/Phoenix-ni/STR.git .

</details>


### [88] [What Am I Missing? Question-Answering as Hidden State Probing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31561)
*Chu Fei Luo,Samuel Dahan,Xiaodan Zhu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文探讨了大模型在推理过程中通过“自我提问”进行测试时干预的可行性，发现虽然可以通过分析隐藏状态准确预测推理结果，但现有的干预策略在修复错误路径时往往会损害正确路径，揭示了模型自我诊断与自我修正能力之间的差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的测试时推理（如思维链）在处理同一输入时存在输出不一致的现象，且其内部推理机制尚不明确。研究者旨在探讨是否可以通过“提问”这一行为作为推理时的干预手段，挖掘模型隐藏状态中的信号，以改善推理表现。

Method: 提出了一种基于师生模型框架的推理时干预机制。首先，训练一个探测器（probe）来分析学生模型在提问前后的隐藏状态，以预测推理轨迹的正确性；随后，将提问过程建模为一个顺序决策问题，并定义门控策略（gating policy），通过该探测器的质量分数来决定是否提问，以最大化推理正确率。

Result: 实验结果表明，该探测器能够有效预测推理轨迹的最终正确性；然而，提出的门控提问策略在应用时表现出局限性：该干预手段虽然能捕捉模型的不确定性，但在尝试修正错误路径时，同样有很高概率破坏原本正确的路径，即诊断与恢复之间存在明显鸿沟。

Conclusion: 研究发现，尽管利用提问作为推理时干预能够有效诊断模型当前推理路径的正确性，但目前的干预手段在修正错误路径的同时也极易破坏正确的路径。这揭示了语言模型在不确定性下的“自我诊断”与“自我修正”能力之间存在显著差距，为后续研究大模型推理的自我完善能力提供了关键启示。

Abstract: Test-time reasoning has become a significant field of study since the introduction of chain-of-thought reasoning in large language models (LLMs). However, the mechanisms of this reasoning process are still under-explored -- from the same input prompt, and even the same partial solution, LLMs can produce varied answers if sampled multiple times. We propose to leverage question-asking as an inference-time intervention that articulates information about the model's hidden state. To achieve that, we present a student-teacher setting where a student asks questions to a teacher. We train a probe on the student's hidden state before and after asking a question and find it is predictive of the trajectory's final correctness, even before generating the teacher's answer. This suggests there is a meaningful signal from the self-diagnosis that occurs during question generation rather than information transfer from the teacher. We then frame question-asking as a sequential decision problem, using this probe as a quality score, and define a gating policy to ask questions that maximize likelihood of correctness. We find that the success of question-asking as an intervention is largely dependent on the model's self-consistency. Our empirical results show a gap between detection and recovery; while our gating policy captures model correctness and uncertainty, interventions are equally likely to harm correct trajectories as they are to recover incorrect ones. This gap between diagnosis and correction has broader implications on language models' capacity for self-refinement under uncertainty.

### [89] [Disagreeing Rationales: Rethinking Classification and Explainability Evaluation in Hate Speech Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31563)
*Benedetta Muscato,Beiduo Chen,Gizem Gezici,Barbara Plank,Fosca Giannotti*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 作者构建了一个统一的监督框架，通过系统地重新实现多种模型、训练策略、损失函数及现有的评估指标，涵盖了不同的标签（硬标签与软标签）和理由表示空间（硬、中介与软）。评估维度包括分类性能（预测性和分布性）以及可解释性（合理性、忠实性和复杂度）。

Result: 实验结果显示，采用软性表示法能够更有效地反映人类标注的多样性和推理过程。研究验证了不同表示空间和指标对模型行为的影响，证明了在主观任务中，软性评价指标比传统的硬标签指标更能捕捉到推理过程的丰富性。

Conclusion: 研究表明，无论是硬指标还是软指标，软性表示法（soft representations）在捕捉人类标注和解释的多样性方面表现更佳。这强调了在主观性较强的自然语言处理（NLP）任务中，重新评估现有评估体系的必要性，并指出应当从单纯追求“硬”共识转向容纳标注中的差异性。

Abstract: Human disagreement is ubiquitous and well-known in labeling. However, variation in explanations, captured through token-level human rationales, remains far less explored. At the same time, it is unclear how to best evaluate human labels and rationales -- or even how to best aggregate rationales beyond majority vote -- in light of this variation. Yet, rationales may provide additional insights into the richness of human reasoning, that may differ in style, values and interpretations -- especially in subjective NLP tasks like hate speech detection. In this work, we unify diverse models, training strategies, loss functions, and existing evaluation metrics under a single protocol by systematically re-implementing them across different label and rationale representation spaces. Classification metrics are organized around two key properties -- predictive and distributional -- while explainability metrics through three complementary dimensions: plausibility, faithfulness, and complexity. In this unified supervision framework, we evaluate model behavior across classification and explainability metrics, as well as metric sensitivity to the choice of label (hard and soft) and rationale representation space (hard, intermediate and soft). Results show that both hard and soft metrics favor softer representations, highlighting their effectiveness in capturing variation and the need to rethink evaluation in subjective NLP.

### [90] [What Gets Unmasked First? Trajectory Analysis of Diffusion Models for Graph-to-Text Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31564)
*Qing Wang,Jacob Devasier,Chengkai Li*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文对掩码扩散语言模型（MDLM）在图到文本生成中的应用进行了首个系统性研究，揭示了SFT会破坏模型原有的解码规律，并提出了改进的推理策略和Graph-LLaDA架构，有效解决了模型过早固定结构标记导致的质量问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管掩码扩散语言模型在自然语言生成中表现优异，但其在图到文本生成任务中的具体运作机制尚不明确，且监督微调（SFT）过程可能破坏模型原有的逻辑生成轨迹，导致生成质量受损，因此需要系统研究并优化这一过程。

Method: 1. 分析了MDLM的解码轨迹，发现其存在“实体优先、结构滞后”的自然生成模式；2. 提出了“lambda-scaled structural decoding”方法，通过在推理阶段降低结构性标记的置信度，从而纠正SFT带来的解码偏差；3. 构建了Graph-LLaDA模型，将图Transformer编码器整合到LLaDA的解码过程中。

Result: 1. 发现SFT会迫使模型过早固定结构性标记，导致信息缺失或幻觉；2. lambda-scaled structural decoding方法在指标上实现了+9.4 BLEU-4的显著提升；3. Graph-LLaDA在LAGRANGE基准测试中展现出比传统基线更好的泛化能力。

Conclusion: 本文证实了掩码扩散语言模型（MDLM）在图到文本生成任务中的潜力，揭示了监督微调可能导致的解码偏差，并提出的无训练推理改进方法能显著提升生成质量，为该领域提供了新的模型架构与优化策略。

Abstract: We present the first systematic study of masked diffusion language models (MDLMs) for graph-to-text generation. We analyze MDLM generation trajectories -- the order in which tokens are unmasked during iterative decoding -- and find that, unlike autoregressive LLMs which generate text linearly, MDLMs naturally prioritize entities first, followed by relational and function words, with structural tokens resolved last. We further identify a previously undocumented failure mode of supervised fine-tuning: SFT disrupts this strategy by prematurely anchoring structural sentence-ending tokens early in the decoding trajectory, effectively fixing the output length which can lead to omitted or hallucinated information. To address this, we propose lambda-scaled structural decoding, a training-free inference-time modification that downweights structural token confidence and recovers +9.4 BLEU-4. Finally, we introduce Graph-LLaDA, which integrates a Graph Transformer encoder into LLaDA's decoding process to explicitly incorporate relational graph structure. Cross-dataset evaluation on LAGRANGE reveals that previous baselines overfit to dataset-specific patterns, while LLM- and MDLM-based approaches generalize significantly better.

</details>


### [91] [Language Models Learn Constructional Semantics, Not To Mention Syntax: Investigating LM Understanding of Paired-Focus Constructions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31586)
*Wesley Scivetti,Ethan Wilcox,Nathan Schneider,Kanishka Misra,Leonie Weissweiler*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究通过评估不同规模的语言模型对英语中“配对焦点”构式的理解，揭示了适中规模的开源模型具备习得稀有构式语义的能力，且发现此类语义理解通常在句法知识习得之后涌现，并与通用世界知识的增长相关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管大型语言模型在处理稀有构式语义方面表现出色，但开源模型是否具备稳健的构式理解能力，以及这种知识习得背后的学习动态尚不明确。本研究旨在探讨适中规模模型在理解稀有构式方面的能力及其学习机制。

Method: 作者构建了一个包含“let alone”、“much less”等配对焦点构式的新数据集，涵盖标量形容词语义和通用世界知识。通过测试不同参数规模、架构和预训练数据量的模型，评估模型对这些构式的理解能力，并分析了开源模型在训练过程中构式句法知识与语义知识习得的动态演变规律。

Result: 实验发现，部分适中规模的模型能够感知配对焦点构式的形式与含义，而仅基于人类规模数据训练的模型则无法完成语义评估任务。训练动态分析表明，模型对配对焦点语义的理解滞后于句法知识的习得，且语义习得与模型世界知识的提升呈正相关。

Conclusion: 本研究证实，适中规模的开源模型具备理解稀有“配对焦点”（Paired-Focus）构式的能力，且这种语义理解能力的习得与通用世界知识的获取存在关联，为理解语言模型中构式语义的涌现提供了经验证据。

Abstract: Grasping the semantics of rare constructions (form-meaning pairings) has been shown to be a challenging problem that has currently only been solved by the largest LLMs. It remains an open question if open-source models have robust constructional understanding, and if so, what learning dynamics underlie the acquisition of this knowledge. Focusing on a set of rare Paired-Focus constructions in English (e.g. "let alone", "much less"), we construct a novel dataset to test their meanings using both scalar adjectival semantics and general world knowledge. Testing a wide range of models differing in parameter count, architecture, and pretraining dataset size, we find that several modestly sized models are sensitive to both the forms and the meanings of Paired-Focus constructions, though models trained on human-scale data fail at all meaning evaluations. Turning to training dynamics for a set of open-checkpoint models, we find that Paired-Focus understanding emerges later in training than Paired-Focus syntactic knowledge, and that learning of Paired-Focus semantics is correlated with gains in some domains of world knowledge. Overall, our empirical results support the conclusion that modestly sized open-source models can grasp the rare Paired-Focus constructions, and demonstrate a connection between knowledge of Paired-Focus constructions and other meaning domains.

</details>

### [92] [PhyDrawGen: Physically Grounded Diagram Generation from Natural Language](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30512)
*Nafiul Haque,Syed Nazmus Sakib,Shifat E Arman*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: PhyDrawGen 是一种结合符号求解器与视觉生成模型的神经符号架构，专门用于生成符合物理定律的科学图表，有效解决了现有大模型在物理绘图中常出现的逻辑和几何幻觉问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前通用生成模型在生成物理图表时虽然视觉效果逼真，但常出现违背物理定律、力向量标注错误及几何约束不符等“幻觉”现象，缺乏物理准确性。

Method: 提出了一种神经符号流水线（Neuro-symbolic pipeline）：首先利用大语言模型从文本中提取类型化的场景图；随后通过确定性求解器将图转化为包含物理约束（如力平衡、光路）的平面直线图（PSLG）；最后使用经过微调的 Qwen-VL 模型进行“提出-验证”循环，以修正视觉约束违规。

Result: 在涵盖力学、光学和电磁学的 1,449 个问题基准测试中，PhyDrawGen 显著优于 GPT-5-image、Gemini 2.5 Flash 和 Gemini 3 Pro，展现了极高的物理准确性，即使在处理非典型物体问题时也表现稳健。

Conclusion: PhyDrawGen 通过神经符号架构有效解决了生成物理图表中的“物理幻觉”问题，证明了将逻辑约束求解与生成模型结合是提升科学可视化准确性的关键路径。

Abstract: Generating physics diagrams from text requires strict adherence to physical laws. While current generative models produce visually plausible outputs, they systematically hallucinate force vectors, ignore conservation laws, and violate geometric constraints. We present PhyDrawGen, a neuro-symbolic pipeline that decouples semantic scene understanding from physical constraint satisfaction. First, a large language model extracts a typed scene graph from the problem text. A deterministic solver then converts this graph into a Planar Straight-Line Graph (PSLG), encoding force balance, optical paths, and field topologies as exact geometric primitives. Finally, a fine-tuned Qwen-VL model implements a visually grounded propose-verify loop to iteratively correct any constraint violations. Evaluated on a benchmark of 1,449 problems spanning mechanics, optics, and electromagnetism, PhyDrawGen significantly outperforms GPT-5-image, Gemini 2.5 Flash, and Gemini 3 Pro, demonstrating robust physical accuracy even on unusual-object problems.

</details>


### [93] [Physically Viable World Models: A Case for Query-Conditioned Embodied AI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30542)
*Adam J. Thorpe,Stepan Tretiakov,Cheng-Hsi Hsiao,Su Ann Low,Xingjian Li,Hassan Iqbal,Neel P. Bhatt,Ufuk Topcu,Krishna Kumar*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文指出传统仅基于观测预测的“世界模型”难以处理物理干预，提出了一种以“查询驱动的物理抽象”为核心的模块化设计框架，旨在构建具备物理可行性、可验证且可审计的具身智能世界模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的具身智能世界模型大多专注于预测未来观测，虽然视觉上合理，但在面对实际物理干预时经常失效。其核心问题在于这些模型未能显式建模控制动作结果的底层物理结构，导致其在规划、安全控制及交互预测中表现不佳。因此，作者旨在建立一种能准确响应干预查询的、具有物理可行性的世界模型设计范式。

Method: 1. 揭示了现有仅基于观测预测模型在处理物理干预时的结构性失效问题；2. 提出了“物理可行性”框架，主张通过模块化设计（环境表示、状态参数估计、动力学建模等）来构建模型；3. 引入“查询驱动的抽象”原则，即根据干预查询的需求，动态组合最简且结构上兼容的组件；4. 构建了受控基准测试以验证模型在不同物理潜变量下的表现。

Result: 实验表明，现有的纯观测预测模型在面对视觉一致但物理规律不同的场景时，无法正确预测交互结果并可能导致不安全的操作。研究通过应用所提的模块化和查询抽象方法，有效解决了现有系统在关键干预查询上的失败，证明了该方法在提升模型鲁棒性、可解释性和物理一致性方面的有效性。

Conclusion: 本文提出，具身智能体需要具备能处理干预查询的物理可行世界模型，而非单纯的观测预测。通过采用模块化设计和针对查询选择最简物理抽象，可以构建出更具可解释性、可验证性和鲁棒性的世界模型，这是未来实现可靠具身智能的关键设计原则。

Abstract: World models for embodied AI must be physically viable: constructed to answer intervention queries by representing the physical structure governing action outcomes, rather than merely predicting future observations. Existing observation-predictive world models can produce visually plausible but physically wrong rollouts. This failure is structural; distinct physical systems can look identical yet diverge under intervention. We expose this problem with controlled benchmarks that fix the visible scene while varying latent physics. We show that such models may recommend infeasible actions, mispredict interaction outcomes, or certify unsafe behavior. We argue that embodied AI requires world models that identify the simplest physical abstraction sufficient to answer an intervention query. Such a model comprises modular components, including environment representation, latent state and parameter estimation, action specification, interventional dynamics, and query-level response. An autonomous orchestrator should identify the relevant abstraction and compose compatible learned and structured components per query. When closed-form physics is unavailable, uncertain, or costly, the transition model may be analytic, simulated, learned, or hybrid, but it must preserve the structure that determines interventional outcomes. This decomposition makes the model interpretable, its components verifiable, and its outputs auditable against the query. It also provides a design principle for new world models and a feasibility test for existing ones: the right abstraction is not the most detailed model of the world, but the simplest model that preserves the distinctions relevant to the query. We demonstrate this approach on queries that existing systems fail to answer correctly, and outline how an orchestrator can dynamically assemble and adapt physically viable models for planning, control, and verification.

</details>


### [94] [Transforming and Encoding FTS for SAT Solving: What Helps, What Hurts (Extended Version)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30563)
*João Filipe,Álvaro Torralba,Gregor Behnke*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种将因子化任务（Factored tasks）编码为SAT的新方法，旨在超越现有的启发式搜索局限，通过优化逻辑编码、利用并行性以及结合任务变换，提升规划求解的效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 因子化任务虽然通过引入析取前置条件、条件效应和天使非确定性提供了比STRIPS或SAS+更紧凑的表示方式，但目前针对该类任务的规划方法仅限于启发式搜索。为了寻求更高效的求解手段，作者致力于研究如何将因子化任务映射并编码为SAT规划问题。

Method: 作者提出了多种将因子化任务及其转换关系（Transition relation）编码为命题逻辑（Propositional logic）的SAT编码方案。此外，研究还探索了在该框架下利用不同层级的并行性（Parallelism）的方法，并系统评估了常见的任务预处理变换对SAT求解器性能的具体影响。

Result: 论文通过实验分析了不同SAT编码策略的优劣，明确了通过合理选择编码方式、利用并行性以及应用任务变换，可以显著优化针对因子化任务的SAT求解性能，验证了SAT方法在处理该类紧凑表示任务中的有效性。

Conclusion: 本文的研究表明，通过将因子化任务（Factored tasks）有效编码为SAT问题，可以克服传统启发式搜索在处理该类任务时的局限性。研究强调了不同的逻辑编码策略、并行化手段以及预处理变换对于提升求解效率的重要性，为因子化任务的规划提供了新的、高性能的求解路径。

Abstract: Factored tasks are a classical planning representation that extends SAS+ with limited forms of disjunctive preconditions, conditional effects, and angelic nondeterminism. This allows for a more compact representation of tasks than traditional formalisms such as STRIPS or SAS+, and supports a wide range of task transformations. However, existing planning approaches for factored tasks have been limited to heuristic search methods.
  In this work, we investigate how to encode factored tasks in SAT. We propose several ways to encode the tasks, focusing on different strategies for translating the factored transition relation into propositional logic. We also analyze how to exploit parallelism at various levels in this setting and study the impact of common task transformations on the performance of SAT-based planners.

</details>


### [95] [Procedural Generation of First Person Shooter Maps using Map-Elites](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30570)
*Simone de Donato,Pier Luca Lanzi,Daniele Loiacono*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究通过引入新的地图表示方法和优化度量指标，改进了MAP-Elites算法在FPS游戏关卡生成中的表现，实现了更高质量和多样性的关卡设计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在解决传统FPS游戏关卡生成方法在多样性和质量上的不足，探讨如何通过更好的地图表示法和度量指标来优化MAP-Elites算法的生成能力。

Method: 研究采用MAP-Elites及其变体MAP-Elites with Sliding Boundaries (MESB) 算法，对比了两种已知（全黑、网格图）和两种自创（点线、空间布局）的FPS地图表示方法，并定义了基于拓扑属性和实际游戏性能（涌现属性）的多种度量指标来引导演化过程。

Result: 实验结果显示，所提出的“点线”和“空间布局”表示方法在生成的关卡多样性和质量方面均优于传统表示方法，证明了这些新表示法在FPS关卡设计中的有效性。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，通过引入更具表现力的地图表示方法（点线和空间布局），能够显著提升MAP-Elites算法在FPS游戏关卡生成中的多样性和质量，验证了特征选择对提升生成效果的重要性。

Abstract: We investigate the application of MAP-Elites (a well-known quality diversity algorithm) to design levels for First-Person Shooter (FPS) games. We consider two well-known map representations (All-Black and Grid-Graph) and introduce two novel representations (Point-Line and Spatial-Layout) that improve the characterization of FPS maps. We define a series of metrics to describe maps' topological properties (which solely depend on maps' layout), and emergent properties (which must be evaluated through actual gameplay). We perform an in-depth analysis to identify the most suitable features to guide MAP-Elites illumination process. We apply MAP-Elites with Sliding Boundaries (MESB) to evolve populations of FPS maps. Our results show that the new representations can generate maps with higher diversity and quality than the representations previously used for evolving FPS maps.

### [96] [Harness Updating Is Not Harness Benefit: Disentangling Evolution Capabilities in Self-Evolving LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30621)
*Minhua Lin,Juncheng Wu,Zijun Wang,Zhan Shi,Yisi Sang,Bing He,Zewen Liu,Tianxin Wei,Zongyu Wu,Zhiwei Zhang,Dakuo Wang,Xiang Zhang,Benoit Dumoulin,Cihang Xie,Yuyin Zhou,Suhang Wang,Hanqing Lu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该论文探讨了LLM智能体在“组件自我演化”中的表现，发现生成有效组件更新的能力与模型基础能力无关，而从更新中获益的能力则呈现非单调性（中等模型获益最大）。研究建议应更关注智能体对组件的调用与指令遵循能力的训练。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的LLM智能体广泛依赖提示词、技能、记忆和工具等可编辑外部组件（harnesses）。目前尚不清楚模型的基础任务解决能力是否能预测其在“组件自我演化”中的表现，即：哪些模型能生成有效的更新，以及哪些模型能真正从这些更新中受益。

Method: 该研究通过对比不同规模的LLM模型，分析了其在“组件更新（harness-updating）”和“组件受益（harness-benefit）”两方面的能力。研究评估了模型根据执行证据生成持久化更新的能力，以及模型在利用这些更新后的组件完成任务时的实际表现，并对不同能力层级模型的失败模式进行了归因分析。

Result: 1. 组件更新能力具有平稳性：不同能力层级的模型在生成有效更新方面表现出惊人的相似性，小型模型（如Qwen3.5-9B）的更新效果与大型模型（如Claude Opus）相当。2. 组件受益能力呈现非单调性：中等规模模型从中获益最多，弱模型因无法有效激活或忠实执行组件而受益有限，强模型则因自身能力已达到瓶颈，边际获益相对较低。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，在构建LLM智能体系统时，应将计算资源优先投入到基础智能体的能力提升上，而非专门针对演化器（evolver）进行优化。此外，未来的智能体训练应重点关注“组件调用（harness invocation）”和“长程指令遵循（long-horizon instruction following）”能力的强化。

Abstract: LLM agents are increasingly deployed as systems built around editable external harnesses, including prompts, skills, memories and tools, that shape task execution without changing model parameters. Harness self-evolution adapts such agents by updating these harnesses from execution evidence. Yet it remains unclear whether a model's base capability in task-solving predicts its capabilities in harness self-evolution: which models produce useful harness updates, and which actually benefit from them? We analyze two harness self-evolution capabilities: (i) harness-updating, the capability to produce useful persistent harness updates from execution evidence; (ii) harness-benefit, the capability to benefit from updated harnesses during task solving. Our analysis reveals two findings. First, harness-updating is flat in base capability: models from different capability tiers produce harness updates that lead to surprisingly similar gains; even Qwen3.5-9B's updates yield gains comparable to those of Claude Opus~4.6. Second, harness-benefit is non-monotonic in base capability: weak-tier models benefit little from updated harnesses, mid-tier models benefit most, and strong-tier models benefit less than mid-tier. We trace low gains at the weak tier to two failure modes: weak-tier models may fail to activate relevant harness artifacts, or activate them but fail to follow them faithfully. These findings suggest investing capability budget in the task-solving agent rather than the evolver, and targeting harness invocation and long-horizon instruction following in agent training. Our source code is publicly available at https://github.com/A-EVO-Lab/a-evolve/tree/release/harness-evolution.

</details>


### [97] [EHRBench: An Automated and Reliable EHR-based Benchmark for Clinical Decision Making with LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30637)
*Yuzhang Xie,Keqi Han,Yunpeng Xiao,Hejie Cui,Guanchen Wu,Ziyang Zhang,Kai Shu,Jiaying Lu,Xiao Hu,Carl Yang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对临床决策中大模型可靠性评估不足的问题，本文推出了EHRBench，这是一个基于真实电子病历的大规模自动化基准测试平台，旨在通过严格的质量控制和跨任务评估，明确大模型在临床应用中的真实能力差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大模型在临床决策中的可靠性缺乏系统性评估，现有的医学基准测试难以满足大规模、高质量及基于真实患者电子病历（EHR）的需求。因此，迫切需要一种自动化且可靠的机制来构建大规模临床决策任务基准。

Method: 提出了一种自动且可靠的“EHR-LLM-KB”交互流水线，利用LLM将电子病历（EHR）转化为结构化模板，并通过确定性实例化和知识库（KB）验证机制进行清洗与增强，最终构建了包含约100万个QA项的临床决策基准测试。

Result: 构建了包含近100万个关于诊断、治疗和预后三个核心临床任务的QA项基准，并测试了超过30个主流大模型。结果表明，现有模型在处理临床逻辑推理时仍面临重大挑战，基准测试的性能趋势验证了该评估体系的可靠性。

Conclusion: EHRBench通过大规模、自动化的EHR基准测试揭示了现有大模型在临床决策任务中的能力瓶颈，证实了在实际临床场景中应用大模型仍存在显著的可靠性差距，为未来医疗AI系统的评估与优化提供了可靠的基础。

Abstract: Clinical decision-making (CDM) is central to real-world clinical workflows, where clinicians infer diagnoses, select treatments, or anticipate future health outcomes under incomplete evidence. LLMs are increasingly used to support these decisions due to strong language capabilities, broad biomedical knowledge, and efficiency, yet the reliability of LLMs on real-world clinical decision tasks remains insufficiently understood. To evaluate CDM models, especially LLM-based models, an ideal and practical medical decision benchmark should be constructed via an automated yet reliable pipeline to ensure both scale and quality. Moreover, the grounding of a CDM benchmark in real patient EHRs can better support evaluation on practical CDM tasks that require substantive biomedical knowledge and clinical inference. To fill the gaps, we introduce EHRBench, an automated and reliable EHR-grounded benchmark for evaluating LLM-based clinical decision-making at scale. To ensure scalability and reliability, EHRBench is constructed through an EHR-LLM-KB(knowledge-base) interaction pipeline. For efficiency, we use a specialized LLM to automatically convert encounter-level EHR trajectories into structured templates and deterministically instantiate the templates into QA items. In parallel, we apply systematic KB-based verification and enrichment to filter hallucinated or ambiguous relations and to improve reliability. Using this pipeline, we construct nearly 1M (960,067) QA items spanning three core inference-required clinical decision tasks: diagnosis, treatment, and prognosis. We benchmark more than 30 representative LLMs on EHRBench and provide detailed analyses of performance and robustness. The results show consistent capability trends across settings, further validating the reliability of EHRBench and highlighting actionable gaps toward clinically reliable LLM systems.

</details>


### [98] [Structure-Induced Information for Rerooting Levin Tree Search](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30664)
*Jake Tuero,Michael Buro,Laurent Orseau,Levi H. S. Lelis*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种利用学习型 rerooter 替代显式子目标生成的策略树搜索框架，通过隐式任务分解实现了更低的计算开销和更好的扩展性，在复杂单智能体任务中表现出优异的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的基于子目标的策略树搜索（subgoal-based policy tree search）在处理复杂确定性任务时虽然有效，但往往依赖于显式的子目标生成，这带来了巨大的计算开销并限制了算法在大规模问题上的扩展性。本文旨在通过学习型的隐式分解机制来克服这些局限性。

Method: 本文引入了基于 $\sqrt{\text{LTS}}$ 算法的学习型“重路由（rerooter）”机制，通过隐式方式将问题分解为软子任务。作者提出了三种具体设计方案：1. 基于聚类的 rerooter，利用全局状态空间结构；2. 基于启发式的 rerooter，利用学习到的剩余代价估计（cost-to-go）；3. 结合两者的混合型 rerooter。该框架通过直接引导搜索避免了显式生成和推理子目标的计算负担。

Result: 实验结果表明，该方法在复杂环境中不仅能够实现比传统子目标搜索方法更好的扩展性，还在多个测试领域中实现了业界领先的在线训练效率，显著降低了计算开销。

Conclusion: 本文提出的基于 rerooter 的学习方法成功解决了传统子目标生成开销大及可扩展性差的问题，证明了隐式任务分解在提升搜索效率和算法可扩展性方面的优势。该框架为复杂单智能体确定性环境中的策略树搜索提供了新的高效路径。

Abstract: Subgoal-based policy tree search, which uses a policy to guide search, is effective for complex single-agent deterministic problems but often relies on explicit subgoal generation that can incur substantial overhead and hinders scalability. In this paper, we overcome these limitations by using a learned ``rerooter'' through the recently-introduced $\sqrt{\text{LTS}}$ algorithm. A rerooter implicitly decomposes the problem into soft subtasks. While previous work focused on the formal guarantees for given or handcrafted rerooters, in this work we propose three rerooter designs: (i) a clustering-based rerooter that exploits global state-space structure, (ii) a heuristic-based rerooter that leverages learned cost-to-go estimates, and (iii) a hybrid that combines both signals. Our framework avoids having to explicitly reconstruct and reason over generated subgoals, thereby enabling scalable allocation of search effort with significantly lower computational overhead. Empirically, our rerooting-based methods scale to complex environments where subgoal-based policy tree search fails, and achieve state-of-the-art online training efficiency on the domains tested.

</details>


### [99] [Healthcare Mechanisms from Policy-as-Code Search under Strategic Provider Response](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30680)
*Zihan Wang,Xiang Xu,Hongyuan Zha,Wenhao Li*

Main category: cs.AI

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究提出了一种基于大语言模型（LLM）的程序合成方法。利用 Medi-Sim 多智能体模拟器，模拟了医疗服务提供者在五种策略渠道（编码、选择、延迟、努力、分诊）下的行为。研究通过激励扫描（Incentive Sweep）重现了医疗经济学中的经典现象，并使用 LLM 指导的进化代码搜索，合成出可检查的混合目标策略程序。

Result: 通过进化代码搜索合成出的机制程序成功消除了升级编码（Up-coding）行为，将患者拒绝率降低了一半，同时保留了大部分基于利润的基准方案的资金水平。实验还发现，仅仅关闭编码渠道会导致低复杂度患者的选择率增加一倍以上，揭示了机制设计中存在的“压力迁移”现象。

Conclusion: 研究表明，将医疗机构机制设计重构为大语言模型的程序合成是可行的。通过这种方法合成的可解释性程序，能够在维持经济效益的同时，显著减少医疗欺诈行为（如升级编码）并优化资源分配效率，为设计更具鲁棒性的医疗支付系统提供了新视角。

Abstract: Healthcare mechanisms are inseparable from the strategic provider response they induce: existing healthcare AI benchmarks hold this response fixed and so cannot evaluate mechanisms by the equilibrium they produce. We recast hospital mechanism design as program synthesis for language models: typed, inspectable rule programs are executed and scored by Medi-Sim, a multi-agent simulator with five strategic provider channels (coding, selection, delay, effort, triage). An incentive sweep recovers classical health-economics findings as adjacent regimes -- up-coding and low-complexity-patient selection under profit pressure, and Goodhart-style drift where measured performance becomes anti-correlated with true outcomes -- and a single audit lever exposes pressure migration: closing the coding channel more than doubles low-complexity selection. LLM-guided evolutionary code search over the same rule-program space then synthesizes an inspectable mixed-objective program that eliminates up-coding, halves rejection, and retains most of the profit-oriented baseline's funds.

### [100] [Generating Graph-like Rules for Knowledge Graph Reasoning via Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30747)
*Haoxiang Cheng,Yunfei Wang,Chao Chen,Kewei Cheng,Zhipeng Lin,Haoxuan Li,Changjun Fan,Shixuan Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了GRiD框架，利用生成式建模与强化学习挖掘复杂的图结构知识图谱规则，有效解决了规则挖掘中的搜索空间爆炸与指标不可微优化难题，提升了知识图谱补全的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有规则挖掘方法多局限于简单的链式规则，忽视了更具表达力的图结构规则（如环和分支）。此外，图结构带来的组合爆炸导致搜索空间巨大，且扩散模型等生成式方法因目标函数不匹配及规则质量指标不可微等问题难以直接应用。

Method: 提出了一种名为GRiD的框架，将图结构规则挖掘重构为条件离散生成过程。该方法包含两个阶段：首先通过监督预训练学习知识图谱元图中的结构先验；随后利用强化学习（策略梯度优化），直接根据不可微的规则质量指标对模型进行微调，从而克服了不可微指标无法引导模型优化的难题。

Result: 在六个基准数据集上的实验结果表明，GRiD在知识图谱补全任务中表现出极强的竞争力。消融实验证实了GRiD的高效性和鲁棒性，并进一步证明了图结构规则能够有效弥补链式规则的不足。

Conclusion: 图结构规则（如环状和分支结构）是提升知识图谱推理能力的有效手段。GRiD框架通过将规则挖掘转化为离散生成过程，成功突破了传统方法在处理复杂规则时的计算瓶颈，证明了图结构规则对链式规则的有效补充作用。

Abstract: Logical rules constitute a cornerstone of knowledge graph (KG) reasoning, valued for their interpretability and ability to model relational patterns. However, existing rule mining methods predominantly focus on simple chain-like rules and therefore neglect the richer relational information encoded in graph-like structures, such as cycles and branches. This limitation is further exacerbated by computational bottlenecks caused by the combinatorial explosion of the search space, which is especially challenging for graph-like rules. Meanwhile, generative approaches such as diffusion models, despite their success in other domains, can not be directly applied to rule mining because their training objectives are not aligned with the goal of learning high-quality rules, and non-differentiable KG rule quality metrics cannot directly guide model optimization. To address these limitations, we propose GRiD, a framework that reformulates graph-like rule discovery as a discrete generative process conditioned on the target relation. GRiD employs a two-phase training strategy. First, supervised pre-training enables GRiD to capture structural priors from subgraphs sampled from the KG meta-graph. Subsequently, reinforcement learning is applied to fine-tune GRiD through policy gradient optimization guided directly by non-differentiable rule-quality metrics. Experiments on six benchmark datasets show that GRiD achieves competitive performance on KG completion tasks. Ablation studies confirm the efficiency and robustness of GRiD and further show that graph-like rules complement chain-like rules in KG completion. Our codes and datasets are available in https://github.com/Haoxiang-Cheng/GRiD

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 引入 AdaCoM 框架，训练一个外部 LLM 作为“上下文管理器”，通过强化学习（RL）策略指导，对冻结的原始智能体（Agent）的上下文进行动态修改（如剪枝、总结等），无需对原始智能体进行重新训练。

Conclusion: AdaCoM 提出了一种通过外部智能体管理上下文的有效方案，揭示了智能体性能与上下文保留策略之间的权衡（保真度与可靠性），并证明了该方法在不同智能体间的可迁移性。

Abstract: LLM agents increasingly face long-horizon tasks such as web search and deep research in real-world applications, where accumulated context can cause long-context degradation and reasoning failures. Prior work mitigates this through context management with agent-side context control or fixed strategies such as summarization, which require training the agent itself for adaptation - making it impractical for closed-source agents and ignoring that different agents may require different strategies. We introduce Adaptive Context Management (AdaCoM), which trains an external LLM to manage the context of a frozen agent through flexible modification actions and end-to-end reinforcement learning. Across diverse agents on web search and deep research benchmarks, AdaCoM substantially improves performance by preserving task constraints and progress while pruning stale content. The learned strategies reveal a Fidelity-Reliability Trade-off: agents with higher vanilla ReAct performance benefit from higher-fidelity context preservation, whereas lower-performing agents require more aggressive compression to stay within a reliable reasoning regime. Transfer experiments show that AdaCoM generalizes most effectively across agents with similar capability (measured by vanilla ReAct performance), suggesting a practical path toward reusable context managers for agent systems.

### [102] [Vector Linking via Cross-Model Local Isometric Consistency](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31100)
*Ziying Chen,Yang Cao,He Sun,Beining Yang,Tianjian Yang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究提出了“矢量链接”（Vector Linking）框架，利用嵌入空间中局部距离的几何一致性，通过少量的配对锚点引导，实现了不同黑盒模型间嵌入向量的自动对齐与匹配。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在不同黑盒编码器生成的嵌入空间中，由于训练数据重叠有限且模型架构不同，直接进行跨模型对象匹配十分困难。研究旨在解决如何在没有原始数据、仅依赖嵌入向量的情况下，实现不同模型间对象对应关系的自动恢复。

Method: 提出了一种基于参考点的迭代几何嵌入哈希（Reference-based Geometric Embedding Hashing）方法。该方法：1. 利用少量已知的配对锚点（anchors）作为参考；2. 将向量表示为到锚点的距离向量；3. 通过哈希空间匹配生成候选链接；4. 采用Beta-Bernoulli后验概率模型聚合证据，逐步引导（bootstrap）并增加高置信度链接。

Result: 实验表明，该方法在多种基准测试和不同模型对之间表现出色，即使在数据集重叠度较低、种子锚点极少或存在域外数据的情况下，仍能保持高准确率和鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了独立训练的对比学习编码器之间存在“局部几何一致性”，并提出了一种高效、鲁棒的矢量链接方法。该方案证明了仅利用矢量信息即可在不同模型之间实现跨域数据对齐，为异构嵌入数据库的集成和跨模型聚类提供了通用解决方案。

Abstract: We study Vector Linking: given two embedding clouds produced by different black-box encoders over partially overlapping datasets, recover cross-model object correspondences using only vectors. Empirically and theoretically, we show that independently trained contrastive encoders exhibit local geometric consistency: short-range distances are approximately preserved up to a scale factor, while long-range distances are not due to model-specific distortion. Building on this, we propose an iterative, reference-based geometric embedding hashing that recovers vector links from a tiny seed set of paired anchors. It represents each vector by distances to sampled paired anchors, proposes candidate links via hash-space matching, and aggregates evidence across views in a Beta-Bernoulli posterior to bootstrap high-confidence links as new anchors. Experiments across multiple benchmarks and embedding model pairs demonstrate accurate and robust linking under varying overlap, seed budgets, and out-of-domain anchors, with applications to vector database integration and cross-model clustering. Code is available at https://github.com/DBgroup-Edinburgh/VecLinking.

### [103] [PReMISE: Policy Rubrics as Measurement Specifications for LLM Judges](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30803)
*Swastik Roy,Rajkumar Pujari,Tharindu Kumarage,Charith Peris,Rahul Gupta,Anna Rumshisky,Pradeep Natarajan,Venkatesh Saligrama*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对LLM作为评判员时评分标准模糊导致评估失效的问题，本文提出了PReMISE框架。该框架能够自动发现并审计评分标准，通过针对性的修复手段，有效提升了LLM评测的准确性、鲁棒性及对人类偏好的对齐能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前利用大语言模型（LLM）作为评判员来评估开放式回答已成为主流，但其评分结果深受评分标准的影响。模糊或不科学的评分标准会导致LLM偏好于看起来“像样”但事实错误或偏离用户意图的回答。因此，研究旨在系统性地评估、优化和发现能准确反映人类偏好的评分标准。

Method: 研究提出了PReMISE框架，主要包含两个核心流程：首先，基于成对人类偏好数据，通过算法自动发现策略级的评分标准集；其次，从结构充分性、可靠性、偏好拟合度和对抗鲁棒性四个维度对评分标准进行审计。此外，该研究还引入了“偏好排序选择”和“可靠性约束精炼”两种修复操作，以优化现有的评分标准。

Result: PReMISE框架在多个评估维度上表现优异，优于现有的评分源。具体而言，应用“偏好排序选择”操作后，LLM判定的准确率从65.0%提升至68.6%；应用“可靠性约束精炼”后，易受攻击的回答获得高分的比例从46.4%降低至36.0%，且在保持了相近的一致性水平下显著提升了防御能力。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，LLM作为评判员的评估质量高度依赖于评分标准（rubric）。通过PReMISE框架，研究证明了通过系统性地审计和修复评分标准，可以显著提高LLM判定的准确性、可靠性和对抗鲁棒性，为建立更可信的自动化评估体系提供了有效路径。

Abstract: LLM judges are increasingly used to evaluate open-ended responses, but their scores depend strongly on the rubrics that condition them. A vague rubric asking for a response to be ``helpful and factual'' can reward polished answers that invent facts or violate user intent. We treat reusable rubrics as measurement specifications: changing the rubric changes the response quality measurement induced by a fixed judge. We introduce PReMISE, a framework that, given pairwise human-preference data, (i) discovers a policy-level rubric set, and (ii) audits any rubric set under LLM-judge use along four axes: structural adequacy, reliability, preference fit, and adversarial robustness. Across rubric sources no raw source is simultaneously reliable, preference-predictive, and adversarially robust; and high inter-rater agreement does not imply low exploitability. PReMISE is the only rubric source to score non-trivially on applicability, specificity, and effective dimensionality simultaneously. We contribute two audit-targeted repair operations: preference-rank selection raises judge accuracy on paired responses from $65.0\%$ to $68.6\%$, competitive with the strongest rubric-discovery baselines and leading on two of three judges in our cross-judge sweep; reliability-constrained refinement reduces the rate at which exploit responses receive high scores from $46.4\%$ to $36.0\%$ with little change in inter-judge agreement ($α{=}.531\to.519$).

</details>


### [104] [Planner-Centric Reinforcement Learning for Deep Research with Structure-Aware Reward](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30824)
*Mustafa Anis Hussain,Xinle Wu,Yao Lu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: DecomposeR 是一种新型的深度研究框架，它将复杂研究任务拆解为有向无环图（DAG），通过显式的两阶段强化学习训练规划器和回答器，有效解决了长任务中规划与执行难以协调的难题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的 LLM 研究任务训练范式过度依赖短文本问答或单一的长轨迹优化，导致规划与执行难以拆解，且对规划过程的信用分配（credit assignment）较弱，限制了模型处理复杂、深度的多分支研究任务的能力。

Method: 提出 DecomposeR 框架，将研究计划表示为类型化的有向无环图（DAG），并采用两阶段强化学习训练策略：第一阶段训练规划器优化图结构与查询分解，第二阶段训练回答器完成分支执行与最终合成，通过对规划 token 进行显式奖励来实现细粒度的优化。

Result: 实验结果表明，DecomposeR-8B 在多个长文本研究基准测试中，相较于同量级的开源强基准模型，性能提升了 5.1 至 8.0 个百分点，显著增强了模型的规划与回答能力。

Conclusion: DecomposeR 通过引入以规划器为中心的显式图结构建模，有效地解决了长周期研究任务中规划与执行耦合度高、信用分配困难的问题，为提升大模型复杂长文本的研究与合成能力提供了高效的范式。

Abstract: Deep research tasks require LLMs to plan what to investigate, retrieve evidence, and synthesize long-form answers across multiple branches of inquiry. Existing training paradigms either rely on short-form verifiable QA as a proxy or optimize monolithic long trajectories, which makes planning and execution difficult to disentangle and yields weak credit assignment for the planning process. We propose DecomposeR, a planner-centric deep research framework that represents research plans as typed directed acyclic graphs (DAGs), allowing planning to be made explicit, structured, and rewardable. We train a Qwen3-8B model in two stages: planner reinforcement learning (RL) first learns graph structure and query decomposition to improve research planning, and answerer reinforcement learning (RL) then learns branch-level execution and final synthesis conditioned on the learned plan. By assigning rewards to explicit planner tokens and structured components rather than to a flat trajectory, DecomposeR enables finer-grained optimization of planning while reducing the ambiguity of end-to-end training. Experiments show that DecomposeR-8B improves over strong comparable open baselines by 5.1-8.0 points on popular long-form benchmarks due to improved planning and answering capabilities.

### [105] [SLAT: Segment-Level Adaptive Trimming for Efficient CoT Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30832)
*Jian Yao,Xiongcai Luo,Ran Cheng,Kay Chen Tan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对大模型推理过程中的“过度思考”问题，研究提出了SLAT框架，通过识别并抑制边际效用低的冗余推理片段，在大幅提升推理效率的同时保持了模型的准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前基于强化学习的思维链（CoT）模型普遍存在“过度思考（overthinking）”的结构性冗余问题，导致计算开销过大；而现有的惩罚机制过于粗糙，容易误删有价值的推理步骤。因此，研究旨在寻找一种更精细、更具针对性的策略来消除推理冗余。

Method: 提出了SLAT（段落级自适应裁剪）框架。该方法首先通过理论推导定义了“正确性-长度权衡”目标下的片段次优性指标，识别出高概率但边际效用低的冗余推理片段；随后在强化学习框架下，针对这些特定片段进行选择性抑制，而非盲目地对整体输出施加统一的长度惩罚。

Result: 实验表明，SLAT在保持竞争性准确率的同时，将推理长度减少了50%，在标准测试集上实现了更优的准确性与效率的帕累托前沿（Pareto frontier）。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，基于理论支撑的段落级自适应裁剪是提升大模型思维链推理效率的有效途径。通过关注边缘效用低的推理片段，可以在维持准确性的前提下显著降低计算冗余，为高效推理模型的设计提供了新的范式。

Abstract: Recent advances in Large Reasoning Models have significantly improved chain-of-thought (CoT) capabilities via reinforcement learning (RL). However, generated reasoning chains frequently suffer from structural redundancy (i.e., \emph{overthinking}), incurring high computational overhead without improving answer correctness. Existing mitigation strategies typically rely on token-uniform length penalties, which provide coarse, segment-agnostic pressure toward shorter outputs and can inadvertently suppress useful reasoning alongside redundancy. To address this, we demonstrate that inefficiency concentrates in high-probability segments with low marginal utility. We derive a theoretical characterization of segment suboptimality under the correctness-length trade-off objective and propose \textsc{SLAT} (Segment-Level Adaptive Trimming), an RL framework that selectively suppresses redundant segments based on this criterion. Empirical results on standard benchmarks indicate that \textsc{SLAT} establishes a superior accuracy-efficiency Pareto frontier, reducing reasoning length by $50\%$ relative to uncompressed baselines while maintaining competitive accuracy. Overall, our results suggest that theoretically grounded, segment-aware trimming is a promising direction for efficient CoT reasoning in large language models.

</details>


### [106] [Distilling LLM Feedback for Lean Theorem Proving](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30861)
*Gaetan Narozniak,Gérard Biau,Rémi Munos,Ahmad Rammal,Pierre Marion*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对推理模型训练中强化学习存在的奖励稀疏和模式崩溃问题，本文提出“反馈蒸馏”方法，通过Token级别的特权反馈提供细粒度监督，在保持模型多样性的同时显著提升了推理能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的推理模型训练通常结合监督微调与强化学习（如GRPO），但这些方法面临奖励信号稀疏、探索能力有限以及模式崩溃（mode collapse）等挑战。作者旨在通过引入Token级别的反馈机制，解决上述问题并优化推理模型的训练。

Method: 提出了一种名为“反馈蒸馏”的训练方法。该方法不再单纯依赖强化学习的稀疏奖励，而是通过利用由语言模型提供的“特权反馈”（privileged feedback），在Token级别引导模型模仿其目标分布，从而实现对生成过程的细粒度监督。此外，该方法可与GRPO结合，通过使用反馈蒸馏检查点初始化GRPO来进一步提升效果。

Result: 在Lean4定理证明任务中，反馈蒸馏相比GRPO保持了更高的生成轨迹多样性，拥有更高的策略熵，并展现出更好的pass@k扩展能力。实验证明，反馈蒸馏与GRPO具有互补性，两者的组合使用效果优于单一方法。

Conclusion: 反馈蒸馏（Feedback Distillation）为复杂推理任务的训练提供了一个高效且可互补的新范式，尤其在处理稀疏奖励环境时，与GRPO结合使用可显著提升模型性能。

Abstract: Post-training for reasoning models typically combines supervised fine-tuning with reinforcement learning from verifiable rewards, most commonly with GRPO. However, this algorithm suffers from sparse rewards, limited exploration, and mode collapse. Building upon recent works on self-distillation, we propose Feedback Distillation, a training method where the model is trained to match, at the token level, its own distribution conditioned on privileged feedback produced by a language model. Feedback Distillation offers token-level supervision and can inject external knowledge. Evaluating our method for Lean4 theorem-proving, we find that Feedback Distillation maintains greater diversity in generated trajectories than GRPO, yielding higher policy entropy and better pass@k scaling. The two methods are complementary: initializing GRPO from a Feedback Distillation checkpoint outperforms either method alone. All in all, our results suggest a promising avenue to improve post-training for complex reasoning.

### [107] [UniScale: Adaptive Unified Inference Scaling via Online Joint Optimization of Model Routing and Test-Time Scaling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30898)
*Kaiyu Huang,Xingyu Wang,Mingze Kong,Zhubo Shi,Yuqian Hou,Hong Xu,Zhongxiang Dai,Minchen Yu,Qingjiang Shi*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了 UniScale 框架，通过结合模型路由与测试时扩展（TTS），利用上下文多臂赌博机技术实现大模型推理的最优质量-成本平衡，解决了传统解耦方法带来的性能瓶颈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的模型路由（不同规模模型切换）和测试时扩展（单模型内增加推理计算）通常是解耦的，导致路由粒度过粗或单模型性能受限。作者旨在通过统一这两个机制，解决大模型在实际部署中推理质量与计算成本之间的权衡难题。

Method: 本文提出了统一推理扩展（UIS）架构，将模型路由与测试时扩展整合到一个统一的优化空间。在此基础上，开发了 UniScale 在线框架，将适应性 UIS 问题建模为上下文多臂赌博机（Contextual Multi-Armed Bandit）问题，并利用 LinUCB 算法学习推理策略，同时结合了效率感知学习和成本建模技术。

Result: 实验结果表明，UniScale 能够充分利用 UIS 空间内的协同效应，在各种动态推理场景下，比单一优化方法提供了更细粒度且始终更优的质量-成本权衡。

Conclusion: UniScale 框架通过将模型路由与测试时扩展（TTS）统一优化，证明了这种整合能有效突破单一维度优化的瓶颈，为在动态环境下实现更细粒度、更具性价比的大模型推理提供了有效途径。

Abstract: In real-world deployments of large language models (LLMs), balancing inference quality and computational cost has become a central challenge. Existing approaches tackle this trade-off along two largely independent dimensions: model routing, which switches among models of different scales to match request complexity, and test-time scaling (TTS), which adjusts inference-time compute within a fixed model for fine-grained control. However, this decoupled design introduces inherent limitations. Model routing yields coarse-grained, discrete performance changes due to the sparse set of model scales, while single-model TTS often encounters capacity ceilings and exhibits diminishing returns as compute increases. Moreover, treating the two mechanisms separately restricts adaptability in dynamic inference environments. To overcome these limitations, we introduce Unified Inference Scaling (UIS), which unifies model routing and TTS in a single optimization space. Building on this formulation, we propose UniScale, an online framework that models adaptive UIS as a contextual multi-armed bandit problem and learns inference policies via LinUCB. The framework incorporates efficiency-aware learning and cost modeling to ensure stable and scalable optimization over high-dimensional action spaces. Evaluation shows that UniScale effectively exploits the synergy in the UIS space to deliver a fine-grained and consistently better quality-cost trade-off across diverse, dynamic inference scenarios.

</details>


### [108] [BilliardPhys-Bench: Benchmarking Physical Reasoning and Visual Dynamics of Multimodal LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30900)

Method: 作者提出了BilliardPhys-Bench基准测试，利用程序化引擎生成包含摩擦力和弹性碰撞的随机台球场景，重点评估模型在球体碰撞预测、墙壁反弹推理及运动停止后最终位置估计这三项能力上的表现。研究对来自GPT、Claude、Gemini和Qwen系列的主流多模态大模型进行了详细的基准测试。

Result: 实验结果显示，随着模拟时间延长和场景几何复杂度的增加，所有模型的性能均出现明显下滑。研究发现了一种普遍的失效模式——“静止偏差”（stasis bias），即当物理结果难以推断时，模型倾向于错误地预测物体不发生任何交互。

Conclusion: 现有的多模态大模型在处理视觉动态推理方面存在显著局限性，尤其是面对需要物理直觉的复杂场景时表现乏力。研究强调，未来的多模态架构必须引入更强的物理归纳偏置，以解决“静止偏差”等根本性缺陷，从而提升对现实世界物理交互的理解能力。

Abstract: Current multimodal models handle static image recognition well, but intuitive physical reasoning remains a weakness. Predicting how objects will move and interact from a single image is still difficult for these systems. We present BilliardPhys-Bench, a benchmark for physical reasoning in synthetic billiards environments. Its procedural engine generates randomized scenarios with friction and elastic collisions. The benchmark tests three abilities: (1) predicting ball-to-ball collisions, (2) reasoning about wall bounces, and (3) estimating final ball positions after motion stops. We evaluate recent MLLMs from the GPT, Claude, Gemini, and Qwen families. Performance drops as simulation time increases and scene geometry grows more complex. We also observe a consistent failure mode we call "stasis bias": when the correct physical outcome is harder to infer, models tend to predict no interaction. These findings show where current MLLMs break down on visual dynamics and point toward the need for better physical inductive biases in multimodal architectures.

We show that modern generative architectures can instantiate and maintain these evaluative personas with high consistency, enabling a form of pluralistic, perspective-dependent benchmarking that more closely reflects real-world consensus variability. However, we further analyze the stability of these simulated evaluators under sequential inference and stochastic prompt perturbations, revealing systematic degradation in persona coherence that manifests as state-space drift and semantic inconsistency. These findings suggest that static alignment constraints are insufficient for sustaining robust evaluative behavior over time. Instead, we argue for the necessity of embedding dynamic, viability-driven regulatory mechanisms within generative systems to preserve coherent cognitive emulation. By framing persona-based evaluation as a structured dynamical system over latent representation manifolds, this study provides a foundation for more adaptive, human-aligned, and context-sensitive approaches to AI evaluation.

Traditional scheduling approaches typically rely on mathematical models to represent satellite mission and resource management. Then, this problem is solved by using optimization algorithms. However, such solutions become less effective when the underlying models are not available, over complex, and inaccurate due to dynamic changes and uncertainties inherent in the space mission environment. A promising alternative is to reformulate the problem as a sequential decision-making process and apply model-free reinforcement learning techniques to enable adaptive and real-time resource management. To this end, we propose a novel transformer-based architecture tailored for heterogeneous satellite cluster autonomous EO Mission with relational observations-actions tokenization and differential attention mechanism. Our experimental results demonstrate significant performance improvements compared to the available baselines. ### [111] [GraphARC: A Comprehensive Benchmark for Graph-Based Abstract Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31031)
*Saku Peltonen,August Bøgh Rønberg,Andreas Plesner,Roger Wattenhofer*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: GraphARC 是一个全新的图结构数据抽象推理基准，通过少样本图转换任务评估模型的泛化能力，研究发现当前大语言模型在执行复杂图转换时存在明显短板和扩展性问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的抽象推理基准（如 ARC）多局限于网格或文本格式，缺乏对图结构数据的专门评估。为了填补这一空白并更好地测试模型的图推理能力，研究人员开发了 GraphARC，旨在系统地评估模型在图转换任务中的泛化能力，并推动图基础模型的发展。

Method: 提出了 GraphARC 基准测试，该方法基于少样本转换学习范式（借鉴了 ARC 的思想），要求模型从少量输入-输出对中归纳出图转换规则，并将其应用于新的测试图。该框架涵盖了局部、全局和分层图转换，支持在大规模多样的图族和规模上进行生成和评估。

Result: 研究发现，先进的大语言模型虽然能回答有关图属性的问题，但在执行完整的图转换任务时表现较差，存在明显的“理解-执行差距”；同时，随着图规模的扩大，模型性能显著下降，表明当前模型在处理复杂图结构推理时存在扩展性瓶颈。

Conclusion: GraphARC 提供了一个评估图结构数据上抽象推理能力的新框架，揭示了当前大语言模型在处理复杂图转换任务时的局限性，并为未来图基础模型的研究提供了重要的基准和测试平台。

Abstract: Relational reasoning lies at the heart of intelligence, but existing benchmarks are typically confined to formats such as grids or text. We introduce GraphARC, a benchmark for abstract reasoning on graph-structured data. GraphARC generalizes the few-shot transformation learning paradigm of the Abstraction and Reasoning Corpus (ARC). Each task requires inferring a transformation rule from a few input-output pairs and applying it to a new test graph, covering local, global, and hierarchical graph transformations. Unlike grid-based ARC, GraphARC instances can be generated at scale across diverse graph families and sizes, enabling systematic evaluation of generalization abilities. We evaluate state-of-the-art language models on GraphARC and observe clear limitations. Models can answer questions about graph properties but often fail to solve the full graph transformation task, revealing a comprehension-execution gap. Performance further degrades on larger instances, exposing scaling barriers. More broadly, by combining aspects of node classification, link prediction, and graph generation within a single framework, GraphARC provides a promising testbed for future graph foundation models.

### [112] [LLM-FACETS: A Privacy-Preserving Framework for Evaluating LLM Transparency and Accountability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31167)
*Tom Lucas,Alessio Buscemi,Alfredo Capozucca,German Castignani,Barbara Delacroix*

Main category: cs.AI

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大型语言模型（LLM）的审计过程对非技术从业者不友好，存在极高的编程与环境配置门槛。此外，现有的云端评估平台存在数据隐私外泄风险，且缺乏针对 AI 合规性（如欧盟 AI 法案及 NIST 标准）的系统化评估框架，导致 AI 监管与开发团队难以实现有效的职能解耦。

Method: 1. 架构设计：采用插件化架构，支持轻松扩展新指标和数据集。2. 隐私与数据安全：实现自托管运行，确定性指标（如 BLEU, ROUGE）无需数据外传，外部模型 API 调用由用户完全控制凭证。3. 三维评估机制：引入代币级对数概率可视化（衡量不确定性）、多裁判共识（减少偏见）和 RAG 三元组指标（检测幻觉）。4. 用户适配：设计三种针对性界面，分别满足技术专家、领域专家和合规官的需求。5. 验证：通过与 18 种 canonical 参考库的对比进行交叉验证。

Result: 成功开发了 LLM-FACETS 框架。该框架实现了在保证数据安全的前提下，对 LLM 输出进行事实性、认知校准和方法论可重现性的自动化评估。通过 18 个指标的交叉验证，证明了系统的准确性和可靠性，填补了合规人员与 AI 技术评估之间的鸿沟。

Conclusion: LLM-FACETS 通过提供一个开源、自托管且模块化的评估框架，有效地降低了 LLM 审计的技术门槛。它通过明确的数据流控制、多维度指标和针对不同利益相关者的角色设计，为 AI 系统实现透明度、可信度和合规性评估提供了一个实用的解决方案，有助于将 AI 审计权从开发团队中解耦。

Abstract: Assessing whether Large Language Models outputs are factually grounded, epistemically calibrated, and methodologically reproducible is a prerequisite for responsible AI deployment. Yet auditing LLMs remains inaccessible to non-technical practitioners: existing tools require programming expertise and non-trivial environment setup, and cloud-hosted platforms transmit evaluation data to external services, creating barriers for domain experts and compliance officers legally responsible for AI oversight. We introduce LLM-FACETS (LLM FActuality Cross-EvaluaTion System): an open-source framework with a browser-accessible interface and a plugin architecture, structured around three practitioner profiles (technical experts, domain experts, compliance officers) that mirror the stakeholder categories identified in the EU AI Act and the NIST AI Risk Management Framework. The architecture makes data flows explicit: deterministic metrics (BLEU, ROUGE, BERTScore) run entirely within the self-hosted server with no outbound transmission; LLM-judge metrics contact external APIs explicitly, with users retaining full credential control. The framework operationalizes transparency through three mechanisms: token-level log-probability visualization for epistemic uncertainty, multi-judge consensus to mitigate judge bias, and RAG Triad metrics (Faithfulness, Answer Relevance, Context Relevance) to detect and localize hallucinations. A plugin architecture allows any new metric or dataset to be integrated without modifying the evaluation pipeline. The open-source implementation enables cross-checking across multiple metrics targeting the same property, ensuring reproducibility and decoupling AI accountability from the teams building the systems assessed. We verify the framework through cross-validation of 18 metric implementations against canonical reference libraries.

### [113] [Formalizing and falsifying causal pathways of rare events](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31254)
*Anahita Haghighat,Dominik Janzing*

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种针对结构方程模型中“罕见事件”的因果路径定义与抽象方法，通过简化模型结构，使得分析复杂系统的因果机制变得既严谨又易于理解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在解决现有因果模型中对于罕见事件（异常值）缺乏形式化路径定义的问题，并弥合口头因果解释与严谨因果建模之间的鸿沟，从而更高效地分析复杂系统中的异常成因。

Method: 基于结构方程模型中针对罕见事件（异常值）的根本原因分析理论，定义了因果路径的形式化框架，并识别了在何种条件下，因果影响的统计特征仅取决于由罕见事件定义的因果抽象，而非依赖于整个底层系统的因果图。

Result: 成功构建了罕见事件的因果路径抽象框架，证明了在特定条件下，只需利用因果路径抽象即可推断其可检验的统计蕴涵，简化了对大型复杂系统因果关系的分析过程。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一种针对罕见事件（异常值）的因果路径形式化定义及因果抽象方法，成功在简洁的语言逻辑解释与复杂的因果模型之间建立了桥梁，为理解和分析结构方程模型中的罕见事件机制提供了理论支撑。

Abstract: Building on recent formalizations of root cause analysis for rare events (``outliers'') in structural equation models, we propose a formal definition of a causal pathway and discuss its testable implications. We identify conditions under which these implications depend only on a causal abstraction defined by the pathway of rare events, rather than on the full causal graph of the underlying system. Accordingly, we introduce an abstraction of causal structure to pathways of rare events that bridges simple verbal causal explanations and detailed causal modeling.

</details>


### [114] [TraceGraph: Shared Decision Landscapes for Diagnosing and Improving Agent Trajectories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31308)
*Junjie Nian,Kang Chen,Ge Zhang,Yixin Cao,Yugang Jiang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: TraceGraph 是一个通过构建图模型来可视化和分析智能体交互轨迹的框架，它不仅能发现传统评分无法揭示的失败模式，还能利用识别出的“陷阱区域”引导智能体进行有效恢复，从而提升整体成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的智能体基准评估过度依赖通过率或奖励得分，忽略了轨迹中丰富的交互过程，无法揭示模型失败的深层原因及导航模式差异。

Method: 构建了 TraceGraph 框架，将多模型智能体的交互轨迹转化为基于状态的图形景观；通过在图中叠加“生产核心”和“陷阱区域”，利用“访问”、“陷阱暴露”和“修复”三个关键事件总结轨迹；并基于此开发了针对 SWE-bench 的陷阱感知恢复流水线。

Result: TraceGraph 揭示了不同基准测试在奖励回避陷阱与奖励从陷阱中恢复方面的侧重差异；在 SWE-bench 上，应用陷阱感知恢复策略后，官方解决率从 40.4% 提升至 43.5%，验证了该方法在提升智能体鲁棒性方面的有效性。

Conclusion: TraceGraph 为评估智能体提供了一种新的过程分析词汇，揭示了基准测试中隐藏的导航差异，并证明了基于“陷阱感知”的恢复机制能有效提升智能体的执行成功率。

Abstract: Agent benchmarks increasingly record rich interaction trajectories, yet evaluation often reduces each rollout to a pass rate or reward score. We introduce TraceGraph, a graph-based framework that turns released multi-model agent trajectories into shared decision landscapes. For each task, TraceGraph builds a graph over observable action-observation states from pooled rollouts before model identity is introduced. It then overlays outcome-informed productive cores and trap regions, and summarizes each rollout with three events: Access, Trap exposure, and Repair. Across trajectories spanning five benchmark splits, TraceGraph profiles reveal navigation differences hidden by aggregate scores and show that splits differ in whether they reward avoiding traps or recovering from them. The same TraceGraph landscape also motivates a trap-aware recovery pipeline for SWE-bench: aruntime detector fires on states matching historical trap regions, then lightweight continuation policies are evaluated from the same prefix. On fired states, the best pooled single-factor policy raises official resolved rate from 40.4% to 43.5% on the per-provider fired subset and from 41.0% to 44.8% on common-fired instances, with provider-specific active components. Overall, TraceGraph provides a process vocabulary for asking what agent benchmarks test, where models diverge on a shared landscape, and how failure regions can guide downstream improvement.

*Yisen Gao,Yixi Cai,Tianshi Zheng,Jiaxin Bai,Yangqiu Song*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有知识图谱上的溯因推理方法在交互式场景中存在局限，难以准确理解多轮对话中不断演变的自然语言意图，且在假设生成失败时缺乏细粒度的诊断与修正能力。

Method: 提出了一种名为 HypoAgent 的智能体框架，包含三个核心模块：意图识别智能体（将对话转化为 KG 条件）、假设生成智能体（基于意图生成假设）以及根本原因分析智能体（对失效假设进行诊断并通过知识图谱邻域探测进行优化）。

Abstract: Abductive reasoning over knowledge graphs aims to generate logical hypotheses that explain observed entities or facts. Existing controllable hypothesis generation methods allow users to guide this process with explicit conditions, but they remain limited in interactive settings: they struggle to ground evolving natural-language intents across multi-turn dialogues and provide little fine-grained diagnosis when generated hypotheses fail. To address these limitations, we propose HypoAgent, an Agentic framework for interactive abductive Hypothesis Generation over knowledge graphs. HypoAgent integrates three agents: an Intent Recognition Agent that grounds user utterances and dialogue history into executable KG conditions, a Hypothesis Generation Agent that performs controllable hypothesis generation according to the extracted user intention, and a Root Cause Analysis Agent that diagnoses unreliable hypothesis fragments and leverages KG neighborhood probing to identify supported refinements. Experiments on commonsense and biomedical domain-specific knowledge graphs demonstrate that HypoAgent achieves state-of-the-art semantic similarity under single-turn, multi-turn, and unconditional settings. Our code is available at https://github.com/HKUST-KnowComp/HypoAgent.

We introduce FAM-Bench, a multi-modal Food-as-Medicine benchmark with 2500 nutrition-expert-verified instances across 13 diet-related health conditions. ### [117] [Answer-Set-Programming-based Abstractions for Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31444)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强化学习在面对大规模状态空间时面临学习和泛化困难，而现有的基于Prolog的CARCASS框架在处理逻辑抽象时存在局限。本文旨在引入更具表现力和完全声明式的答案集编程（ASP）来优化CARCASS框架，以更好地利用领域知识构建抽象，提高强化学习效率。

Method: 作者提出了利用答案集编程（ASP）作为CARCASS框架的底层建模语言来实现抽象化，并对比了其与传统Prolog实现的差异。通过在Blocks World（积木世界）和Minigrid（迷你网格）两个典型领域进行实验评估，验证了该方法的有效性。

Abstract: Reinforcement Learning (RL) enables autonomous agents to learn policies from experience, but realistic problems often involve enormous state spaces, making learning and generalisation challenging. Abstraction and approximation are therefore essential. Relational Reinforcement Learning (RRL) offers a way to reason about objects and their relations, and the CARCASS framework by Martijn van Otterlo demonstrates how logical representations can model Markov Decision Processes (MDPs) in first-order domains. Originally implemented in Prolog, CARCASS leverages domain knowledge to create powerful abstractions. We explore Answer-Set Programming (ASP), which is a rich and, contrary to Prolog, fully declarative modelling language, to realise CARCASS abstractions. We evaluate our ASP-based implementation in case studies of two domains, viz. Blocks World and Minigrid. Our results indicate that CARCASS with ASP provides a promising approach to constructing abstractions for RL, especially when domain knowledge is available.

### [118] [AutoSci: A Memory-Centric Agentic System for the Full Scientific Research Lifecycle](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31468)
*Weitong Qian,Beicheng Xu,Zhongao Xie,Bowen Fan,Guozheng Tang,Jiale Chen,Xinzhe Wu,Mingtian Yang,Chenyang Di,Jiajun Li,Lingching Tung,Peichao Lai,Yifei Xia,Ziyi Guo,Yanwei Xu,Yanzhao Qin,Shaoduo Gan,Xupeng Miao,Bin Cui*

Result: AutoSci 实现了一个能够执行、记忆并跨项目进化的持久化研究环境，填补了当前自动化科研系统在全生命周期管理和自我优化方面的空白。

Conclusion: AutoSci 展示了构建自动化科学研究系统的潜力，通过将记忆管理、流程控制、多智能体协同和自我进化有机结合，为实现长周期、跨项目的全流程科学研究自动化提供了有效的框架。

Abstract: Scientific research has traditionally been human-intensive, requiring researchers to coordinate literature, ideas, experiments, manuscripts, and review responses across long project cycles. The rise of LLM-based scientific agents creates an opportunity to automate this process. Such a system must support the full research lifecycle, maintain structured persistent memory across projects, and improve its own research procedures over time. However, existing systems either partially satisfy or fail to satisfy these requirements, leaving a gap for a unified automated scientific research system. As a result, we present AutoSci, a memory-centric agentic system for the full scientific research lifecycle. AutoSci is organized around four modules. SciMem provides schema-governed research memory, separating Long-Term Knowledge Memory for reusable scientific knowledge from Active Research Memory for project-level artifacts such as ideas, experiments, manuscripts, and reviews. SciFlow executes a five-stage lifecycle from literature understanding to rebuttal through a harness that controls state, context, verification, feedback, and orchestration. SciDAG augments difficult skills with DAG-shaped multi-agent operators and reusable stage-specific templates. SciEvolve converts feedback signals from users, experiments, reviews, and external environments into versioned updates to SciMem organization, SciFlow skills, and SciDAG templates. Together, these modules make AutoSci a persistent research environment that can execute, remember, and evolve across research projects. The code repository is available at https://github.com/skyllwt/AutoSci.
