### [119] [LinTree: Improving LLM Reasoning with Explicitly Structured Search Histories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31492)
*Liwei Kang,Yee Whye Teh,Wee Sun Lee*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 大语言模型的思维链推理本质是搜索，但仅仅提供历史记录效率不高。研究发现，将思维链明确组织为“线性树”（LinTree）结构，能显著增强模型的回溯能力和推理性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然大语言模型通过生成思维链进行推理，本质上是在进行搜索，但其依赖于隐式的搜索轨迹，缺乏对搜索树结构的显式认知。本文旨在探究利用搜索历史是否能提升推理性能，并分析显式化搜索树结构对模型推理能力的改善作用。

Method: 本文采用了受控的推理环境（Blocks World、网格导航、Sokoban），对比了三种方案：1. 基于当前状态的启发式搜索（Best-First Search）；2. 基于隐式搜索轨迹的大模型推理（Raw Trace）；3. 基于显式 linearized tree (LinTree) 结构的大模型推理。通过引入父节点指针（Parent Pointers）使搜索树结构显式化，评估性能提升。

Result: 实验发现：1. 仅凭大模型感知原始搜索历史，性能无法稳定超过基于局部状态的启发式搜索；2. 显式添加父节点指针（LinTree）后，模型的任务完成率和搜索效率均得到了显著提升，证实了结构化历史信息对推理的重要性。

Conclusion: 研究表明，仅仅让大模型感知搜索历史是不够的，将搜索轨迹显式地表示为结构化的树（如通过父节点指针），能显著提升大模型在复杂推理任务中的表现和搜索效率。这为未来设计更具“结构感知能力”的推理模型提供了方向。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) often solve reasoning problems by generating intermediate traces that explore and revise partial solutions. From a search perspective, these traces can be viewed as linearized search trees, where the model extends a partial solution, abandons it when it fails, and backtracks to try alternatives. Compared with traditional heuristic-guided search, such a policy has a potential advantage: it conditions on the whole search trace rather than only on the current local state. We first test whether LLMs utilize this advantage by comparing trace-conditioned reasoning policies against best-first search equipped with an LLM heuristic that only observes the current local state. Across three controlled reasoning environments, Blocks World, grid Navigation, and Sokoban, we find that raw access to search history alone is not enough to reliably outperform heuristic search. We then study one possible reason: in LLM reasoning traces, the underlying search tree is only implicitly represented, and when the model backtracks or switches branches, the trace does not explicitly identify which earlier search state is being revisited. We show that adding simple parent pointers to explicitly represent the linearized tree (LinTree) structure improves both task performance and search efficiency relative to implicit reasoning models and LLM-heuristic-guided search. These results suggest that search history becomes most useful when its tree structure is made explicit, motivating more structure-aware representations for LLM reasoning.

</details>


### [120] [Choosing the Lens: Strategic Perspective Activation in Context-Dependent Argumentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31581)
*Albert Sadowski,Jarosław A. Chudziak*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了上下文相关论证框架（CDAFs），通过允许主体控制论证环境中的相关性集合，从而实现对论证结果的战略操纵，并定义了相关的决策问题及其复杂度分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的论证框架（如Dung的理论）在处理处于不同外部环境下的论证评估时存在局限性，无法直接捕捉到主体利用其对环境的影响力作为“战略杠杆”来改变论证结果的能力。因此，作者旨在建立一种能够显式建模主体如何操纵论证环境的机制。

Method: 本文提出了一种名为上下文相关论证框架（CDAFs）的扩展模型，该模型通过引入“击败函数”（defeat function）来根据不同上下文确定攻击的有效性。此外，文章采用“视角标记特化”（perspective-labeled specialisation），将击败函数分解为相关性集合（ρ）和优先级（π），并将主体的操纵行为建模为选择这些相关性集合的决策问题（ACTIVATION-MANIPULATION）。

Result: 通过一个工作示例验证了CDAFs的有效性，证明了在某些情况下，即使在全相关注入优先级下目标论证被拒绝，通过部分激活也能使其被接受，且这种激活方式无法被现有的价值论证框架（VAF）所模拟。文章同时定义了ACTIVATION-MANIPULATION决策问题，并给出了其基础的计算复杂度界限。

Conclusion: 本文引入的上下文相关论证框架（CDAFs）成功地为论证理论提供了更强的策略性建模能力，使得研究者能够分析主体如何通过改变环境来操纵论证结果。该框架揭示了即使在看似受限的论证条件下，通过部分激活相关集合仍可能改变最终结论，这一发现为理解论证操纵行为提供了严谨的数学基础。

Abstract: The same arguments often need to be evaluated under different external regimes. An agent with influence over the regime has a strategic lever that standard formalisms do not directly capture. We introduce context-dependent argumentation frameworks (CDAFs), an extension of Dung's theory in which a defeat function determines, per context, which attacks succeed. A perspective-labeled specialisation derives the defeat function from a relevance set $ρ$ and a priority $π$. The relevance set is the agent's action space. In a small worked example, the agent's target argument is rejected under every full-relevance injective priority, yet accepted under partial activations, one of which no VAF audience can mirror. We define the corresponding decision problem, ACTIVATION-MANIPULATION, and record baseline complexity bounds. Tight bounds and multi-agent variants are left open.

</details>

### [121] [Gait2Hip-60: A Unified Deep Learning Benchmark for Predicting Hip Muscle Forces and Joint Moments from Multi-Cadence Gait Kinematics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30374)
*Jiaqi Zhang,Ji Hou,Qing Sun,Xianzhi Gao,Bo Huo*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 研究开发了一种深度学习框架，仅凭步态运动学数据即可高效估算髋部肌肉力和关节力矩。对比实验显示Transformer模型性能最优，且在跨病理人群的零样本测试中展现了初步的应用前景，为临床步态动力学评估提供了一种更便捷的替代方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的肌肉骨骼仿真方法虽然能够提供详尽的髋部肌肉力和关节力矩信息，但计算耗时且复杂，难以直接应用于临床环境。因此，研究旨在开发一种高效的深度学习方法，通过步态运动学数据直接预测髋部动力学参数，以简化临床评估流程。

Method: 本研究建立了一个深度学习框架，使用60名健康成年人的步态数据（作为训练集）和9名股骨头坏死（ONFH）患者的数据（作为外部验证集）。输入为下肢关节角度，输出为OpenSim计算的髋部肌肉力和关节力矩。研究对比了LSTM、Transformer和Mamba三种序列模型在统一预处理和评价指标下的性能，并对最优模型进行了零样本（zero-shot）外部验证。

Result: 在健康受试者基准测试中，Transformer模型表现最优，在髋部肌肉力和关节力矩预测上均达到较高的拟合优度（R2分别为0.819和0.862）。在对ONFH患者的零样本验证中，该模型保持了中等程度的预测能力（R2分别为0.537和0.569），证明了其在不同步态及病理状态下的预测潜力。

Conclusion: 本研究验证了利用深度学习模型从步态运动学直接估算髋部动力学参数的可行性，确定了Transformer模型在现有架构中的性能优势，并强调了在临床应用前进一步优化模型泛化能力和开展更广泛病理学验证的必要性。

Abstract: Estimating hip muscle forces and joint moments during gait typically relies on musculoskeletal simulation, which is informative but time-consuming and difficult to apply in clinical settings. This study developed a deep learning framework to predict these hip dynamics parameters directly from lower-limb gait kinematics and compared three representative sequence models under a unified protocol. Gait data were collected from 60 healthy adults under three metronome-guided cadence conditions. Ten bilateral lower-limb joint angles were used as inputs, and OpenSim-derived hip muscle forces and hip joint moments were used as reference outputs. Three deep learning models of LSTM, Transformer, and Mamba were trained and evaluated using the same subject-level split, preprocessing pipeline, and metrics. The best model was then directly tested on an external cohort of 9 patients with osteonecrosis of the femoral head (ONFH) without retraining. In the healthy-subject benchmark, Transformer achieved the best subject-level mean performance for both hip muscle force prediction (RMSE = 1.33 N/kg, MAE = 0.57 N/kg, R2 = 0.819) and hip joint moment prediction (RMSE = 0.11 Nm/kg, MAE = 0.07 Nm/kg, R2 = 0.862), with similar advantages across walking cadences. In zero-shot external validation, Transformer retained moderate predictive ability in ONFH for hip muscle force prediction (RMSE = 1.51 N/kg, MAE = 0.70 N/kg, R2 = 0.537) and hip joint moment prediction (RMSE = 0.17 Nm/kg, MAE = 0.12 Nm/kg, R2 = 0.569). These findings support the feasibility of estimating hip dynamics from gait kinematics, identify Transformer as a strong baseline, and highlight the need for broader pathological validation and improved generalization before clinical application.

### [122] [Unicorn: Scaling High-Dimensional Time Series Forecasting via Universal Correlation Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30376)
*Haochen Yuan,Yichen Song,Yunbo Wang,Xiaokang Yang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对现有时间序列模型难以兼顾扩展性与跨数据集泛化的问题，本文提出了Unicorn框架，通过共享潜空间原型码本捕捉通用的跨通道依赖模式，实现了高性能的多数据集预训练。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了Unicorn（Universal Correlation Network）框架，其核心是利用潜空间原型码本（latent prototype codebook）将异构通道投影到共享潜空间，从而解耦相关性建模与具体通道身份，学习可迁移的、与身份无关的交互模式。

Result: 实验表明，Unicorn在多变量时间序列预测任务中显著优于现有的先进架构，尤其是在少样本迁移场景下展现出极强的通用性和泛化能力。

Conclusion: Unicorn通过解耦通道身份与相关性建模，成功实现了跨数据集的通用时间序列表示学习，为构建大规模多变量时间序列基础模型提供了一条可扩展的新途径。

Abstract: Modern time series architectures face a fundamental trade-off: channel-independent models scale well with increasing data volume but ignore critical inter-channel dependencies, while channel-dependent models are expressive but remain ``dimension-bounded'', struggling to generalize across heterogeneous datasets.To bridge this gap, we introduce Unicorn (Universal Correlation Network), a framework for scalable, multi-dataset pretraining on high-dimensional time series. At the core of Unicorn is a latent prototype codebook that decouples correlation modeling from specific channel identities. By projecting heterogeneous channels into a shared latent space, UniCorN learns identity-agnostic, reusable interaction patterns that transfer across domains with diverse dimensionalities and semantics. Extensive experiments show that Unicorn significantly outperforms state-of-the-art forecasting architectures, particularly in few-shot transfer scenarios, offering a scalable path toward multivariate time series foundation models.

### [123] [When LLMs Learn to Be Consistently Wrong: A Multi-Model Study of Linear Representations of Synthetic Deception](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30381)
*Vahideh Zolfaghari*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过微调五个主流Transformer模型构建“合成不诚实”样本，证明了欺骗行为在模型内部存在高度鲁棒、跨领域一致的线性表征，这些表征在早期层即可被探测，为AI安全监测提供了理论依据与技术路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 欺骗性对齐（Deceptive Alignment）是AI安全的核心挑战，而“合成不诚实”（synthetic dishonesty）为研究欺骗背后的表征机制提供了一个可控的实验环境。研究旨在验证欺骗行为是否在模型内部具有可探测的线性表征，以及这些表征在不同模型架构间的表现差异。

Result: 实验发现，欺骗行为在模型早期层（1-3层）即可被线性探测器以近乎完美的AUC（≥0.99）识别，支持了线性表征假设。Gemma-2模型展现出高维表征的稳定性，而其他模型则表现出表征塌陷。探测器在跨领域任务中表现出良好的泛化性，且欺骗方向在深层模型中不断巩固。

Conclusion: 研究表明，欺骗性的表征在模型中具有高度的鲁棒性且与领域无关，仅需少量的监督微调即可在模型内部根深蒂固。这一发现强调了基于激活的监测技术在AI安全中的重要性，同时指出不同架构（如Gemma-2与Llama/Qwen）在表征稳定性上存在显著差异。

Abstract: Deceptive alignment, in which models maintain accurate internal representations while deliberately producing false outputs, remains a central challenge in AI safety. While strategic deception is the primary long-term concern, synthetic dishonesty - induced via direct optimization on incorrect answers - provides a controlled testbed for studying the representational basis of learned deception. We introduce a multi-model paradigm in which honest and deceptive variants of five transformer models (Pythia-1.4B, Gemma-2-2B/9B, Qwen2.5-7B, Llama-3.1-8B) are fine-tuned using LoRA on the same question distribution. Linear probes trained on mean-pooled hidden states detect synthetic dishonesty with near-perfect AUC (greater than or equal to 0.99) as early as layers 1-3 in four architectures, while Pythia-1.4B reaches a peak of 0.705. Logistic regression probes consistently match or outperform MLP probes, supporting the Linear Representation Hypothesis. Probes trained on TruthfulQA generalize with near-zero loss (Delta AUC approx. 0) to held-out MMLU subjects. Late-layer representations show strong robustness to Gaussian noise, with Gemma-2 models exhibiting exceptional stability. Mechanistic analysis of Fisher Discriminant Ratio, effective rank, centroid geometry, directional stability, cross-domain alignment, and calibration (ECE) reveals two regimes: representational collapse in Pythia/Llama/Qwen versus high-dimensional preservation in Gemma-2. Across all models, the dishonesty direction consolidates progressively in deeper layers, with optimal calibration (ECE less than 0.01 except Pythia) achievable in layers 1-4. These results demonstrate that robust, domain-invariant dishonesty representations can be rapidly entrenched via modest supervised fine-tuning, with implications for activation-based monitoring.

### [124] [A Novel Evaluation Metric for Unsupervised Learning in AIS-Based Maritime Anomaly Detection: MADQI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30388)

  <summary>Details</summary>

2. 结合 Haversine 距离计算对 AIS 数据进行空间和行为特征分析。

These anomalies include abnormal vessel behaviours related to speed, position jumps, time gaps, and turn angles. Although unsupervised learning algorithms such as Isolation Forest are widely used for detecting anomalous vessel movements, they often lack systematic and meaningful evaluation measures. To address this limitation, we propose a novel quality metric called Maritime Anomaly Detection Quality Index (MADQI). The prosed MADQI is a composite index designed to evaluate the anomaly detection performance of machine learning models without requiring labelled data. The proposed framework uses Haversine distance calculations to analyse AIS datasets and identify anomalies based on their spatial and behavioural characteristics. The proposed MADQI evaluation framework integrates four interconnected metrics: Anomaly Rate Consistency (ARC), Physical Plausibility Score (PPS), Score Distribution Separation (SDS), and Extreme Case Evidence (ECE). These metrics are combined through automatic normalisation using multi-chunk evaluation and adaptive scaling techniques. Experimental results on the AIS dataset show that the proposed framework achieved a MADQI score of 80.37%, demonstrating its effectiveness for unsupervised anomaly detection. In particular, the algorithm performed strongly in identifying abnormal vessel behaviour. Among the individual MADQI components, ECE and ARC achieved scores of 0.907 and 1.000, respectively, indicating excellent capability in detecting extreme anomalies and maintaining anomaly rate consistency. Overall, these results are encouraging and demonstrate that the proposed framework provides a reliable and meaningful approach for evaluating unsupervised anomaly detection in maritime AIS data.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 作者提出了“NumLeak”测量框架，结合了对闭源生产模型（Frontier LLMs）的API探测和对开源因果语言模型（Causal LM）的白盒对照验证。通过分析模型在历史数值指标（如Fama-French因子、失业率、CPI、温度）上的表现，引入受控验证（Holdout）和对数概率（logprob）排序分析，从而量化模型的记忆水平。

Result: 实验发现顶级大语言模型在已知数值指标上具有极高的记忆相关性（Pearson r≈0.99）。在测试近期未公开的holdout数据时，模型回答率大幅下降，但已回答部分的准确率依然极高，印证了其记忆机制。此外，模型在复杂任务中表现出的“市场情绪预测”能力，在剔除掉模型对特定数值的记忆回溯后，其实际有效性几乎归零。

Conclusion: 当前大语言模型在数值任务上的高性能往往归功于预训练数据的“记忆”而非真正的推理能力。该研究揭示了数值预测性能与记忆力之间的强相关性，并指出单纯的黑盒评估低估了记忆现象。此外，研究还提供了一种基于系统提示词的防御策略，能在不损失通用任务能力的前提下有效降低记忆风险。

Abstract: Public numeric benchmarks appear in pretraining, so an evaluation that conditions on a date may be measuring memorized recall rather than out-of-sample skill. We introduce NumLeak, a measurement framework that combines API-boundary probes on production models with a white-box controlled validation on an open causal LM. Top-tier frontier LLMs recall the Fama-French market excess return at 3-seed pooled Pearson r=0.97-0.99 while staying within 0.15 within-25bps on the five sibling factors; comparable fidelity appears on U.S. unemployment, CPI inflation, and NOAA temperature. The white-box experiment reproduces the dose-response, and logprob ranking detects memorization that open-ended generation misses, implying closed-API black-box probes understate the channel. A Sonnet "date to market-sentiment" regression that correlates with true Mkt-RF at r=0.74 collapses to r=0.02 once the model's own recall is residualized out. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准测试多聚焦于孤立或短期的任务，无法有效衡量智能体在真实世界中处理复杂、长程且需不断演变的分析任务的能力。

Method: 提出了 LongDS 基准测试，包含 68 个基于真实 Kaggle 笔记本的任务，涵盖 6 个领域，总计 2225 轮交互。该基准设计了状态演变模式（如反事实扰动、回滚、多状态组合），平均依赖跨度为 11.3 轮，用以评估智能体在长周期内维护、更新及恢复分析上下文的能力。

Result: 在对五种 SOTA 模型评估后发现：最好模型的平均准确率仅为 48.45%；随着任务轮次推移，性能下降接近 47 个百分点；长程推理错误占总失败案例的 52% 到 69%；增加交互步数并不必然提升性能。

Conclusion: 目前的智能体在处理长程、多轮数据分析任务时表现较差，核心瓶颈在于难以维护和更新长期的分析状态，而非交互步骤不足。LongDS 为未来的智能体评估与改进提供了基准。

Abstract: Real-world data analysis is inherently iterative, yet existing benchmarks mostly evaluate isolated or short interactive tasks, leaving agents' ability to track evolving analytical context over long horizons untested. We introduce LongDS, a benchmark for long-horizon, multi-turn data analysis where agents must maintain, update, restore, and compose evolving analytical states. LongDS comprises 68 tasks constructed from real-world Kaggle notebooks, spanning 2,225 turns across six domains including Geoscience, Business, and Education. Tasks are designed around state-evolution patterns (e.g., counterfactual perturbation, rollback, multi-state composition), with an average dependency span of 11.3 turns. Evaluating five state-of-the-art models, we find that the best model reaches only 48.45% average accuracy, performance drops nearly 47 points from early to late turns, and long-horizon errors account for 52%--69% of failures. Further analysis shows that additional agent steps do not necessarily improve performance, suggesting that the key bottleneck is maintaining a correct analytical state rather than increasing interaction budget. We release LongDS to support research on reliable long-horizon agentic data analysis. Code and data will be released at https://github.com/zjunlp/DataMind.

### [127] [Calibrated Preference Learning: The Case of Label Ranking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30447)
*Santo M. A. R. Thies,Viktor Bengs,Timo Kaufmann,Sebastian J. Vollmer,Eyke Hüllermeier*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的校准研究多集中于分类和回归任务，缺乏针对概率标签排序任务的正式校准框架；直接将排序视为分类任务会忽略其内在结构，无法有效捕捉成对或Top-k预测等关键模态。

Method: 作者形式化地定义了标签排序的校准概念，构建了一个包含完整排序、子排序和Top-k排序的校准层次结构；通过理论分析证明了各层级间的逻辑关系，并实证评估了主流标签排序模型及RLHF奖励模型的校准性能。

Abstract: Calibration, the alignment of predicted probabilities with true outcome frequencies, is essential for reliable decision-making. While extensively studied for classification and regression, calibration has not been formally addressed for probabilistic label ranking, where the goal is to predict a distribution over orderings of a label set. Naively treating rankings as classes ignores their structure and fails to capture important modalities such as pairwise and top-k predictions. We formalize calibration for label ranking and develop a hierarchy of notions covering full rankings, sub-rankings, and top-k rankings. We prove that full-rank calibration implies the others but not conversely, and sub-ranking and top-k calibration are incomparable. Empirically, we find popular label ranking models are often poorly calibrated, with substantial differences between sub-ranking and top-k metrics. Applying our framework to RLHF reward models, we find that calibration correlates strongly but not perfectly with benchmark accuracy, suggesting it captures a meaningful quality dimension beyond top-1 accuracy. These findings motivate future work on understanding the downstream effects of miscalibration and developing methods to correct it.

### [128] [Bounded Behavioral Indistinguishability for Black-Box LLM Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30448)
*Munawar Hasan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文指出语义相似度评估无法全面衡量大模型蒸馏的效果，引入了“有界行为不可区分性”框架。研究发现，即使语义匹配度很高，学生模型在对抗性测试中仍能被区分，因此黑盒蒸馏的评估需要超越语义层面，转向更全面的行为与对抗性维度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前黑盒大模型蒸馏主要通过输出语义匹配度来评估，但这种方法无法保证学生模型在实际行为上与教师模型完全一致。作者旨在解决“输出相似不代表行为无异”这一核心问题，通过建立更严格的定量评估框架来揭示蒸馏模型中潜藏的行为偏差。

Method: 该论文提出了“有界行为不可区分性”（bounded behavioral indistinguishability）的概念，通过包含查询限制、计算限制及对抗类别的一套形式化指标来度量模型行为。研究者构建了一个包含5,000个提示词的行为探测套件，通过对Qwen和Llama教师-学生模型对进行LoRA蒸馏实验，利用对抗性判别器、成对教师识别对抗机制以及跨模型判别器评估蒸馏效果，对比了蒸馏前后模型在行为上的可区分性变化。

Result: 实验发现，尽管LoRA蒸馏显著提高了语义相似度（Qwen从0.788提至0.862，Llama从0.814提至0.874），但对抗性评估表明模型间仍存在显著的行为差异。行为差异主要集中在风格/格式、模型鲁棒性和特定领域技术提示词中。虽然蒸馏降低了行为可区分性（如Qwen从0.158降至0.081），但并未完全消除。此外，基于分歧的数据采集策略并不一定优于分层随机抽样，表明覆盖率和多样性在评估中依然至关重要。

Conclusion: 该研究结论指出，单纯依赖语义相似度作为评估指标是不够的。黑盒大模型蒸馏需要引入有界、对抗性和类别感知的评估体系，以确保学生模型在行为上真正与教师模型不可区分。仅仅优化语义匹配并不能消除学生模型与教师模型在风格、稳健性和领域特异性方面的行为差异。

Abstract: Black-box LLM distillation is usually evaluated as an output-matching problem: a student is considered successful when its responses are semantically similar to, or task-consistent with, those of a teacher. However, output similarity does not imply that the student is behaviorally indistinguishable from the model it imitates. We introduce bounded behavioral indistinguishability, formalized as $(ε,q,t,\mathbb{A})$-behavioral indistinguishability over an explicit prompt distribution, where $ε$ bounds distinguishing advantage, $q$ bounds oracle queries, $t$ bounds computation, and $\mathbb{A}$ denotes the adversary class.
  We instantiate this notion on Qwen and Llama teacher-student pairs using a controlled $5,000$-prompt behavioral probe suite. For each family, we compare the teacher with both the base student and the LoRA-distilled student, measuring whether distillation reduces distinguishability rather than merely improving similarity. LoRA raises semantic similarity from $0.788$ to $0.862$ for Qwen and from $0.814$ to $0.874$ for Llama. Yet adversarial evaluation reveals remaining behavioral differences: learned discriminators retain nonzero advantage, and pairwise category analysis shows artifacts concentrated in style/format, robustness, and domain-technical prompts. A pairwise teacher-identification adversary confirms this trend. With a different-family Llama judge and A/B-swap consistency filtering, Qwen distinguishing advantage drops from $0.158$ for the base student to $0.081$ after LoRA distillation. Query-budget experiments show that disagreement-guided acquisition does not consistently outperform stratified random sampling, indicating that coverage and diversity remain strong baselines. Our results show that semantic fidelity is useful but insufficient: black-box LLM distillation requires bounded, adversarial, and category-aware evaluation.

</details>


### [129] [VeriGate: Verifier-Gated Step-Level Supervision for GRPO](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30451)
*Aakriti Agrawal,Minghui Liu,Furong Huang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: VeriGate 是一种改进的 GRPO 算法，通过动态结合结果与过程监督，并引入 token 级优势函数分配机制，有效解决了传统 GRPO 训练中奖励稀疏和学习停滞的问题，显著提升了推理模型的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的 GRPO 在训练推理模型时依赖基于结果的奖励，当所有样本奖励相同时，学习过程会因梯度消失而停滞。此外，缺乏步骤级信用分配限制了模型对复杂推理能力的学习，且容易产生奖励欺骗（reward hacking）。

Method: 1. Verifier-Gated 机制：根据奖励分布动态选择使用结果监督（Verifier）或过程监督（PRM）；2. 未来累积奖励（Future-cumulated rewards）：将过程奖励转换为考虑后续轨迹的信用分配；3. 分组归一化 token 级优势函数：通过该转换生成更具信息量的梯度，以实现细粒度的信用分配。

Result: 在 MATH 数据集上使用 Qwen2.5-Instruct（1.5B 和 7B）进行实验，在六个推理基准测试中，1.5B 和 7B 模型准确率分别提升了约 20% 和 12%，显著减少了梯度失效现象，并降低了奖励欺骗行为。

Conclusion: VeriGate 通过结合结果监督与过程监督，有效解决了 GRPO 在奖励稀疏或退化情况下的学习停滞问题。该方法在保持结果监督主导地位的同时，利用细粒度的过程反馈进行梯度优化，在提升推理性能的同时增强了训练的稳定性和抗黑客行为能力。

Abstract: Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) is an effective recipe for training reasoning models with verifier-based outcome rewards, but its supervision is sparse: when all sampled trajectories for a prompt receive the same verifier reward, the group-relative advantage collapses to zero and learning stalls. Outcome-only rewards also provide no step-level credit assignment, limiting exploration and making it harder to learn robust reasoning. We present VeriGate (Verifier-Gated Step-Level GRPO), a verifier-gated extension of GRPO that addresses these limitations with three design choices. First, VeriGate keeps the verifier in charge whenever verifier rewards induce a meaningful preference among sampled trajectories, and uses process supervision only when verifier rewards are degenerate. Second, instead of collapsing Process Reward Model (PRM) step scores into a single trajectory reward, VeriGate converts them into future-cumulated rewards to assign continuation-aware credit. Third, VeriGate transforms these rewards into group-normalized token-level advantages, restoring informative gradients and fine-grained credit assignment while remaining less susceptible to reward hacking than methods that optimize aggregated PRM scores. Empirically, training on MATH with 1.5B and 7B Qwen2.5-Instruct models and evaluating on six reasoning benchmarks, VeriGate improves average accuracy by about 20% and 12% for 1.5B and 7B models respectively, substantially reduces zero-gradient failures, decreases reward-hacking behavior, and improves reasoning quality relative to outcome-only GRPO and PRM-as-outcome baselines.

</details>


### [130] [A Unified Framework for Gradient Aggregation in Multi-Objective Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30452)
*Zeou Hu,Kelvin Ho,Yaoliang Yu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一个统一的梯度聚合框架，通过引入充分对齐条件和原始优化视角，理论化地解决了多目标优化中的收敛性问题，并据此设计出更具鲁棒性的新算法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的多目标优化（MOO）算法种类繁多、动机各异，且缺乏统一的理论框架来分析不同梯度聚合方法在收敛性上的共性和差异。为了解决这一局限性，作者旨在建立一个统一的理论框架，以确立 Pareto 平稳性的收敛速率并指导算法设计。

Method: 1. 建立了一个统一的梯度聚合框架，涵盖多种多目标优化算法；2. 提出了“充分对齐条件”（Sufficient Alignment Condition）以分析收敛性；3. 从原始优化视角对梯度聚合进行建模，并利用对偶锥投影确保可行性；4. 引入基于 CVaR 的 Capped MGDA 算法。

Result: 1. 推导出在凸包内选择非冲突梯度作为收敛的充分条件；2. 证明了通过对偶锥投影可以保证算法的可行性；3. 通过实验验证了理论分析的正确性，并展示了 Capped MGDA 在对抗性联邦学习中的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 本文提供了一个统一的梯度聚合框架，明确了多目标优化收敛的充分条件。通过将现有算法纳入统一的原始优化视角，不仅理清了算法间的理论联系，还为开发更鲁棒的新型算法（如 Capped MGDA）提供了坚实的理论支撑。研究证明了该框架在处理对抗性联邦学习等复杂场景下的有效性。

Abstract: Many machine learning problems involve multiple inherent trade-offs that are best addressed by gradient-based multi-objective optimization (MOO) algorithms. Existing methods are often proposed with various motivations, analyzed case by case, and differ algorithmically in how the component gradients are aggregated at each step. In this work, we develop a unifying framework for gradient aggregation in MOO, establishing (optimal) rates of convergence to Pareto stationarity, the standard measure of performance in MOO. Central to our analysis is a sufficient alignment condition, from which we derive a theorem showing that non-conflicting directions, when chosen within the convex hull of gradients, form a fundamental sufficient condition for convergence. We further show that feasibility can be ensured through projection onto the dual cone, broadening the scope of methods that admit convergence guarantees. In parallel, we present a primal optimization perspective of gradient aggregation that encompasses established algorithms, clarifies their theoretical relationships, and enables the design of new variants. As an illustration, we introduce capped MGDA, derived from a CVaR-based formulation, and demonstrate its robustness in adversarial federated learning. Finally, we validate our theory through experiments on synthetic problems and practical benchmarks.

</details>


### [131] [Scalable Constrained Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning via State Augmentation and Consensus for Separable Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30461)
*Santiago Amaya-Corredor,Miguel Calvo-Fullana,Anders Jonsson*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种可扩展的分布式约束MARL框架，通过邻居间对偶变量的一致性通信，实现了大规模多智能体系统下的全局资源约束协同，有效克服了传统方法在扩展性和可行性上的缺陷。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的多智能体强化学习方法在处理全局资源约束时面临挑战：独立学习难以确定各智能体对全局约束的贡献，导致无法产生可行解；而传统的“集中式训练、分布式执行”（CTDE）方法随着智能体数量增加，计算复杂度呈二次方增长，难以扩展至大规模系统。因此，亟需一种既能满足全局约束，又具备高扩展性的分布式学习架构。

Method: 本文提出了一种分布式约束多智能体强化学习（MARL）方法，其核心在于：1. 采用状态增强的策略学习，将局部状态与编码约束反馈的对偶变量结合；2. 利用邻域间对偶变量（拉格朗日乘子）的分布式一致性算法，在无中心控制的情况下实现全局约束协同。该方法具备线性扩展性，且在执行阶段仅需局部通信。

Result: 实验结果表明，在智能电网需求响应场景下，缺乏一致性协同的智能体无法解决约束问题；而引入对偶变量一致性后，智能体能够收敛至共享的对偶变量，在满足全局容量约束的同时确保需求履行。此外，该方法成功扩展至数千个智能体，而对比的CTDE基准方法仅能处理数十个智能体。理论分析证明了共识误差与约束违例之间的紧密联系及其收敛性。

Conclusion: 本文提出的基于对偶变量一致性的分布式约束MARL方法，在保证全局约束满足的前提下，通过轻量级通信实现了线性扩展性。研究表明，在多智能体协作任务中，通过邻域通信达成对偶变量共识是实现约束满足和系统可行性的关键。该方法优于传统的CTDE范式，特别适用于大规模智能体系统。

Abstract: We present a distributed approach for constrained Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning (MARL) that combines state-augmented policy learning with distributed consensus over dual variables. Our method targets systems where agents have separable dynamics but must coordinate to satisfy global resource constraints, a setting in which, as we demonstrate empirically, independent learning fails to produce feasible solutions because agents cannot determine appropriate individual contributions toward collective constraint satisfaction. The key technical contribution is showing that lightweight neighbor-to-neighbor consensus over Lagrange multipliers suffices for globally coordinated constraint enforcement while preserving the scalability of independent training. Each agent learns a single augmented policy offline, conditioned on both its local state and a dual variable encoding constraint feedback. During execution, agents reach agreement on this dual variable through local communication alone. We prove that under mild connectivity assumptions, the consensus error among agents' multipliers is bounded, and show that this translates to a bounded constraint violation that decreases with graph connectivity and the number of consensus rounds. Unlike centralized training with decentralized execution (CTDE) approaches, whose complexity grows at least quadratically with agent count, our method scales linearly in both training and execution. Experiments on smart grid demand response demonstrate that consensus coordination is \emph{essential for feasibility}: without it, agents satisfy grid capacity constraints only by indefinitely postponing demand, a degenerate non-solution. With consensus, agents converge to a shared dual variable and satisfy both grid constraints and demand fulfillment, scaling to thousands of agents while CTDE baselines are limited to dozens.

</details>


### [132] [idSCD: Identifying Training Datasets through Semantic Correlation Descriptors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30462)
*Andrada Gobeaja,Ionut Hodoroaga,Elena Burceanu,Marius Leordeanu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种名为“语义相关性描述符（SCD）”的白盒方法，通过分析模型内部学习到的虚假语义关联来识别模型的训练数据成员身份，其性能优于多种主流的黑盒与白盒攻击基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的大多数成员推理攻击依赖于黑盒行为（如置信度分数、损失、生成样本等），这些方法往往存在局限性。作者认为，数据集在模型中留下了特定的“虚假相关性”痕迹，即在特定数据集内具有预测性但在任务层面并非因果性的规律，通过捕捉这些痕迹可以更准确地识别数据集的成员身份。

Method: 提出了一种基于语义相关性描述符（SCD）的白盒指纹识别方法。SCD旨在捕获模型所学习到的语义相关结构并使其在不同数据集混合中具有可比性。研究通过对比目标数据集的SCD与模型的SCD，构建了一种无需重新训练模型的成员推理分数，从而判断数据集是否包含在模型的训练集中。

Result: 在自然语言推理、情感分类和医学文本分类三个实验场景中，基于SCD的成员推理分数在识别准确性上表现最佳，ROC-AUC指标表现优于RMIA、Attack-P、LiRA及SIF等现有基线方法。当数据集具有显著的语义独特性时，相对性能提升超过60%。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了数据集成员身份可以通过模型内部学习到的语义相关性结构进行追踪。通过利用这种“语义指纹”，可以有效地识别模型训练数据的来源，为评估模型训练数据的版权、隐私及公平性提供了新的审计工具。

Abstract: Can a dataset be recognized from the spurious correlations it induces during training? We argue that datasets leave dataset-specific traces in a model's learned semantic correlation structure: incidental regularities that are predictive within a dataset, but not causal for the underlying task, can be internalized during training. We use this insight to study dataset-level membership inference, moving beyond existing methods that rely on behavioral or distributional evidence such as confidence scores, losses, margins, generated samples, or query responses. We introduce a white-box semantic fingerprinting approach based on semantic correlation descriptors (SCDs), which capture the semantic correlation structure learned by a model and make it comparable across dataset mixtures. In a controlled leave-one-dataset-out diagnostic, SCDs recover dataset-specific changes and perfectly separate matching from non-matching dataset pairs. We then propose a practical SCD-based membership score that tests whether a target dataset is part of a model's training mixture using only the model's SCD and the target dataset's standalone SCD, without requiring leave-one-dataset-out models. Across three diverse experimental settings, with dataset groups for natural language inference, emotion classification, and medical text classification, we test both the advantages and limitations of SCD-based membership inference with different degrees of semantic separation and keyword support between dataset splits. On average, the classifier based on this score achieves the highest performance and the lowest std, outperforming black-box baselines RMIA, Attack-P, and LiRA, as well as the white-box SIF baseline. These results show that dataset membership can be traced through internal semantic correlations, with the largest relative gain exceeding 60% in ROC-AUC when dataset groups expose distinct semantic particularities.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种针对图分类模型的黑盒模型提取攻击方法，核心步骤包括：1. 利用解释输出引导蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）边敏感度估计，通过Hoeffding不等式保证估计精度，从而定位决策边界；2. 利用解释子图（Explanation Subgraphs）缩小搜索空间，提高攻击效率。该方法仅依赖离散标签和二值解释掩码，无需概率分数或梯度信息。

Result: 在多个领域的基准图数据集上的实验结果表明，该攻击方法显著优于同类基准方法，能够在无需访问内部参数、概率分数或梯度的情况下，有效提取图分类模型。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了图机器学习服务（GMLaaS）中可解释性接口带来的严重安全隐患。由于可解释性工具生成的掩码（Mask）泄露了关于决策边界的关键信息，攻击者可以在极度受限的黑盒条件下提取图分类模型。这一发现强调了在部署XAI（可解释人工智能）时，必须在透明度需求与模型安全性之间进行权衡，并呼吁制定更完善的防御机制和政策框架。

Abstract: Graph Machine Learning as a Service (GMLaaS) platforms increasingly implement explainability interfaces to meet regulatory transparency requirements. However, this transparency creates exploitable vulnerabilities for model extraction attacks. We present the first model extraction attack specifically designed for graph classification under strict black-box constraints where the attacker observes only discrete class labels and binary explanation masks (no probability scores, gradients, or confidence values). Our method (1) uses model explanation outputs to guide Monte Carlo edge sensitivity estimation toward decision boundaries, with Hoeffding concentration guarantees on estimation accuracy and (2) exploits explanation subgraphs to efficiently narrow the boundary search space. Extensive experiments on benchmark graph datasets across multiple domains demonstrate our method's superiority over comparable baselines. These findings demonstrate that such explainability interfaces create exploitable attack surfaces, informing both defensive mechanisms and policy frameworks for explainable AI mandates. The implementation code is provided in https://github.com/LabRAI/XSTEAL/.

### [134] [Universal Multiclass Transductive Online Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30479)
*Steve Hanneke,Hongao Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过提出LCLL树这一组合结构，为具有无界标签空间的通用直推式在线分类问题提供了完整的可学习性刻画，并证明了其错误率仅表现为有界或对数增长两种情况。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的在线学习理论通常假设标签空间有限或固定。针对标签空间可能无限大且实例序列先验已知（直推式）的场景，缺乏一套完整的可学习性判别准则和错误率界限刻画，因此需要建立新的理论框架来分析此类问题。

Method: 本文采用了理论计算机科学与在线学习理论的研究方法，提出了“层约束Littlestone树”（LCLL树）作为刻画可学习性的新组合结构，并结合无动于衷（indifference）属性，推导了可学习性的充分必要条件及最优错误率界限，同时将研究范围扩展至不可知模型和随机生成过程情形。

Result: 研究表明，在通用直推式在线分类设置中，可学习概念类的最优错误率仅存在两种可能：常数界或对数级增长。研究构建了基于LCLL树的判定准则，并成功将其推广至不可知（agnostic）学习场景及仅已知实例生成随机过程的场景。

Conclusion: 本文通过引入LCLL树这一新型组合结构，完全刻画了具有无界标签空间的通用直推式在线分类问题的可学习性，并指出了该设置下最优错误率的两种离散形态（有界或对数增长）。

Abstract: We consider the problem of universal transductive online classification with a possibly unbounded label space. This setting considers online learning, with the sequence of instances (without labels) known to the learner in advance. We say a concept class $\mathcal{H}$ is learnable if there is a learning algorithm $\mathcal{A}$, such that for every realizable sequence, the number of mistakes made by $\mathcal{A}$ grows at most sublinearly with the number of predictions. We characterize the learnability of this setting and show that there are only two possible optimal rates for the learnable classes: either bounded or increasing logarithmically. We introduce a new combinatorial structure, called ``Level-Constrained-Littlestone-Littlestone (LCLL) tree'', which, along with the indifference property, characterizes the learnability. We also extend the learnability result to the agnostic case and the case where only the stochastic process that generates the instance sequence is known.

### [135] [Discovering a Zeta Map Algorithm on Dyck Paths via Mechanistic Interpretability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30482)
*Xiaoyu Huang,Blake Jackson,Kyu-Hwan Lee*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 作者训练了一个小型Transformer模型（单层、单头编码器-解码器架构）来学习Dyck路径的zeta映射，并利用机械可解释性技术（解码器交叉注意力分析、线性探测和因果干预）剖析模型的内部计算机制，进而提炼出名为“脚手架映射”（scaffolding map）的组合算法。

Conclusion: 通过机械可解释性工具解析机器学习模型，能够将原本“黑盒”的模型行为转化为严谨、人类可验证的数学算法，为AI辅助数学发现提供了一种可控且可靠的新范式。

Abstract: Machine learning is increasingly used in mathematical discovery, but in mathematics the desired output is often not a prediction itself, but an explicit construction that can be checked independently. We study this setting through the zeta map on Dyck paths, a classical bijection in the combinatorics of the q,t-Catalan numbers. We train a deliberately small one-layer, one-head encoder-decoder transformer on this map and analyze its learned computation using mechanistic interpretability tools, including decoder cross-attention analysis, linear probing, and causal intervention. The analysis reveals a level-based mechanism: encoder representations make path levels linearly accessible, while the decoder selects and traverses input positions in a structured way. Translating these signals into combinatorics leads to the scaffolding map, an explicit peak-centered traversal algorithm for Dyck paths. We prove that this algorithm agrees with the zeta map, modulo a reversal convention in the labeling. This gives a controlled example of AI-assisted mathematical discovery in which mechanistic interpretability turns model behavior into a precise, human-verifiable combinatorial algorithm.

### [136] [MAAT: Multi-phase Adapter-Aware Targeted Unlearning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30514)
*Suryash Yagnik,Shubham Gaur,Saksham Thakur,Vinija Jain,Aman Chadha,Amitava Das*

TL;DR: 针对现有机器遗忘评估对“因果推理（Why）”类问题覆盖严重不足的问题，本文提出了平衡基准5WBENCH，并设计了MAAT框架，有效解决了深度推理知识的遗忘难题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前的机器遗忘（Machine Unlearning）评估基准存在结构性偏差，对涉及因果与逻辑关系（Why类问题）的样本覆盖极低（通常低于1.3%），导致模型在这些关键推理任务上的遗忘失败被掩盖，缺乏有效的量化评估手段。

Method: 1. 构建了5WBENCH数据集：包含5000个样本，均分为Who、What、When、Where、Why五类，专门用于量化模型在因果推理方面的遗忘能力。2. 提出了MAAT框架：一种针对LoRA适配器的三阶段遗忘方法，结合了梯度投影上升、SVD秩维度剪枝、任务向量取反以及混合KL散度-隐藏层状态保留修复技术。

Result: 研究表明，现有的遗忘算法在Why类问题上难以同时兼顾遗忘效果与知识保留。MAAT框架在5WBENCH基准上取得了突破，首次实现了对因果知识的高效遗忘并同时保持了其他核心知识的稳健性，在遗忘-保留的帕累托前沿达到了新的高度。

Conclusion: 现有的机器遗忘评估基准严重偏向事实性知识，忽略了对因果和关系推理（Why类问题）的评估。MAAT框架通过多阶段适配器感知技术，有效地解决了因果知识遗忘中存在的遗忘效果与知识保留之间的权衡难题，为机器遗忘研究提供了新的性能基准。

Abstract: Machine unlearning evaluation is structurally skewed: Why-type questions, which probe causal and relational knowledge, comprise less than 0.06% of CounterFact, 0.6% of ZSRE, and less than 1.3% of TOFU, MUSE, and WMDP-Cyber. This near-zero representation means that methods that fail on causal knowledge can score highly in aggregate, and this failure is undetectable without balanced evaluation. We present 5WBENCH, a balanced 5,000-sample benchmark with 1,000 examples per 5W category (Who, What, When, Where, Why), making causal unlearning failures quantifiable for the first time. Using 5WBENCH, we show that no existing baseline simultaneously achieves high forgetting and high retention on Why-type questions: aggressive forgetting degrades retained knowledge, while conservative methods fail to forget causal facts. Why-type difficulty stems from multi-hop reasoning chains (44% of Why entries vs. less than or equal to 2% for others) and gradient dilution over 40.1-token answer spans. We present MAAT (Multi-phase Adapter-Aware Targeted Unlearning), a three-phase framework operating on LoRA adapter weights, combining gradient-projected ascent, SVD rank-dimension pruning, task vector negation, and hybrid KL-hidden-state retain repair. MAAT is the first method to simultaneously achieve high forgetting and high retention on Why-type causal knowledge, reaching a new operating point on the forget-retain Pareto frontier. We make our code publicly available.

</details>


### [137] [Revisiting Padded Transformer Expressivity: Which Architectural Choices Matter and Which Don't](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30523)
*Anej Svete,William Merrill,Ryan Cotterell,Ashish Sabharwal*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了Transformer与布尔电路的精确计算等价性，发现通过合理的填充与循环配置，Transformer能够覆盖多种电路复杂度类，并证明了其表达能力主要取决于数值精度与模型深度，而非模型宽度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有关于Transformer计算能力的研究缺乏精确的定性表征，且研究结果高度依赖于特定的模型建模假设，缺乏对注意力类型、模型宽度和统一性变化下鲁棒性的系统性探究。

Method: 利用电路复杂度理论工具，分析不同配置下的Transformer模型（包括填充、数值精度、模型深度、宽度以及循环机制），将Transformer的计算能力与L-uniform AC0、TC0以及FO-uniform AC^d/TC^d等电路复杂度类进行对齐与等价证明。

Result: 证明了多项式填充的常数精度Transformer等价于L-uniform AC0；增长精度Transformer等价于L-uniform TC0；引入循环机制后，常数精度可达到FO-uniform AC^d，增长精度可达到FO-uniform TC^d。此外，发现超过对数级别的宽度或精度增加并不会进一步提升模型表达能力。

Conclusion: 本文确立了带填充（padded）的Transformer与布尔电路类之间的精确等价关系，证明了模型的表达能力主要受数值精度和深度的限制，而模型宽度和注意力机制类型的变化对表达能力的影响具有高度鲁棒性。

Abstract: Recent work describes what transformers can and cannot compute through connections to boolean circuits, but existing results lack exact characterizations and are sensitive to modeling choices. Padded transformers -- to whose input filler symbols such as ``...'' are appended -- emerge as a useful gadget for establishing equivalences to circuit classes by providing polynomial space for adaptive parallel computation. However, only a limited set of padded transformer idealizations has been studied, leaving open how robustly these equivalences hold under changes to attention type, model width, and uniformity. We find that, under practical assumptions, padded transformers are surprisingly robust to all of these, and identify numeric precision and model depth as the main factors affecting expressivity. Concretely, we prove that polynomially padded $\text{L-uniform}$ constant-precision transformers are equivalent to $\text{L-uniform AC}^0$, while growing-precision ones achieve $\text{L-uniform TC}^0$ regardless of width. Furthermore, looping enables sequential processing analogous to circuits: $\log^d N$-looped constant-precision transformers reach $\text{FO-uniform AC}^d$, and growing-precision ones reach $\text{FO-uniform TC}^d$. Interestingly, growing width or precision beyond logarithmic does not increase expressivity, and all our results hold for both softmax and average hard attention transformers.

### [138] [Representation Collapse in Sequential Post-Training of Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30524)
*Yichen Liu,Mingyu Chen,Hao Wang,Xiaoran Xu,Chenxi Lin,Rui Zhang,Yutong Zhou,Yuxin Yang,Jiarui Wu,Wei Sun*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了大型语言模型在多阶段后训练过程中表征空间退化（变低秩、同质化）的现象，揭示了其对模型可塑性和泛化能力的损害，并提出了一系列旨在保持模型学习能力的轻量级干预策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大型语言模型通常采用多阶段链式后训练而非单一指令微调，这种演进方式对模型内部表征空间的影响尚不明确。作者旨在探讨这种序列化后训练是否会导致模型内部表征向低秩、各向异性及同质化的方向退化，并揭示这种表征过度集中对模型后续适应性、泛化性能及校准能力的负面影响。

Method: 研究团队构建了一套测量工具集，对隐藏状态、Logits、词元轨迹及LoRA更新权重进行定量分析。通过在受控的阶段顺序下，对比监督微调、偏好优化、安全/拒绝调整、数学代码特化及长思维链调整等多个后训练阶段，考察表征随时间演变的几何特性。此外，文中还评估了包括混合领域回放、特征刷新、表征多样性正则化以及LoRA更新去相关在内的多种轻量级干预策略。

Result: 研究发现：1. 序列化后训练确实会显著导致模型表征空间的几何收缩与同质化；2. 这种表征集中化现象不仅是理论几何特征，更直接预测了模型后续适应阶段的“可塑性瓶颈”；3. 应用提出的干预技术（如领域回放、LoRA去相关等）能有效改善模型表征的分布状态，从而在不损害特定任务表现的前提下，提升模型持续学习的能力。

Conclusion: 研究证实，语言模型在多阶段后训练中会不可避免地出现表征崩塌（即特征空间变低秩、各向异性增强和同质化），这种过度集中的表征会导致模型后续学习的可塑性降低、泛化能力受损及校准性能下降。通过引入混合领域回放、特征刷新和LoRA更新去相关等干预手段，可以在维持任务行为收益的同时，有效缓解表征退化，保留模型的未来可学习性。

Abstract: Large language models are now adapted through chains of post-training stages rather than through a single instruction-tuning pass. This paper studies whether such sequential post-training gradually compresses internal representations into low-rank, anisotropic, and homogeneous feature spaces. We define a measurement suite for hidden states, logits, token trajectories, and LoRA updates, and we use it to analyze supervised fine-tuning, preference optimization, safety/refusal tuning, math and code specialization, and long chain-of-thought tuning under controlled stage orderings. The central hypothesis is that excessive representation concentration is not merely a geometric curiosity: it predicts reduced plasticity during later adaptation, weaker out-of-domain generalization, and poorer calibration. We further evaluate lightweight interventions, including mixed-domain replay, feature refresh, representation diversity regularization, and LoRA update decorrelation, as ways to preserve future learnability without giving up the behavioral gains of post-training.

### [139] [Measuring, Localizing, and Ablating Alignment Signatures in LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30526)
*Aniket Anand,Janvijay Singh,Zhewei Sun,Dilek Hakkani-Tür,Nick Feamster*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文揭示了语言模型的对齐后训练会引入独特的“AI风格”特征，并提出了一种名为PASTA的解码时消融方法，通过去除模型内部的对齐特征方向，在降低AI检测率的同时提升了生成文本的风格多样性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管对齐语言模型普遍表现出一种明显的“AI风格”，但这种风格与后训练（Post-training）过程及模型内部表示之间的关联尚不明确，缺乏对其风格化规律的量化理解与因果验证。

Method: 1. 对比分析：在相同前缀条件下，对比人类文本、基础模型（Base Model）与对齐模型（Aligned Model）的生成结果，评估其AI风格差异。
2. 提出PASTA（Post-training Alignment Signature Targeted Ablation）：一种无需训练的方法，通过计算对齐模型与基础模型在激活空间的残差对比，提取“对齐特征方向”，并在解码过程中对这些方向进行激活消融（Ablation）。
3. 验证：在11个对齐模型与6种AI检测器上进行实验，评估检测率下降效果及文本质量。

Result: 1. 对齐过程确实使生成的文本偏离人类风格，并增加了模型生成内容被AI检测器识别的概率。
2. PASTA方法成功降低了大多数对齐模型的AI检测率，且该效果具有良好的迁移性。
3. 消融后生成的文本在保持相关性和连贯性的同时，展现出更多的风格多样性，证实了AI风格具有可定位的内部特征。

Conclusion: 本文证明了语言模型的对齐后训练过程会引入可识别的“AI风格”，这种风格在模型内部具有可定位的特征方向。通过PASTA方法，研究者能够在不重新训练模型的情况下，通过消融这些特定的激活方向，有效地降低生成内容的AI检测率，同时保持文本的相关性与连贯性。

Abstract: Aligned language models often exhibit a recognizable AI-like style, yet its connection to post-training and internal representations remains poorly understood. In this work, we study whether post-training introduces or amplifies AI-like stylistic regularities and whether these regularities have a localized internal signature. To this end, we compare human text, base-model generations, and aligned-model generations under matched human-source prefixes. Aligned generations show lower human-corpus affinity and higher AI-detection rates than base generations, suggesting that post-training shifts generated text away from human-corpus style and toward detector-visible AI-like text. We then introduce PASTA (Post-training Alignment Signature Targeted Ablation), a training-free method that estimates a post-training alignment signature from aligned-base residual contrasts and ablates the corresponding direction during decoding. Across 11 aligned models and 6 AI detectors, PASTA lowers the detection rate for most aligned models; this effect transfers well across detectors and is not reproduced by random directions. Qualitative analysis suggests that PASTA generations remain relevant and coherent while exhibiting greater stylistic variation. Together, these results show that AI-like stylistic effects of post-training can be measured, localized, and causally tested through activation ablation.

### [140] [DisasterLex: An Expert Concept-to-Schema Knowledge Graph for Geospatial Reasoning in Disaster Analytics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30538)
*Yiming Xiao,Ankit Basu,Kai Yin,Sahil Vartak,Christian Swords,Ali Mostafavi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: DisasterLex 是一种基于专家知识图谱的 Text-to-SQL 框架，通过因果推理和路由机制，显著提升了灾害管理领域复杂地理空间数据库的查询准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前通用 Text-to-SQL 方法难以处理灾害管理领域中高度异构的地理空间数据库模式，且缺乏对复杂灾害因果关系的推理能力，导致灾害应急响应中的数据查询效率低下。

Method: 提出了 DisasterLex 框架，采用知识图谱中介机制，通过四个阶段（实体识别、领域路由、因果推理规划、SQL生成）对用户查询与数据库进行桥接。该方法使用专家知识图谱（EKG）定义概念与因果逻辑，通过概念到表（concept-to-table）的映射限制模型搜索空间，减少不相关模式的干扰。

Result: 在包含36个地理空间表和150个列的灾害分析数据库上，DisasterLex 在7个主流模型上均表现优异，性能指标超过 LightRAG、HippoRAG 2 等四种前沿基准方法 1.4 到 2.75 倍，有效解决了多表合成和领域路由任务中的常见错误。

Conclusion: DisasterLex 通过引入专家知识图谱（EKG）作为中间层，有效解决了通用 Text-to-SQL 方法在灾害领域由于模式复杂和因果关系推理不足而表现不佳的问题，显著提升了灾害管理中结构化数据的查询性能。

Abstract: Disasters are inevitable and increasingly costly, and effective response depends on querying structured tabular data: precise, information-dense records of hazard, exposure, vulnerability, and lifeline infrastructure that underpin disaster management. Current text-to-SQL methods enable natural-language access to such tables but transfer poorly to the disaster domain, where queries span heterogeneous geospatial schemas and require reasoning over causal relations. We introduce DisasterLex, a knowledge-graph-mediated framework that inserts an Expert Knowledge Graph (EKG) of curated concepts and typed causal edges between the user query and the database, bridged to schema by concept-to-table links. The orchestration runs four stages (identifying query entities, routing to the operational domain, planning over causal edges, and grounding the SQL), restricting the schema passed to the model at each step. We instantiate it on a disaster-analytics database (36 geospatial tables, 150 columns) with an EKG of 107 concepts, 117 causal edges, and 52 concept-to-schema links, evaluated on a 75-query test set. On all seven base models spanning proprietary and open-weight families, DisasterLex beats four state-of-the-art baselines (LightRAG, HippoRAG 2, ReFoRCE, CHESS) by 1.4x to 2.75x, with absolute scores of 1.65 to 3.56 (of 5.0). Error analysis shows baseline failures cluster in routing and multi-table SQL composition, the operations our orchestration explicitly addresses. Code, data, and the EKG artifact are available at https://github.com/YimingXiao98/DisasterLex and on Zenodo at https://doi.org/10.5281/zenodo.20388029.

We address these limitations with SubsurfaceGen, a GPU-accelerated generator for 3D velocity models and seismic data. Along with SubsurfaceGen, we release a paired dataset of 4,276 2D velocity slices, 5 s wavefields, and 8 s shot gathers drawn from 42 realistic, field-scale 3D velocity models, each spanning 10 km x 10 km laterally and 6.19 km deep at 10 m resolution. ### [142] [Early Prediction of Future Behavioral Strategy from Process Traces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30550)
*Robert Kasumba,Dennis Barbour,Chien-Ju Ho*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 为了解决自适应系统中难以从有限行为数据中推断个体特质的问题，本研究提出了一种过程级潜在变量模型（PLVM），通过跨任务的过程轨迹融合，实现了对新任务中个体行为策略的早期精准预测。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种过程级潜在变量模型（PLVM）。该模型通过对任务特定行为过程（过程轨迹）进行编码，将其融合到一个共享的个体级潜在表示中，旨在从部分源任务轨迹中推断出可迁移的个体特质，进而预测目标任务中的行为策略。

Conclusion: 本研究证明了利用过程级潜在变量模型（PLVM）能够有效地从部分任务行为中提取跨任务的个体特质，从而实现对新任务中策略行为的早期准确预测，为自适应系统在数据稀缺情况下的个性化决策提供了新的方法论。

Abstract: Adaptive systems often need to make task-specific decisions about people from limited evidence: a tutor may need to anticipate how a learner will approach a new problem, a game may need to adapt when a player enters a new level, and a human-AI system may need to infer whether a partner will persist with a plan or switch goals. These decisions depend on person-level tendencies that shape how people solve related tasks, but such tendencies are difficult to infer from standard behavioral evidence. One approach is to use aggregate outcome summaries, such as scores, completion rates, or productivity; these summaries are compact and available across tasks, but can collapse distinct behavioral processes into similar outcomes. Another approach is to use process-level traces, which record how behavior unfolds; however, process modeling within one task can entangle stable person-level tendencies with task-specific layout and affordances. In this work, we study early cross-task behavioral inference: whether partial source-task process traces can reveal transferable person-level structure that predicts strategy in a held-out target task. We introduce a Process-Level Latent Variable Model (PLVM), which encodes task-specific traces and fuses them into a shared person-level latent representation for cross-task prediction. In PowerWash Simulator, a naturalistic telemetry dataset of human gameplay, PLVM uses partial traces from two cleaning tasks to predict locally persistent Zone Planner behavior versus frequent Zone Hopper behavior in the held-out Fire Station level. Controlled simulations with known latent types show that cross-task fusion helps when source tasks reveal complementary dimensions of a shared latent process. These results suggest that process-level cross-task modeling can support early prediction of target-task strategy when observing sufficient target-task behavior is impractical.

### [143] [Destruction is a General Strategy to Learn Generation; Diffusion's Strength is to Take it Seriously; Exploration is the Future](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30553)
*Pierre-André Noël*

TL;DR: 本文从“破坏与恢复信息”的视角重新审视了扩散模型，论证了其在数据匮乏环境下的优势，并探讨了扩散模型与强化学习结合时的潜力和挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在从更宏观的视角理解扩散模型，探讨其作为一种灵活的数据处理与训练机制的优势，特别是针对数据匮乏场景，并试图解决将强化学习技术引入扩散模型时所面临的理论与实践挑战。

Method: 本文通过将扩散模型归类为一种通过“信息隐藏与恢复”进行训练的技术框架，对比了其与传统人工信息隐藏技术的差异，并引入了一种新的概率图模型来解释扩散过程。同时，通过探讨强化学习在扩散环境中的应用，分析了其中的探索（exploration）问题。

Result: 作者阐述了扩散模型中“破坏信息-恢复信息”的核心逻辑，论证了其相较于传统方法的灵活性；指出了当前强化学习在扩散模型应用中的局限性，并为未来研究方向提供了视角。

Conclusion: 扩散模型提供了一种通过“破坏-生成”过程学习数据的灵活框架，特别是在数据匮乏的情况下具有潜力；此外，将强化学习方法与扩散模型结合时面临探索机制等挑战，需要发展更符合扩散模型特性的原生方法。

Abstract: I present diffusion models as part of a family of machine learning techniques that withhold information from a model's input and train it to guess the withheld information. I argue that diffusion's destroying approach to withholding is more flexible than typical hand-crafted information withholding techniques, providing a rich training playground that could be advantageous in some settings, notably data-scarce ones. I then address subtle issues that may arise when porting reinforcement learning techniques to the diffusion context, and wonder how such exploration problems could be addressed in more diffusion-native ways. I do not have definitive answers, but I do point my fingers in directions I deem interesting. A tutorial follows this thesis, expanding on the destroy-then-generate perspective. A novel kind of probabilistic graphical models is introduced to facilitate the tutorial's exposition.

</details>


### [144] [Zeroth-Order Non-Log-Concave Sampling with Variance Reduction and Applications to Inverse Problems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30573)
*M. Berk Sahin,Behzad Sharif,Abolfazl Hashemi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对高维非对数凹分布在梯度缺失（黑盒）条件下的采样困难，本文提出了一种方差缩减的零阶朗之万采样方法，通过创新的梯度估计器实现了更高的采样稳定性和效率，并首次在理论上证明了其在一般分布及分数生成先验设置下的非渐进收敛性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在高维非对数凹分布采样任务中，当无法获取梯度（黑盒环境）时，现有的采样方法往往存在高方差且缺乏非渐进收敛保证的问题。为了解决这些限制，研究者旨在开发一种高效、稳定且具备理论收敛保证的零阶采样框架。

Method: 该研究提出了一种方差缩减的零阶（Zeroth-Order）朗之万采样方法。该方法采用了一种新型梯度估计器，显著降低了传统批次零阶估计器的方差，并消除了对样本批次规模的维度依赖。此外，还提出了ZO-APMC算法，专门用于结合预训练分数生成先验的黑盒反问题采样。

Result: 1. 建立了首个关于非对数凹分布零阶采样的非渐进收敛保证（基于相对Fisher信息及总变差距离）。2. 建立了首个结合预训练分数生成先验的黑盒反问题采样的非渐进收敛保证。3. 通过合成实验及线性与非线性反问题实验，验证了该方法的理论有效性与强大性能。

Conclusion: 该研究通过引入方差缩减的零阶朗之万采样算法，成功克服了高维非对数凹分布采样中梯度缺失带来的挑战，提供了理论保障并证明了该方法在处理黑盒反问题时的有效性，为基于预训练分数模型的生成先验采样提供了强有力的理论与实践支持。

Abstract: Sampling from high-dimensional, non-log-concave distributions with unnormalized densities remains a fundamental challenge in machine learning, particularly in black-box settings where gradient information is inaccessible or computationally prohibitive. While Langevin dynamics provides a principled framework for sampling when gradients are accessible, its extension to the black-box settings suffers from high variance and lacks non-asymptotic convergence guarantees for non-log-concave sampling. To address these limitations, we propose a variance-reduced zeroth-order Langevin sampling method. Our method employs a gradient estimator that substantially reduces the variance of the classical batched zeroth-order estimator and eliminates the unfavorable dimensional dependence of the batch size required for accurate estimation, enabling practical and stable sampling. We establish the first non-asymptotic convergence guarantees for zeroth-order non-log-concave sampling in terms of $\varepsilon$-relative Fisher information, and, under a Poincaré inequality assumption, squared total variation distance. We further propose ZO-APMC, a posterior sampling algorithm for black-box inverse problems with pre-trained score-based generative priors, establishing the first non-asymptotic convergence guarantees for such methods. We validate our theory through synthetic experiments and demonstrate strong empirical performance on practical linear and nonlinear inverse problems.

### [145] [Counterfactual Evaluation Reveals Hidden Capability Profiles in Clinical LLMs and Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30590)
*Matt Turk*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文指出临床AI的传统覆盖率评估指标存在局限性，提出了一种名为“因果敏感度评分（CSS）”的干预性指标。研究发现CSS能揭示传统指标无法发现的模型临床响应盲点和结构性缺陷，并能有效评估模型对临床变化的实际处理能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的临床AI评估体系多基于覆盖率（如CMS），导致看似得分相似的模型在实际临床输入变化时表现迥异。为了解决这种评估指标与实际临床响应能力脱节的问题，研究旨在建立一种能够捕捉模型因果敏感性与响应性的评估框架。

Method: 研究团队提出了因果敏感度评分（CSS）这一预注册的干预性评估指标。CSS通过对肿瘤学案例进行五种临床维度（生物标志物、既往治疗失败、手术状态等）的变异扰动，测量模型在面对临床信号改变时是否能做出正确的更新，并采用{0, 0.5, 1.0}的评分量表进行量化。同时，研究对比了CSS与传统的共识匹配分数（CMS），并探索了其在ReAct风格智能体中的应用。

Result: 研究发现，CSS与CMS的评估排名近乎相反，且现有模型在手术状态干预上表现出普遍的盲点（CSS最高仅17.2%），这一问题在传统CMS评估中完全无法察觉。此外，CSS揭示了即便智能体调用了正确工具，部分模型仍存在结构性响应缺失的深层问题。实验通过交叉裁判和医学专业人士验证，证明了CSS的有效性与可靠性。

Conclusion: 基于覆盖率的传统评估指标（如CMS）在评估临床AI时存在严重的局限性，无法反映模型对临床变数的敏感性和响应能力。因果敏感度评分（CSS）作为一种补充指标，能有效揭示模型的结构性缺陷和响应盲区，是未来临床AI评估与强化学习奖励设计的关键工具。

Abstract: Two clinical AI systems can score nearly identically on coverage-based rubrics yet behave radically differently when their patient inputs change: one updates its recommendations to match the new clinical signal, while the other produces the same output regardless. We introduce the Causal Sensitivity Score (CSS), a pre-registered interventional metric that mutates oncology tumor-board cases along five clinically meaningful dimensions - biomarker flips, prior-treatment failures, biomarker removals, surgery-status changes, and stage perturbations - and scores whether each model updates its recommendations in the pre-registered correct direction using a {0, 0.5, 1.0} scale. Benchmarked against the Consensus Match Score (CMS), a coverage-based weighted recall metric, six frontier models from three labs evaluated in single-shot inference across 224 cases rank in nearly opposite orders: all six models change rank, the CMS-worst model becomes CSS-best, and one upper-mid CMS model ranks last on CSS. We further surface a universal safety blind spot: every frontier model fails on surgery-status interventions (at most 17.2% CSS on Family D), a finding CMS does not expose. The metric also transfers to tool-using agents: in a ReAct-style experiment, tool use improves CSS for five of six models (+2.5 to +20.3 percentage points), yet the lowest-CSS model retrieves the same chart sections and still fails to update its recommendations - revealing a structural responsiveness deficit visible only under counterfactual evaluation. Cross-judge replication and three-rater medical-professional validation confirm the aggregate findings. Interventional pre-registered metrics like CSS complement coverage-based evaluation for clinical AI agents: they capture responsiveness that coverage metrics miss and offer a candidate dense reward signal for future agentic RL systems.

TL;DR: 针对发动机健康管理中数据复杂且缺乏不确定性评估的问题，提出了一种联合预测性能指标与剩余寿命（RUL）的多任务深度学习框架，实现了高精度的区间预测，助力风险感知型运维决策。

Method: 提出了一种多任务科学机器学习架构，采用共享序列编码器（包含卷积层、残差双向LSTM层及注意力池化层）提取通用特征，并分支连接任务专用头。其中包括用于概率回归的均值-方差估计模块以及用于阈值事件建模的生存分析头，能够同时输出TGTU、DTGT和RUL的预测值及置信区间。

Conclusion: 该论文提出的多任务科学机器学习框架，通过联合预测涡轮性能指标和剩余寿命，并量化预测不确定性，能够有效应对工业领域异构且非平稳的飞行数据。该框架的灵活性和可调性使其能够紧密结合企业的维护策略，从而为风险感知型的资产健康管理提供可靠的决策支持。

Abstract: Engine Health Management (EHM) depends on reliable forecasting of Remaining Useful Life (RUL) and on tracking thermal indicators such as turbine gas temperature (TGT). In practice, real-world fleet data are heterogeneous and non-stationary, and point predictions alone are insufficient for risk-aware maintenance decisions. This paper presents a multi-task scientific machine learning framework for turbine prognostics that jointly predicts turbine gas temperature untrimmed (TGTU), Delta Turbine Gas Temperature (DTGT), and RUL, with quantified uncertainty in the form of prediction intervals whose empirical coverage is evaluated. A shared sequence encoder (convolutional front-end with residual bidirectional LSTM layers and attention pooling) feeds task-specific heads, including mean--variance estimation for probabilistic regression and, optionally, a survival head for threshold-based event modeling. The framework is designed to be tunable via a small set of practitioner-facing parameters (e.g., DTGT thresholding rules and RUL target construction) so that deployment can align with in-house policies and proprietary criteria. The predictive performance of the proposed framework is evaluated using both point and interval metrics, including mean absolute error (MAE), prediction interval coverage probability (PICP), mean prediction interval width (MPIW), and the coverage--width criterion (CWC). Results are reported both in aggregate and stratified by flight phase and maintenance segment to highlight operational-context effects and to support uncertainty-aware monitoring.

### [147] [ScaleMAP: Preserving Local Density and Neighborhood Structure in Low-Dimensional Embeddings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30597)
*Rajas Poorna,Marcus T. Cicerone*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: ScaleMAP 是一种新型的降维尺度恢复技术，通过变量代换而非竞争目标函数，在保留 UMAP 高质量邻域结构的同时，有效恢复了数据中的稀疏特征和全局密度分布。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的非线性降维方法（如 UMAP 和 PaCMAP）在构建图时会自适应地归一化局部距离，导致原始数据的尺度信息丢失，从而破坏了稀疏结构（如细胞发育轨迹中的桥接结构）和窄光谱峰值的特征表现。虽有 DensMAP 尝试修复，但其惩罚项会与原有的吸引-排斥力产生冲突，造成分布散乱。

Method: ScaleMAP 在嵌入优化过程中引入了一个新变量，将每对点的嵌入位移除以它们在原始空间中局部半径的几何平均值。这种方法通过变量代换将原始空间的尺度信息重新注入到嵌入空间中，而非像 DensMAP 那样添加相互竞争的惩罚项。

Result: 在多个基准测试及生物学数据集（转录组学、高光谱成像、流式细胞术）上，ScaleMAP 在保持 UMAP 级别邻域保留能力的同时，实现了与 DensMAP 相当的密度保留效果，且能有效恢复稀疏桥接结构并精确表征跨越 17 个数量级的密度分布。该方法应用于 PaCMAP 同样有效，证明了其泛化性。

Conclusion: ScaleMAP 提出了一种通过坐标变换而非竞争性目标函数来注入尺度信息的方法，成功解决了现有降维算法在保持邻域结构的同时丢失原始数据密度和尺度信息的问题，并具有良好的泛化能力。

Abstract: Nonlinear dimensionality-reduction methods such as UMAP and PaCMAP adaptively normalize local distances during graph construction, erasing neighborhood scale from the data. This distorts more than relative cluster sizes: sparse structures like bridges between transitioning cell types and narrow spectral spikes in hyperspectral images can be suppressed or lost entirely. DensMAP adds a density penalty to correct this, but this penalty competes with UMAP's attraction-repulsion forces, scattering points far from their neighborhoods. ScaleMAP takes a different approach: each pairwise embedding displacement is divided by the geometric mean of the two endpoints' original-space local radii, re-injecting scale information as a change of variables rather than as a competing objective. Across standard benchmarks and scientific datasets from transcriptomics, hyperspectral imaging, and flow cytometry, ScaleMAP matches DensMAP on density preservation while maintaining UMAP-level neighborhood preservation. In transcriptomic data, it recovers sparse bridges between cell populations that UMAP collapses; in flow cytometry, it faithfully represents density structure across 17 orders of magnitude. The same principle applied to PaCMAP yields consistently improved density preservation, suggesting the approach generalizes beyond UMAP.

</details>


### [148] [AMNESIA: A Large Scale Medical Unlearning Benchmark Suite with Disease-Informed Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30599)
*Saeedeh Davoudi,Reihaneh Iranmanesh,Ophir Frieder,Nazli Goharian*

Main category: cs.LG

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 医学知识不断更新，医疗大语言模型需要具备删除特定训练数据（如过期或敏感信息）的能力。然而，现有的遗忘基准多基于合成或小规模通用数据，缺乏针对临床环境的深入研究。

Method: 作者提出了一个名为AMNESIA的大规模开源医学遗忘基准，包含来自11个疾病类别的8820份患者笔记，共70560个问答对。研究评估了四种主流遗忘方法在患者级和疾病级的表现，并引入了一项检测医疗术语泄露的新指标。

Result: 实验发现，在遗忘单个患者信息时，模型往往会同时损失同一病症下其他患者的相关知识（即知识侵蚀现象），这突显了当前遗忘方法在保持医学知识准确性与区分度方面的不足。

Conclusion: 现有的机器遗忘方法在处理医疗数据时存在明显的局限性，特别是在删除特定患者信息时，往往会误删该病症的通用临床知识。研究表明，需要开发能够更好地区分个体数据与共享临床知识的遗忘技术。

Abstract: Medical knowledge is continuously evolving. This creates a need to update or selectively forget information encoded in already-trained medical LLMs. Machine unlearning aims to remove the influence of specific training data from a model without full retraining. Yet, existing unlearning benchmarks rely on synthetic or small-scale general data, leaving clinical unlearning understudied. We introduce AMNESIA, the first large-scale, open source benchmark for medical unlearning, with 70,560 question-answer pairs from 8,820 patient notes across 11 disease categories. AMNESIA includes both factual questions testing direct recall and reasoning questions testing clinical inference. We use it to evaluate four widely used unlearning methods at both random patient and disease-level, and introduce a new metric for detecting leakage of medical terminology. We show that unlearning individual patients erodes knowledge of others with the same condition, calling for methods that can better separate patients from shared clinical knowledge.

### [149] [The Fast Mixing Mechanism for Differential Privacy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30600)
*Omri Lev,Moshe Shenfeld,Vishwak Srinivasan,Katrina Ligett,Ashia C. Wilson*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了首个高效的差分隐私普通最小二乘法，通过引入基于快速变换的差分隐私草图机制，在保证隐私和精度的同时，显著提升了算法的运行效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的差分隐私线性回归方法虽然具备良好的 utility 保障，但在计算效率（运行时长）上未能突破传统方法的限制，缺乏在保持精度的同时大幅提升速度的高效算法。

Method: 利用快速变换（Fast Transforms）构建差分隐私草图机制，替代传统的耗时高斯草图，并结合现代草图算法实现差分隐私线性回归。

Result: 在特定场景下实现了与经典快速草图方法相媲美的计算速度，同时在隐私保证上达到了最先进水平，与高斯草图在常数因子内相当。该算法在差分隐私最小二乘法中展现了优异的性能。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一种基于快速变换的差分隐私草图算法，成功在保持高精度 utility 的前提下，显著降低了差分隐私线性回归的计算复杂度，实现了该领域首个高效的普通最小二乘法算法。

Abstract: Randomized sketching is a central tool for compressing large-scale optimization problems while preserving accuracy. In particular, sketches that are based on structured matrices, such as the Hadamard matrix, can be applied efficiently and often yield solutions that approximate those of the original problem at much lower computational cost. In differential privacy (DP), Gaussian sketching has been used to solve DP linear regression, beginning with \citet{sheffet2017differentially, sheffet2019old} and later refined by \citet{lev2025gaussianmix, lev2026near}. However, although these methods achieve strong utility guarantees, they usually do not improve runtime over classical DP approaches. In this work, we introduce a new DP sketching mechanism based on fast transforms, which, in certain cases, matches the runtime of classical fast sketching methods. We prove state-of-the-art privacy guarantees for this mechanism and show that, in favorable regimes, they match those of the Gaussian sketch up to a constant factor. As an application, we combine this mechanism with recent sketch-based methods for DP linear regression to obtain a new algorithm with strong utility and improved runtime. We establish privacy and accuracy guarantees for this algorithm, yielding, to the best of our knowledge, the first fast method for DP ordinary least squares.

### [150] [Constrained Flow Optimization via Sequential Fine Tuning for Molecular Design](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30610)
*Sven Gutjahr,Riccardo De Santi,Luca Schaufelberger,Kjell Jorner,Andreas Krause*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种名为CFO的约束流优化算法，通过数学框架严谨地解决了生成式模型在优化奖励的同时必须满足特定约束的难题，实现了在科研任务中平衡效果与可行性的目标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在分子设计和蛋白质工程等领域，如何让生成式模型在优化奖励函数（如结合亲和力）的同时，严格满足现实约束（如可合成性），且实现方式可靠、可控，是目前算法层面亟待解决的挑战。

Method: 研究者提出了一套严谨的“约束生成优化”（Constrained Generative Optimization）框架，并开发了“约束流优化”（Constrained Flow Optimization, CFO）算法。CFO通过将原始任务简化为一系列可扩展的微调过程，利用优化视角自动且可证明地平衡奖励最大化与约束满足。

Result: 实验结果表明，CFO算法在合成基准测试和真实分子设计任务中表现优异，能够稳定提升奖励值，并始终保持极高的约束满足率，验证了其在实际科学应用中的实用价值和收敛保证。

Conclusion: 该研究成功将约束生成优化问题转化为可控的序列微调问题，并通过CFO算法在理论和实验上证明了在保证约束满足的同时实现奖励最大化的可行性，为生成式模型在科学发现中的应用提供了可靠的框架。

Abstract: Adapting generative foundation models, in particular diffusion and flow models, to optimize given reward functions (e.g., binding affinity) while satisfying constraints (e.g., molecular synthesizability) is fundamental for their adoption in real-world scientific discovery applications such as molecular design or protein engineering. While recent works have introduced scalable methods for reward-guided fine-tuning of such models via reinforcement learning and control schemes, it remains an open problem how to algorithmically trade-off reward maximization and constraint satisfaction in a reliable and predictable manner. Motivated by this challenge, we first present a rigorous framework for Constrained Generative Optimization, which brings an optimization viewpoint to the introduced adaptation problem and retrieves the relevant task of constrained generation as a sub-case. Then, we introduce Constrained Flow Optimization (CFO), an algorithm that automatically and provably balances reward maximization and constraint satisfaction by reducing the original problem to sequential fine-tuning via established, scalable methods. We provide convergence guarantees for constrained generative optimization and constrained generation via CFO. Ultimately, we present an experimental evaluation of CFO on both synthetic, yet illustrative, settings, and a molecular design task. Across these evaluations, CFO achieves consistent increases in reward while ensuring high constraint satisfaction, showcasing its practical utility for constrained generative optimization.

### [151] [Improving Selective Classification with Pairwise Queries for Binary Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30615)

TL;DR: 针对大语言模型置信度估计不准导致的选择性分类误差问题，本文提出了一种利用成对查询（pairwise queries）来识别高风险样本的策略，显著提升了分类的可靠性和效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在大语言模型的上下文学习（in-context learning）中，模型自身的置信度估计往往与其实际预测表现不一致，导致模型在选择性分类时错误率较高，进而浪费昂贵的人工标注资源。

Method: 提出了一种利用模型进行额外成对查询的方法。通过比较样本对的相对置信度或一致性，识别高错误风险的样本，并将其纳入选择性分类机制中，以此改进仅依赖模型原始置信度（如预测logits）的拒绝策略。

Result: 理论分析证明了成对查询在特定条件下优于单纯的置信度估计。在1个合成数据集和4个真实二分类任务上的实验表明，基于成对查询的算法在所有情况下均获得了更优的精度-成本权衡。

Conclusion: 通过引入成对查询（pairwise queries），本文提供了一种比传统置信度估计更可靠的方法来优化大语言模型的选择性分类，在降低非拒绝样本误差的同时实现了更好的精度-成本权衡。

Abstract: In selective classification, a model predicts the labels of data samples where it is confident, and abstains from predicting labels for samples on which it is not confident. The rejected samples are often labeled by an expert, which is expensive. The budget for the expert is best utilized when the model has low error on non-rejected samples. However, the estimate of a model's confidence might be inconsistent with the model's predictions, which can lead to high error on non-rejected points. Such situations can readily occur in in-context binary classification by LLMs. To remedy this, we propose making additional pairwise queries to the same model. These pairwise queries can detect high-error samples and be incorporated into selective classification techniques to reduce the error on non-rejected samples. Theoretically, we establish the conditions under which a simple algorithm using pairwise queries outperforms an inconsistent confidence estimate. We support this insight through extensive experiments for $1$ synthetic and $4$ in-context learning-based real binary classification datasets. In all these cases, we show that our algorithms, using pairwise queries, obtain a better accuracy-cost tradeoff than using only the raw confidence estimates, for instance, the LLM's next-token logits.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在单细胞生物学等领域，从稀疏快照中推断连续概率路径面临挑战，且目前缺乏针对Wasserstein空间（概率测度空间）中分布演化轨迹的主动学习策略，特别是现有插值方法无法有效量化认知不确定性。

Method: 利用线性化最优传输（Linearized Optimal Transport, LOT）将分布快照映射到切空间，使其能够应用高斯过程进行建模，从而构建了一个可处理的概率替代模型，并据此设计了通过最小化路径不确定性来选择最优测量时间的实验策略。

Result: 实验结果表明，该主动学习策略在合成数据集和真实数据集上均显著优于传统的无不确定性感知基准方法，能够更高效地通过稀疏观测重建概率路径。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一种在Wasserstein空间中进行主动学习的新颖框架，通过线性化最优传输（LOT）成功将分布路径问题转化为高斯过程回归问题，证明了在分布空间中量化认知不确定性并指导最优观测时间选择的可行性与优越性。

Abstract: Inferring continuous probability paths from sparse snapshots is a fundamental challenge in domains like single-cell biology, where high-fidelity data acquisition is often destructive and constrained by prohibitive sequencing costs. This motivates the need for active learning strategies to strategically select optimal measurement times. However, designing active learning policies for this setting remains an open problem: the target objects reside on the infinite dimensional Wasserstein space where standard Euclidean metrics are ill-defined, and current interpolation methods lack epistemic uncertainty quantification. We introduce a framework which extends active experimentation to the space of measures. By leveraging Linearized Optimal Transport (LOT), we map distributional snapshots into a tangent space amenable to Gaussian Process modeling, allowing us to construct a tractable probabilistic surrogate for the underlying probability path. This yields an acquisition policy that iteratively selects measurement times to minimize uncertainty. Empirical results demonstrate that our strategy outperforms uncertainty-agnostic baselines on both synthetic and real-world datasets.

### [153] [CellBRIDGE: Learning Cellular Trajectories via Interaction-Aware Alignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30635)
*Silas Ruhrberg Estévez,Nicolas Huynh,Tennison Liu,Roderik M. Kortlever,Gerard I. Evan,David L. Bentley,Mihaela van der Schaar*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 单细胞 RNA 测序（scRNA-seq）具有破坏性，无法直接追踪个体细胞的时间演化，导致轨迹推断存在不确定性。现有的最优传输方法多依赖于基因表达距离，忽略了细胞间复杂的相互作用（配体-受体信号传导），从而限制了推断结果的生物学合理性。

Method: 提出了一种名为 CellBRIDGE 的方法。它在传统基于特征（基因表达距离）的最优传输（OT）模型基础上，引入了基于配体-受体活性的定向、类型化相互作用成本项，从而将细胞间的通讯结构显式地建模到快照对齐过程中。

Result: 在合成和真实的 scRNA-seq 数据集上，CellBRIDGE 相比仅基于特征的基准方法，显著提升了快照间的耦合精度和轨迹估计质量；此外，该方法还能通过硅片扰动（in silico perturbations）模拟特定的配体-受体抑制，并成功复现了生物学预期的轨迹改变。

Conclusion: CellBRIDGE 通过将细胞间通讯（配体-受体相互作用）融入最优传输框架，有效提升了单细胞动态推断的准确性和生物学解释性，为研究细胞分化与药物干预效应提供了一种强有力的计算工具。

Abstract: Inferring dynamics from population snapshots is a fundamental challenge in machine learning and biology. In scRNA-sequencing (scRNA-seq), destructive measurements preclude direct tracking of individual cells across time, making trajectory inference underdetermined. Optimal Transport (OT) provides a principled framework for snapshot alignment, but a long-standing modeling question is which cost functions yield biologically meaningful couplings. Standard OT approaches rely on gene-expression distances, implicitly treating cells as independent points and neglecting structured cell-cell communication mediated by ligand-receptor signaling. We introduce CellBRIDGE (Cell-Based Regularized Interaction-Driven Gene Expression), which augments feature-based OT with a directed, typed interaction cost derived from ligand-receptor activity. By explicitly modeling cell-cell communication, CellBRIDGE improves cross-snapshot couplings and downstream trajectory estimates across synthetic and real scRNA-seq datasets relative to feature-only baselines. Notably, CellBRIDGE enables mechanistically interpretable in silico perturbations: on lung cancer data, silencing specific ligand-receptor pairs induces trajectory shifts that recapitulate expected effects of targeted pathway inhibition.

### [154] [Score Broadcast and Decorrelation: A General Framework for Broadcast-Based Credit Assignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30638)
*Mustafa Uzun,Mete Erdogan,Cengiz Pehlevan,Alper T. Erdogan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了SBD框架，通过利用损失函数得分与隐藏层激活的正交性，将生物学上合理的误差广播方法推广至通用可微损失函数，并为三因子学习规则提供了理论支撑，有效提升了训练性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的反向传播算法由于需要权重转置（weight transport），在生物学上不具备合理性。现有的误差广播方法（如EBD）多局限于均方误差（MSE），缺乏对更广泛损失函数族的通用理论支撑。本文旨在建立一个统一的理论框架，解决通用可微损失下的广播式信用分配问题。

Method: 提出了“评分广播与去相关”（SBD）框架，利用最优得分与隐藏层激活之间的正交性原理，将误差广播推广至交叉熵、Bregman散度等通用损失函数。同时，引入了“得分向量扩展”（score vector expansion）技术，在保持正交性框架的前提下增强了广播信号的表征能力。

Result: 在CIFAR-10和Tiny ImageNet数据集上的实验表明，SBD显著优于现有的误差广播方法，且得分向量扩展进一步提升了模型的性能，验证了该框架在深度学习中的有效性。

Conclusion: SBD框架通过将损失函数的得分（Score）作为广播信号，成功将基于生物学启发的误差广播机制推广到了广泛的可微损失函数族，并为神经科学中的三因子学习规则提供了严谨的数学基础。

Abstract: We introduce Score Broadcast and Decorrelation (SBD), a principled framework for broadcast-based credit assignment for general families of differentiable losses. Error broadcast is a biologically plausible alternative to backpropagation that sends output information to hidden layers without weight transport. The Error Broadcast and Decorrelation (EBD) framework, recently introduced for the mean-squared-error (MSE) setting, grounded this mechanism in the stochastic orthogonality of optimal estimators, under which the optimal residual is orthogonal to functions of the input. We generalize that foundation by introducing an orthogonality principle between the output score (the gradient of loss with respect to the final-layer output) and hidden-layer activations, which holds whenever the optimal score has conditional mean zero. This single principle unifies broadcast-based credit assignment across the standard differentiable-loss families, including cross-entropy, Bregman divergences, proper scoring rules, and exponential-family negative log-likelihoods. The framework supplies a theoretical grounding for the three-factor learning rule under general losses, with the neuromodulatory factor derived as the broadcast loss score. We derive the cross-entropy case explicitly, characterize the admissible loss class, and introduce a score vector expansion technique that enriches the broadcast signal while preserving the orthogonality framework. Experiments on CIFAR-10 and Tiny ImageNet show that SBD substantially improves over existing broadcast approaches, with score vector expansion delivering further gains. Overall, this work identifies the loss score as the signal to broadcast, supplies the orthogonality theory and theoretical grounding for the three-factor learning rule from neuroscience, and shows how score vector expansion enriches the decorrelation directions of the resulting objective.

</details>


### [155] [CSULoRA: Closest Safe Update Low-Rank Adaptation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30640)
*Oleksandr Marchenko Breneur,Adelaide Danilov,Aria Nourbakhsh,Salima Lamsiyah*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: CSULoRA 是一种用于修正 LoRA 适配器的后验防御方法，通过估计安全子空间并对更新进行平滑正则化，在保护大语言模型安全性的同时最大程度维持了微调后的任务性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的 LoRA 微调容易受到少量不安全或对抗性数据的攻击，导致对齐模型的安全性下降；而现有的防御方法（如投影、剪枝等）往往会牺牲任务相关信息或需要额外的训练步骤，缺乏效率和灵活性。

Method: 提出了 CSULoRA（Closest Safe Update Estimation），这是一种事后（post-hoc）修正方法。该方法首先通过基础模型与安全对齐模型之间的权重位移估计出一个安全子空间，然后将 LoRA 更新分解为完全对齐、部分对齐和空间外分量，并通过求解一个闭式惩罚最小化问题，在保留对齐分量的同时，根据能量比例平滑衰减不安全的更新方向。

Result: 在对抗性微调实验中，CSULoRA 在显著降低攻击成功率的同时，依然保留了标准 LoRA 微调所获得的大部分任务效能。

Conclusion: CSULoRA 证明了通过后验估计安全子空间并对 LoRA 更新进行正则化处理，可以在不对模型进行额外训练或硬性剪枝的前提下，有效防御针对对齐模型的对抗性微调，从而在保持模型效能的同时提升安全性。

Abstract: Low-rank adaptation has become a standard method for parameter-efficient fine-tuning of large language models, but even small amounts of unsafe or adversarial fine-tuning data can substantially weaken the safety behavior of aligned models. Existing safety-preserving LoRA methods often rely on hard interventions such as projection, pruning, thresholding, or additional training objectives. While these methods can suppress unsafe update directions, they may also remove task-relevant information or require extra tuning. We introduce CSULoRA, a post-hoc method for correcting trained LoRA adapters through closest safe update estimation. CSULoRA estimates a safety-aligned subspace from the weight displacement between a safety-aligned model and its corresponding base checkpoint. It then decomposes each LoRA update into fully aligned, partially aligned, and off-subspace components. Instead of discarding components outside the estimated safety subspace, CSULoRA solves a closed-form penalized minimum-change problem that preserves the fully aligned component while smoothly attenuating potentially unsafe directions according to their relative energy. In adversarial fine-tuning experiments, CSULoRA substantially reduces attack success rate while preserving most of the utility gains obtained from standard LoRA fine-tuning.
