<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管强化学习在仿真环境下对工业能源系统优化表现出色，但在真实工业场景下的部署和应用仍面临诸多限制，缺乏从理论到实际应用的系统性分析，因此迫切需要探究其在真实热力网应用中的落地挑战。

Method: 将工业热网控制问题形式化为马尔可夫决策过程（MDP），并从状态感知（部分可观测性）、动作空间设计、奖励函数设计以及“仿真到现实”（Sim-to-Real）的差距这四个维度系统性地分析了在现实工业环境中部署强化学习所面临的挑战。

Result: 研究发现，尽管强化学习在实际工业热网中能够维持操作稳定性，但其性能表现与仿真环境相比存在显著差距，验证了在真实部署过程中面临的复杂性和技术瓶颈。

Conclusion: 在真实工业热力网中部署强化学习是可行的，能够实现运行稳定性，但目前仍面临现实环境带来的巨大性能差距。该研究强调了从仿真走向现实时，必须解决模型与真实系统之间的差异以及环境的复杂性。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning has shown promising results for optimizing the control of industrial energy systems, yet most existing studies remain limited to the application in simulation environments. We investigate the challenges of deploying reinforcement learning in a real-world industrial energy system, considering a thermal heating network as a use case. We formulate the task as a Markov Decision Process and systematically analyze the associated challenges along the structure of the formal description, including partial observability, action space design, reward design, and the simulation-to-reality gap. The challenges are grounded in an existing real-world deployment, where reinforcement learning achieves operational stability but shows a significant performance gap compared to simulation.

### [201] [dashi: A Python library for Dataset Shift Characterization to Support Trustworthy AI Development and Deployment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31360)
*David Fernández-Narro,Pablo Ferri,Ángel Sánchez-García,Juan M. García-Gómez,Carlos Sáez*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文介绍了 dashi，一个用于探索、量化和表征数据集偏移的开源 Python 库，旨在通过无监督（信息几何）和有监督分析手段，提升医疗 AI 生命周期的稳健性与安全性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在 AI 开发与应用过程中，数据集偏移（训练集与测试集分布不一致）会导致模型性能严重下降，在对安全性要求极高的医疗 AI 领域，这种偏移可能直接影响患者安全。目前虽有理论基础，但缺乏易于使用且全面的软件工具来分析这些偏移，因此作者开发了 dashi。

Method: dashi 采用了双重分析策略：1. 无监督方法：基于信息几何和非参数统计流形技术，对数据变异性进行表征和分析（如信息几何时间图、全局概率偏差等指标）；2. 有监督方法：通过评估用户定义的时序或跨源批次，量化模型性能随数据偏移的衰减情况。该库还提供了交互式视觉分析功能。

Result: 作者通过妊娠糖尿病、COVID-19 和急救医疗调度三个真实及模拟的医疗 AI 案例，验证了 dashi 在量化数据相干性、检测模型性能衰减以及提供可解释性视觉分析方面的有效性。

Conclusion: dashi 通过提供一套开源且全面的工具，弥补了现有工具在数据集偏移分析方面的空白。它通过量化数据变异性和模型性能衰减，有效提升了 AI 生命周期的可信度，为构建健壮、安全的医疗 AI 管道提供了关键支持。

Abstract: The Artificial Intelligence (AI) life cycle requires a thorough understanding of the underlying data dynamics for robust, safe and cost-effective AI development and use. Dataset shifts are defined as changes between train and test data distributions. Whether occurring over time (temporal) or across different sites (multi-source), they can severely degrade model performance and compromise data quality. This is particularly important in health AI, where the safety and fundamental rights of patients can be severely affected by uncontrolled shifts both at training and operational stages. While the theoretical foundations of covariate, prior, and concept shifts are well established, there is a lack of accessible and comprehensive software tools to perform their analysis. We introduce dashi, an open-source Python library designed for the exploration, quantification, and characterization of dataset shifts. dashi provides a dual approach: an unsupervised approach that leverages information geometry and non-parametric statistical manifolds to data variability characterization and analysis (e.g., Information Geometric Temporal plots and Multi-Source Variability metrics like Global Probabilistic Deviation and Source Probabilistic Outlyingness), and a supervised approach that quantifies and characterizes model performance degradation. Both unsupervised and supervised approaches work across user-defined temporal and domain/source batches. We demonstrate the utility of dashi on three simulated and real-world health AI case studies on gestational diabetes mellitus, COVID-19 and emergency medical dispatch. By providing interactive visual analytics and variability metrics, dashi supports trustworthiness of AI life cycle stages enabling robust and safe machine learning pipelines through the assessment of data coherence and AI performance.

Result: 理论分析表明，该方法在温和的假设条件下比传统BO具有更快的收敛速度。在合成基准测试和实际应用基准测试中的广泛实验也进一步验证了该方法的有效性和优越性。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一种将最佳臂识别（BAI）与信任域贝叶斯优化相结合的轨迹感知框架。理论分析与实验结果均表明，该方法能够有效提升在高维或多峰优化问题中的搜索效率与收敛速度，证明了通过预测优化轨迹来动态筛选搜索区域的策略是处理复杂黑盒优化问题的有效途径。

Abstract: Gaussian process-based Bayesian optimization (BO) is a popular approach for expensive black-box optimization, but its performance often degrades on complex multimodal or high-dimensional problems. Trust region-based BO mitigates this issue by focusing on local regions, and recent studies suggest that selecting an effective region can be formulated as a multi-armed bandit problem. We propose a trajectory-aware framework that integrates best-arm identification (BAI) with trust region-based BO to efficiently solve multimodal optimization problems. Our method extrapolates the optimization trajectories of multiple locally initialized optimizers to predict their final performance and progressively eliminates suboptimal candidates via BAI. We theoretically show that the proposed BAI-guided BO converges faster to the global optimum than conventional BO under mild assumptions, and demonstrate its effectiveness through extensive experiments on synthetic and real-world benchmarks.

### [203] [Learning to Bid in FCR Markets: A Best-of-Both-Worlds Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31070)
*Marius Potfer,Cheng Wan,Pierre Gruet*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 研究人员提出了一种适用于欧洲FCR市场的在线学习投标算法，通过将市场清算转化为组合半强盗学习问题，实现了在随机和对抗环境下高效的投标决策，并在真实历史数据中验证了其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 欧洲FCR（频率控制储备）市场的参与者面临信息不对称（竞争对手报价不可见）和反馈有限（仅能观测清算价格和中标量）的挑战，导致投标决策困难。亟需一种在不完全信息下能够有效自适应学习的投标策略。

Method: 将欧洲多国FCR市场结算问题转化为针对内生对手报价向量的重复多单元统一价格拍卖问题；引入并适配了一种“两全其美”（Best-of-Both-Worlds）的组合半强盗（Combinatorial Semi-Bandit）算法，仅需市场提供的清算价格和中标量等标准反馈即可实现。

Result: 该算法在随机环境中实现了对数级伪遗憾（logarithmic pseudo-regret），在对抗性环境中实现了O(√T)遗憾。合成实验证实了其扩展性，历史数据回测表明其在稳定产品上表现优异，且在实践中具备竞争力。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了基于学习的投标策略在欧洲FCR市场中不仅具备坚实的理论基础，而且在实践中具有可行性。该方法在稳定市场环境下表现卓越，但在市场波动剧烈时需要结合特定算法策略以平衡性能与鲁棒性。

Abstract: Bidding in the European Frequency Containment Reserve (FCR) market is challenging for flexibility providers because competing offers are hidden and bidders observe only partial feedback form the market, such as, clearing price and awarded quantity. For a participant active in a single country, we show that the multi-country FCR clearing problem can be recast as a repeated multi-unit uniform-price auction against an endogenous vector of opposing bids. This reformulation yields an online learning problem and allows us to adapt a Best-of-Both-Worlds combinatorial semi-bandit algorithm implementable from this standard market feedback. The resulting bidder achieves logarithmic pseudo-regret in stochastic environments and $\mathcal{O}(\sqrt{T})$ regret in adversarial ones. Synthetic experiments confirm the expected scaling, and backtests on historical European FCR data show competitive performance in practice: the method performs especially well on stable products, while EXP3-type baselines can be safer under stronger non-stationarity. Overall, the results show that learning-based bidding in FCR markets is theoretically grounded and practically useful when the learning rule matches product-level market stability.

### [204] [Subspace-Decomposed JEPAs: Disentangling Progression and Content in Latent World Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31111)
*Lucas Thil,Jesse Read,Rim Kaddah,Guillaume Doquet*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 研究者提出了一种名为SD-JEPA的方法，通过将潜空间解耦为“进度”与“内容”两个正交子空间，使模型在保持强大预测能力的同时，能精确追踪任务进度并识别关键语义事件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的联合嵌入预测架构（JEPA）虽然能学习到紧凑的潜在世界模型，但缺乏专门用于编码“任务进度”的机制，导致难以直观地追踪任务执行状态或识别语义上的关键时刻。

Method: 提出SD-JEPA方法，将JEPA的潜空间划分为两个正交子空间：一是通过余弦间隔三元组损失（cosine-margin triplet loss）训练的低维进度子空间；二是通过既有的SIGReg目标正则化的高维内容子空间。通过证明两者的反坍缩力作用于不相交的坐标轴，实现了两个目标的相加式优化，避免了竞争。

Result: SD-JEPA在多个控制基准测试中优于LeWM基线，并在Push-T任务上超越了最强非LeWM的JEPA基线。实验表明，进度子空间（仅占潜在空间的4.2%）能解释72-95%的任务进度方差，且在定位语义事件时的AUC显著优于传统的预测误差指标。

Conclusion: 本研究提出的SD-JEPA通过将表征空间解耦为进度子空间和内容子空间，成功解决了JEPA在任务进度追踪上的局限。该方法不仅在控制任务性能上优于基线，还提供了一个具有可解释性的“语义指南针”，能有效量化任务进度并检测语义事件。

Abstract: Joint-Embedding Predictive Architectures (JEPAs) learn compact latent world models by predicting future embeddings, but no single coordinate of the latent is designated to encode task progression. We carve the JEPA latent into two orthogonal subspaces with disjoint roles: a low-dimensional progression subspace shaped by a cosine-margin triplet loss, and a high-dimensional content subspace regularised by the existing SIGReg objective of LeWM. We prove that the two anti-collapse forces act on disjoint coordinates, so they compose additively rather than competing on the same dimensions. Our method, SD-JEPA improves over the LeWM baseline on the majority of its control benchmarks at matched compute, and outperforms the strongest non-LeWM JEPA baseline on Push-T; a subspace-ablation falsifier confirms the split is the load-bearing ingredient. Beyond planning, the resulting 1-D angular progression coordinate functions as a scene-aware compass on the latent. It advances with task progress, regresses when the agent backtracks, and under controlled perturbations both spikes and relocalises to a semantically appropriate new task-phase sector, separating the moment of surprise from its meaning in a way that prediction-error scalars cannot. Three quantitative tests back this up: $|Δθ_t|$ outperforms the standard latent-prediction-error surprise at localising semantic events on 40 held-out cube episodes by up to +0.18 pooled AUROC (97.5% per-episode win rate at $\pm 1$-step tolerance); a within-episode linear probe across all four environments (40 episodes per env) shows the 8-dimensional progression subspace (4.2% of the latent) explains 72-95% of task-progress variance..

Method: 作者首先统一了现有的多尺度建模方法，提出了“尺度算子族”的概念。在此基础上，提出了 SiGMA (Single Generalized Multi-scale Architecture)，该模型通过基于尺度空间理论的可学习离散高斯 (LDG) 核，实现了距离感知的连续尺度缩放，从而克服了传统固定离散尺度带来的限制。

Conclusion: SiGMA 提出的基于可学习离散高斯核的距离感知尺度缩放机制，为时间序列预测中的多尺度建模提供了一个通用且高效的理论框架，证明了灵活性与可学习的尺度变换优于传统的固定离散尺度方法。

Abstract: Multi-scale modeling has emerged as an effective design principle for time-series forecasting by capturing temporal dynamics at multiple resolutions. As no principled foundation has been established in the literature, we unify existing scaling methods into a scaling operator family, revealing a fundamental limitation of existing approaches: reliance on fixed and discrete scaling. To address this limitation, we propose SiGMA (Single Generalized Multi-scale Architecture), which enables distance-aware scaling via the learnable discrete Gaussian (LDG) kernel grounded in scale-space theory. We evaluate SiGMA comprehensively on long- and short-term forecasting benchmarks against state-of-the-art multi-scale baselines. SiGMA outperforms all competitors on both tasks, especially achieving the best performance in 13 out of 16 long-term evaluation settings. Beyond accuracy, SiGMA significantly improves training speed by up to 5.3 times and reduces memory consumption by up to 3.8 times over the strongest competitors. Code is available at https://github.com/cheonwoolee/SiGMA.

### [206] [Learning Hyperspherical Time-Frequency Representations for Time-Series Out-of-Distribution Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31155)
*Willian T. Lunardi,Samridha Shrestha,Martin Andreoni*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种利用von Mises-Fisher分布在超球面上学习时间序列表征的新方法，通过整合时频特征并优化类条件结构，显著提升了时间序列分布外（OOD）数据的检测精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前时间序列的分布外（OOD）检测研究相对滞后，缺乏针对监督时间序列表征如何有效应对分布偏移的系统理解，因此需要一种能诱导类条件结构以实现可靠检测的新方法。

Method: 作者提出了一种基于von Mises-Fisher (vMF) 似然目标函数的表征学习方法，将时间序列数据映射到单位超球空间上；同时结合了时间域和频率域的双流编码器提取特征，并利用k-近邻（k-NN）和马氏距离作为检测得分指标。

Result: 在UCR和UEA大规模时间序列数据集的跨数据集评估中，该方法在k-NN和马氏距离得分下，均表现出优于现有的对比学习和后验（post-hoc）基线模型的检测性能。

Conclusion: 本文提出的基于vMF分布的超球空间表征学习方法，为时间序列OOD检测提供了一种更加结构化和鲁棒的框架，证明了利用类别条件结构优化嵌入空间对于提升检测性能具有显著作用。

Abstract: Out-of-distribution (OOD) detection for time-series data remains comparatively underexplored compared to vision and language, with a limited principled understanding of how supervised time-series representations can be leveraged for reliable detection under distributional shifts. This work formulates time-series OOD detection as representation learning with hyperspherical embeddings, where class-conditional structure is induced by a von Mises-Fisher (vMF) likelihood-based objective on the unit sphere. The learned representation combines time- and frequency-domain views of the input signal via domain-specific encoders, integrating them into a joint embedding space for OOD detection. Detection uses distance-based scores over the learned embeddings, including k-nearest neighbors (k-NN) and Mahalanobis scores. We evaluate the approach at scale on the complete UCR and UEA time-series archives under a cross-dataset protocol. Empirical results show consistent improvements under both k-NN and Mahalanobis scoring over strong contrastive learning and post-hoc baselines in the same setting. Code is available at https://github.com/tiiuae/hypertf-time-series-ood.

</details>


### [207] [TabCausal: Pretraining Across Causal Environments for Tabular Causal Discovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31156)
*Zi-Rong Li,Si-Yang Liu,Tian-Zuo Wang,Han-Jia Ye*

Main category: cs.LG

Across both synthetic and semantic environments, TabCausal demonstrates robust structure recovery, especially under interventional evidence, highlighting broad causal pretraining as a key ingredient for transferable amortized causal discovery.

### [208] [Convergence of Two-Timescale Markovian Stochastic Approximations with Applications in Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31172)
*Vagul Mahadevan,Claire Chen,Shuze Daniel Liu,Shangtong Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对强化学习中常见的两时间尺度随机逼近算法，在更符合现实的马尔可夫噪声条件下，证明了其稳定性和收敛性，并首次证明了带有资格迹的离线TDC算法的收敛性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的两时间尺度随机逼近（SA）理论主要局限于独立同分布（i.i.d.）噪声假设。然而，在强化学习（如TDC和Actor-Critic）的实际应用中，数据通常是马尔可夫序列。因此，有必要在更符合实际的马尔可夫噪声设定下，建立两时间尺度SA的稳定性和收敛性理论。

Method: 该研究的核心技术创新在于：在分析过程中，不再直接使用当前的慢时间尺度参数来控制快时间尺度参数，而是利用慢时间尺度参数的运行最大值（running max）进行控制。这种方法有效地处理了马尔可夫噪声带来的复杂性，无需引入投影算子或假设噪声在紧空间内。

Result: 成功建立了马尔可夫噪声环境下两时间尺度随机逼近算法的稳定性和收敛性证明。作为关键应用，证明了离线学习（off-policy）设定下，采用线性函数逼近和资格迹的TDC算法具有几乎确定的（almost sure）收敛性。

Conclusion: 本文通过引入新的分析技术，成功在马尔可夫噪声环境下证明了两时间尺度随机逼近算法的稳定性和收敛性，摆脱了对投影算子和紧空间假设的依赖，为强化学习算法的理论分析提供了重要支撑。

Abstract: This work studies the convergence of two-timescale stochastic approximations (SA), a class of iterative algorithms that update two sets of parameters in fast and slow timescales respectively. Notable examples of two-timescale SA in reinforcement learning (RL) include temporal difference learning with gradient correction (TDC) and actor-critic methods. Previously, the stability (i.e., boundedness) and convergence of two-timescale SA were only established under i.i.d. noise. This work instead establishes the stability and convergence of two-timescale SA under Markovian noise, a setup that is more realistic in RL. Notably, we do not need to use any projection operator and the noise does not need to live in a compact space. Our key technical novelty is to control the fast timescale parameter with the running max of the slow timescale parameter, instead of with the current slow timescale parameter, as most prior works do. As a key application, we establish the first almost sure convergence of TDC with eligibility traces under off-policy learning with linear function approximation.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种自动化的组合选择方法，从候选池中选择一小部分具有多样性的检索器集合。该方法将问题形式化为查询分布上的“预期最佳-k（expected best-of-k）”目标，并设计了一种具有近乎最优保证的高效构建算法，配合路由器机制实现对查询的动态分配。

Result: 在多个问答基准测试中，所提出的检索器组合与路由器流水线在检索指标和回答质量上均优于单一检索器及传统的简单多检索器基线；同时，由于支持并行检索，该方法在保持高准确率的前提下，显著降低了推理延迟与Token消耗。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了利用“检索器组合（Portfolio）”方法，在处理多样化查询时，能够有效兼顾检索性能与计算效率，为构建高效、可扩展的RAG系统提供了一种优于单检索器和实时参数调优的解决方案。

Abstract: Retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) systems typically rely on a single retriever and a single set of hyperparameters, despite facing highly heterogeneous queries that range from simple factoid questions to complex multi-hop reasoning. We propose a method that automatically selects a small, diverse subset of retrievers (a portfolio) from a large pool of candidates, to cover different regions of the target query distribution. We formalize this setting via an expected best-of-$k$ objective over the query distribution and show that it admits an efficient portfolio construction algorithm with near-optimal guarantees. Across multiple QA benchmarks, our learned portfolios and router pipeline consistently outperform single-retriever and naive multi-retriever baselines on both retrieval metrics and answer quality. In addition, compared to inference-time hyperparameter tuning approaches, fixed portfolios enable parallel retrieval and LLM calls, achieving comparable (and sometimes better) accuracy with substantially lower latency and token cost.

The proposed research studies eight drift detection quality metrics in relation to the classifier's performance across seven synthetic data stream generation tools, additionally considering drift dynamics as a factor. The studies aim to identify the most informative set of drift detection quality metrics and provide a deep understanding of the method's evaluation.

### [211] [Skill Reuse as Compression in Agentic RL](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31509)
*Zhikun Xu,Yu Feng,Jacob Dineen,Taiwei Shi,Jieyu Zhao,Ben Zhou*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 为解决大模型强化学习智能体泛化能力弱的问题，本文提出了ReuseRL框架。通过基于MDL原则的轨迹压缩和技能重用机制，强制模型学习抽象且可复用的行为模式，显著提升了智能体在复杂环境中的泛化性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前利用强化学习训练的大语言模型智能体往往会学习到脆弱的、针对特定任务的“捷径”（Shortcuts）。研究者假设，如果智能体的成功轨迹在结构上是可压缩的——即可以分解为一组可重用的抽象模式——那么智能体将具备更好的泛化能力。

Method: 该研究提出了ReuseRL方法，其核心是将最小描述长度（MDL）原则引入智能体强化学习中。该方法从成功的轨迹中提取一个共享的“技能字典”，并通过在强化学习目标函数中增加一个分割代价项（Segmentation Cost），显式惩罚那些难以压缩的特异性行为。此外，作者还为该压缩惩罚项推导了PAC-Bayes泛化界。

Result: 在ALFWorld、TextWorld-Cooking和Countdown-Stepwise等多个任务基准测试中，ReuseRL在分布内（In-distribution）和分布外（Out-of-distribution）场景下的成功率均优于基准方法（如Vanilla GRPO以及强轮次长度基线）。

Conclusion: 通过引入基于最小描述长度（MDL）原则的ReuseRL框架，研究表明，强制智能体学习具有高度结构压缩性的技能模式，能够有效克服强化学习中对特定任务捷径的过度拟合，从而显著增强智能体的通用性。

Abstract: Large language model agents trained with reinforcement learning (RL) often learn brittle, task-specific shortcuts. We hypothesize that agents generalize better when their successful trajectories are structurally compressible, decomposed into a small set of reusable abstract patterns. To formalize this, we introduce ReuseRL, which grounds agentic RL in the Minimum Description Length (MDL) principle. ReuseRL extracts a shared skill dictionary from successful trajectories and augments the RL objective with a segmentation cost, explicitly penalizing idiosyncratic behaviors that encode poorly. We prove a PAC-Bayes generalization bound for this compression penalty. Across ALFWorld, TextWorld-Cooking, and Countdown-Stepwise, ReuseRL improves in- and out-of-distribution success over vanilla GRPO and strong round-length baselines.

</details>


### [212] [FlagGAM: Rule-Based Generalized Additive Modeling for Explainable Tabular Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31189)
*Zijie Zhao,Roy E. Welsch*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: FlagGAM 是一种新型表格预测框架，通过将特征处理为可解释的规则基，结合加性或灵活的预测模型，在确保模型透明度和鲁棒性的前提下，实现了与主流模型相媲美的预测性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在高风险领域（如医疗、金融等），表格预测模型不仅需要高准确性，还必须具备透明度（可解释性）以及对缺失值或噪声等不完美输入数据的鲁棒性。现有模型往往在解释性与准确性之间难以取得平衡，因此需要一种新的框架来实现这两者的兼顾。

Method: 提出了一种名为 FlagGAM 的规则定义基框架，主要分为两个部分：1. Flag核心模块：通过阈值、类别级别、尾部偏差等规则将原始数据转换为稀疏、人类可读的单变量基；2. 预测头：利用加性模型（GAM）或更灵活的非线性模型对这些基进行组合预测。该方法保留了稀疏规则矩阵，支持混合类型数据的分类与回归。

Result: 在多个基准测试中，FlagGAM 在透明加性模式下表现接近 EBM（可解释增强机），在混合类型回归任务中表现优于岭回归，且在面对缺失和噪声扰动时，其 AUROC 的衰减显著小于常见的对比模型。通过使用灵活的预测头，其精度可进一步提升并逼近树模型。

Conclusion: FlagGAM 为高风险领域的表格预测任务提供了一种实用的平衡方案，在保持高准确性的同时，实现了模型的可解释性与对不完美输入数据的鲁棒性。它作为一种透明度与高性能之间的中间地带，特别适用于需要规则审计和决策支持的应用场景。

Abstract: Tabular prediction in high-stakes domains requires models that are accurate, transparent, and robust to imperfect inputs. We propose FlagGAM, a rule-defined basis framework that separates feature-level rule construction from prediction. A Flag Core Module converts numerical and categorical variables into sparse, human-readable univariate bases, including threshold flags, category-level flags, tail-deviation bases, and categorical step functions; a default additive head then combines these bases as a restricted GAM-style predictor. Rather than reducing triggered rules to compact count summaries, FlagGAM retains a sparse rule-basis matrix that supports mixed-type classification and regression, feature-specific weighting, and optional flexible prediction heads. Across tabular benchmarks, default FlagGAM remains close to EBM in transparent additive mode, improves substantially over ridge regression on mixed-type regression, and shows smaller AUROC degradation than common baselines under missing and noisy perturbations. Flexible heads further improve accuracy and approach strong tree-based baselines, with the caveat that the resulting model should be interpreted as a rule-basis representation followed by a nonlinear predictor rather than as a fully additive GAM. Overall, FlagGAM provides a practical middle ground for tabular settings that require competitive accuracy, communicable rules, and robustness to imperfect inputs.

### [213] [Student Capacity Moderates Knowledge Distillation Effectiveness: A Systematic Study Across ResNet Teacher-Student Pairs on CIFAR-10](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31191)
*Umut Onur Yasar*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过对ResNet模型在CIFAR-10上的对比研究，指出学生模型容量是蒸馏效果的关键限制，强调了正确的蒸馏算法实现（特别是特征层映射）以及对输入分辨率的架构适配是获得最优表现的前提。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在探索教师模型与学生模型之间的容量差异（Capacity Gap）如何影响知识蒸馏的有效性，并澄清在蒸馏实现过程中常见的技术误区（如实现细节对性能的影响），从而为知识蒸馏的有效应用提供可复现的基准。

Method: 在CIFAR-10数据集上，对ResNet系列模型（R50, R34, R18）进行交叉配对，系统性对比Logit-KD与Feature-KD。研究通过控制变量、多次随机种子重复实验，并修复了特征蒸馏中的梯度裁剪实现缺陷（projection layers问题）以及ResNet对32x32图像输入适配的架构缺陷（ResNet stem修改），确保实验结果的准确性。

Result: 1. 学生模型容量越大，蒸馏增益越明显；2. 修复特征蒸馏中的技术实现缺陷后，Feature-KD的表现优于或等同于Logit-KD；3. 针对输入分辨率调整ResNet的初始层（Stem）所带来的性能提升，远超任何蒸馏方法所带来的增益。

Conclusion: 研究强调了模型容量、正确的方法实现（如特征映射层的处理）以及架构对输入分辨率的适配是决定知识蒸馏（KD）成败的关键因素。尤其在处理小分辨率图像（如CIFAR-10）时，基础架构的校准（如修改ResNet stem）比蒸馏算法本身更能带来显著的性能提升。

Abstract: We investigate how teacher-student capacity relationships modulate knowledge distillation (KD) effectiveness in ResNet-based image classification on CIFAR-10. Across three teacher-student pairs -- R50->R18, R34->R18, and R50->R34 -- we compare Logit-KD and Feature-KD under controlled, reproducible conditions (3 seeds, mean+/-std reported throughout). We report three main findings. First, student capacity is a key moderating factor in distillation gain: R34 students benefit substantially more from KD than R18 students even when teacher-student accuracy gaps are comparable, with the strongest gain of +0.30pp observed for R50->R34 Feature-KD versus +0.18pp for R34->R18 Feature-KD and +0.00pp for R34->R18 Logit-KD. Second, implementation correctness critically affects Feature-KD: a gradient clipping bug that excluded projection layers suppressed Feature-KD performance and produced misleading comparisons with Logit-KD. After correction, Feature-KD matches or outperforms Logit-KD in two of three pairs, reaching 95.55% on R50->R34 against a baseline of 95.25%. Third, input-resolution-aware architecture is a prerequisite for effective distillation: correcting the ResNet stem for 32x32 inputs raises teacher accuracy by over 5pp -- an order of magnitude larger than any KD gain. All code and results are available at github.com/umutonuryasar/kd-capacity-gap.

### [214] [Positional versus Symbolic Attention Heads: Learning Dynamics, RoPE Geometry, and Length Generalization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31558)
*Felipe Urrutia,Juan José Alegría,Cinthia Sanchez Macias,Jorge Salas,Cristian B. Calderon,Cristobal Rojas*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文揭示了Transformer注意力头在多跳推理任务中的功能分化，证明了符号性机制在长序列扩展性上优于位置性机制，并为理解Transformer的注意力运作模式提供了几何解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管Transformer在各类任务中表现优异，但其解决结构化任务的底层工作机制尚不明确。为了实现安全部署和行为预测，亟需深入研究注意力头在不同推理任务（位置推理与符号推理）中的学习动态及其计算角色。

Method: 该研究在受控环境下训练GPT-J模型，通过“数字任务”（涉及位置推理）和“字母任务”（涉及符号推理）进行对比分析。利用注意力头分类指标识别其功能类型，并结合RoPE（旋转位置编码）的几何特性，通过理论构造和实证验证，量化分析了注意力头在不同任务需求下的计算角色及对序列长度的鲁棒性差异。

Result: 实验发现，模型在成功训练后形成了分工明确的“纯头”（即单一的位置性或符号性头）；位置性机制在处理长序列时表现出明显的局限性，而符号性机制表现出更强的外推鲁棒性；研究通过“差异度”（discrepancy）这一新概念定量验证了上述结论。

Conclusion: 研究表明，Transformer中的注意力头在执行结构化任务时会展现出明确的功能分化（位置性或符号性）。符号性机制在长序列外推方面具有更高的鲁棒性，而位置性机制则受到更严格的约束。这一发现为理解大模型的机制可解释性提供了理论基础和量化指标。

Abstract: Transformer-based language models are widespread in today's society. As such, understanding the mechanisms by which they solve structured tasks and predicting how they may behave in novel scenarios is of great importance for safe deployment. We study the learning dynamics of attention heads in a controlled setting by training a decoder-only Transformer (GPT-J) on two structurally equivalent multi-hop reasoning tasks: a number task requiring positional reasoning and a letter task requiring symbolic reasoning. Using a recently introduced metric that classifies attention-head behavior as positional or symbolic for a given prompt, we show that successful learning is associated with the emergence of pure heads, i.e., heads that express themselves as either positional or symbolic. Despite the tasks' structural equivalence, they impose different mechanistic demands: the number task requires both positional and symbolic heads, whereas the letter task requires only symbolic heads. We then identify the computational roles of these heads, characterize the basic functions they implement, and give theoretical constructions showing how single-layer RoPE-based attention can realize these functions through geometrically interpretable query, key, and value operations. This analysis yields a quantitative separation between positional and symbolic mechanisms in their robustness to longer sequences, formalized through a novel notion of discrepancy. We empirically validate the resulting predictions in both controlled and real-world models, showing that symbolic mechanisms extrapolate more reliably to longer sequences while positional mechanisms face sharper limitations.

</details>


### [215] [Geometry-based Schrödinger Bridges for Trustworthy Multimodal Fusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31193)
*Jiayu Xiong,Jing Wang,Qi Zhang,Wanlong Wang,Jun Xue*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 为了解决现有模型依赖自身预测置信度评估数据质量导致的盲点，本研究提出一种基于几何传输代价的GMF框架，通过计算数据在潜在空间中的校正量来独立衡量可靠性，显著提升了多模态系统在面对低质量数据时的鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的多模态信任融合方法高度依赖模型自身的预测置信度来判断数据质量，这导致了“循环依赖”问题：即当模型在错误预测时依然保持高置信度，现有方法将无法识别并处理低质量或冲突数据。

Method: 提出几何多模态融合（GMF）框架，利用扩散薛定谔桥（Diffusion Schrödinger Bridge）结合修正流（Rectified Flow）技术。该方法通过计算输入数据在潜在空间中所需的传输校正量（以初始速度平方作为衡量指标）来评估数据可靠性，而非依赖模型预测的置信度。

Result: 实验表明，GMF在面对严重的传感器噪声和语义冲突时，其鲁棒性显著优于现有的基于置信度的基准方法。该几何信号能够作为独立的“裁判”，有效识别并减轻不确定性输入的影响。

Conclusion: 该研究通过引入几何视角的可靠性评估机制（GMF），有效解决了现有基于模型预测置信度进行多模态融合的局限性，证明了利用潜在空间传输代价作为独立判定指标在处理噪声和冲突数据时的优越性。

Abstract: Real-world multimodal systems must be robust against low-quality data, such as sensor noise, incomplete multimodal data and conflicting inputs. However, existing trustworthy fusion methods rely on the model's own prediction confidence to judge data quality. This creates a circular dependency: when a model is confident but wrong, these methods fail to detect the error. To break this loop, we propose Geometry-based Multimodal Fusion (GMF). Instead of relying on predictions, we evaluate reliability by measuring how much transport correction the input needs in latent space. We implement Diffusion Schrödinger Bridge transport with Rectified Flow, where the squared initial velocity gives an efficient learned correction score. Valid data has low squared velocity magnitude, while noisy, incomplete data or conflicting data requires stronger transport correction. This geometry-based reliability signal acts as an independent judge, effectively flagging unreliable inputs even when the classifier is fooled. Extensive experiments demonstrate that GMF significantly improves robustness against severe sensor noise and semantic conflicts compared to confidence-based baselines.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的可解释机器学习方法（如GAM、SHAP等）大多基于加性模型，在处理强特征交互时会产生信号抵消和外推错误，从而导致信息丢失和解释性降低。研究者希望开发一种既能保持结构可解释性，又能有效捕捉复杂特征交互的新型模型。

Method: 提出了一种名为张量分离学习（TSL）的回归模型。该方法通过阶段性贪婪过程（stagewise greedy procedure）配合正交重拟合（orthogonal refitting），学习一系列一元特征函数的秩-1乘积之和。该模型能够显式地建模高阶特征交互，并确保模型可以通过一阶偏相关函数完整重构。

Result: 理论上，作者推导了针对具有有界混合偏导数函数的逼近率保证。实验表明，TSL在回归任务中表现出色，其预测性能可与先进的黑盒模型相媲美，同时提供了更忠实于原始数据的解释能力。

Conclusion: 张量分离学习（TSL）为高维复杂数据的可解释性建模提供了一种新的途径，证明了在保留模型可解释性的同时，通过捕捉特征交互作用能够达到与黑盒模型相当的预测性能。

Abstract: Interpretable machine learning requires models that are accurate and structurally faithful to the data.Existing explainability methods rely heavily on additive representations (e.g., Generalized Additive Models (GAMs), SHapley Additive exPlanations (SHAP), functional ANOVA), which can suffer from signal cancellation and off-support extrapolation in the presence of strong interactions. We propose Tensor Separation Learning (TSL), a regression model that learns a sum of rank-1 products of univariate per-feature functions via a stagewise greedy procedure with orthogonal refitting. By enforcing separability, TSL avoids the information loss inherent in additive projections caused by marginalizing higher-order interactions. The learned TSL model can be fully reconstructed from first-order partial dependence functions, up to constant factors. This stage-wise correspondence ensures that the resulting visualizations are faithful to the fitted components. We establish approximation-rate guarantees for functions with bounded mixed $p$-th order partial derivatives and demonstrate that TSL competes with black-box models on regression benchmarks.

### [217] [Fixed-Point Masked Generative Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31215)
*Andrea Miele,Yiming Qin,Alba Carballo-Castro,Justin Deschenaux,Pascal Frossard*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对掩码生成模型（MGM）训练成本高及低采样预算下表现不佳的问题，本文提出了CoFRe框架。该框架通过固定点求解器替代固定深度去噪器，并引入跨步一致性损失与三态重用机制，在显著降低模型参数量、训练时间和显存开销的同时，提升了多模态生成的质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 掩码生成模型（MGM）虽然具备并行解码能力，但其在训练过程中计算开销大，且在低采样预算下推理质量会严重下降。现有的改进方法通常为每个去噪步骤分配固定的计算量，缺乏灵活性，因此需要一种更高效、更具成本效益的生成框架。

Method: 1. 提出固定点掩码生成模型（FP-MGMs），将部分去噪器替换为跨共享注意力层的固定点求解器，实现自适应深度。2. 引入跨步一致性损失（Cross-step consistency loss），对齐相邻去噪步骤的隐藏表示。3. 设计三态重用（3SR）机制，利用上一步的解对求解器进行热启动（Warm-start）。4. 开发了将预训练MGM转换为FP-MGMs的微调策略，无需完整重训。

Result: 在文本生成（OpenWebText）任务中，相比MDLM，CoFRe减少了38.8%的参数量、11.5%的训练时间和16.9%的显存占用，且在96次Transformer块前向传播预算下，困惑度从830.8大幅提升至101.8。在图像生成（ImageNette）任务中，训练时间减少了48.6%，显存减少了50.7%，并在所有采样预算下均提升了FID指标。

Conclusion: 本文提出的CoFRe框架通过固定点求解器和参数共享，成功解决了掩码生成模型（MGM）在训练成本和低采样预算下生成质量低下的问题，为高效掩码生成提供了一种实用的新范式。

Abstract: Masked Generative Models (MGMs) enable parallel decoding and achieve strong performance across modalities, but require full-sequence bidirectional transformers at every step, making training costly and degrading quality under low sampling budgets. Existing work improves efficiency via better samplers or cheaper fixed-depth denoisers, but they still allocate a fixed amount of denoiser computation to each refinement step. We introduce Fixed-Point Masked Generative Models (FP-MGMs), which replace part of the denoiser with a fixed-point solver over shared attention layers to enable adaptive depth with fewer parameters. To make it more effective for masked generation, we first introduce a cross-step consistency loss, which aligns hidden representations at neighboring denoising steps and, second, three-state reuse (3SR) which warm-starts the solver using the previous solution by treating differently unchanged, still-masked, and newly revealed tokens respectively. Together, these components define our complete training-to-inference framework for fixed-point masked generation, \emph{CoFRe}. We also show that pre-trained MGMs can be converted into FP-MGMs with short fine-tuning, avoiding full retraining. Across modalities, CoFRe improves the quality and cost trade-off. On OpenWebText, CoFRe reduces parameters by 38.8\%, training time by 11.5\%, and VRAM by 16.9\%, while improving generative perplexity from 830.8 to 101.8 at a budget of $96$ transformer-block forward passes, compared to MDLM. In ImageNette, CoFRe reduces training time by 48.6\% and VRAM by 50.7\%, while improving FID in all sample budgets tested. Overall, CoFRe offers a practical framework for cheaper training and stronger low-budget masked generation.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本文采用了“切片（Slicing）”方法，将高维回报分布投影到一维空间，从而利用一维分布强化学习中成熟的散度度量（如Wasserstein、Cramér和MMD）。此外，文中还引入了“最大切片（Maximum-slicing）”变体，并证明了其在一般稠密折扣矩阵下的贝尔曼收缩性。

Conclusion: 本文提出了切片分布强化学习（SDRL），成功将一维分布强化学习的方法扩展至多维场景。通过投影技术，SDRL不仅解决了多维分布在计算上的复杂性问题，还在理论上证明了在特定条件下的贝尔曼收缩性，为处理复杂的多维回报分布提供了有效且可扩展的解决方案。

Abstract: Distributional reinforcement learning (DRL) models the full return distribution rather than expectations, but extending it to multivariate settings remains challenging. Many common metrics do not naturally generalize beyond one dimension or lose computational tractability, and the multivariate case introduces additional difficulties such as general matrix discounting, for which no contraction results are available. We introduce Sliced Distributional Reinforcement Learning (SDRL), which lifts tractable one-dimensional divergences to multivariate return distributions via projections. We prove Bellman contraction for uniform slicing under shared scalar discounting, and introduce a maximum-slicing variant with contraction under general dense discount matrices. SDRL supports a broad class of base divergences; we analyze Wasserstein, Cramér, and Maximum Mean Discrepancy (MMD), and characterize which SDRL variants suit the standard single-sample Bellman update used in distributional RL. Abstract: Token mixing layers play a key role in how language models can learn and generate long-range dependencies. Their efficiency relies on the necessary trade-off between decoding speed and the memory requirements, along with the cache size. Considering causal generation, this paper explores new trade-offs thanks to a unified framework which separates two crucial features: (i) the direct influence of inputs on outputs in one generation step; (ii) the recurrent propagation of information through past outputs. This framework encompasses major architectures such as attention and state-space models, but also generalizes the recurrence equations by allowing each state to depend on multiple past states rather than only the immediate predecessor. By introducing structure, we design new recurrence patterns that provably achieve the desired complexity, while providing theoretical insights on their expressivity -- trading runtime for expressivity in a principled way. Empirical validation is performed on synthetic tasks, along with language modeling. Together, these results provide a unified toolkit for the understanding and design of efficient and expressive token mixers across model families.

### [220] [DRIFT: Decoupled Rollouts and Importance-Weighted Fine-Tuning for Efficient Multi-Turn Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31455)
*Jian Mu,Tianyi Lin,Chengwei Qin,Zhongxiang Dai,Yao Shu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: DRIFT 是一种新型训练框架，它通过将强化学习目标转化为重要性加权的监督学习，解决了多轮交互任务中强化学习成本高与监督微调性能不佳的矛盾，实现了高效且高性能的模型微调。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的多轮交互场景大模型训练存在困境：在线强化学习虽然能处理多轮动态，但全轨迹生成的更新成本极高；而离线监督微调虽高效，却易受分布偏移和行为崩溃影响。研究旨在寻找一种既能处理多轮动态又能保持高效训练的优化方法。

Method: 提出 DRIFT（解耦执行与重要性加权微调）框架。该方法利用 KL 正则化强化学习目标等价于重要性加权监督学习的理论基础，通过从固定参考策略中采样离线交互轨迹，计算基于回报的重要性权重，随后在这些轨迹上执行加权监督微调，从而实现了轨迹采集与策略优化的解耦。

Result: 实验结果表明，DRIFT 在性能上可以媲美甚至超越现有的多轮强化学习基线模型，同时保持了与标准监督微调相当的训练效率和简洁性。

Conclusion: DRIFT 通过将强化学习目标转化为加权监督学习，成功在保持高效训练的同时，解决了多轮交互场景下在线强化学习成本高昂以及离线监督微调（SFT）存在的分布偏移和行为崩溃问题。该框架为大模型在复杂交互环境下的训练提供了一种高效且高性能的替代方案。

Abstract: Large language models are increasingly deployed in multi-turn interactive settings where users or environments can iteratively provide lightweight feedback. Unfortunately, optimizing such behavior presents a sharp dilemma in practice: online reinforcement learning is able to effectively address multi-turn dynamics but is prohibitively expensive due to the cost of generating full correction trajectories at every update, whereas offline supervised fine-tuning (SFT) is efficient but suffers from distribution shift and behavioral collapse. To this end, we novelly propose DRIFT (Decoupled Rollouts and Importance-Weighted Fine-Tuning), a framework that operationalizes the theoretical insight that the KL-regularized RL objective is equivalent to importance-weighted supervised learning. DRIFT decouples rollout from optimization by sampling offline interaction trajectories from a fixed reference policy, deriving return-based importance weights, and optimizing the policy via weighted SFT on the resulting dataset. Empirically, we demonstrate that DRIFT matches or exceeds the performance of multi-turn reinforcement learning baselines while maintaining the training efficiency and simplicity of standard supervised fine-tuning. Code is available at https://github.com/2020-qqtcg/DRIFT.

</details>


### [221] [Spectral Reach: Understanding Neural Scaling as Progress into the Spectral Tail](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31244)
*Konstantin Nikolaou,Jonas Scheunemann,Sven Krippendorf,Samuel Tovey,Christian Holm*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文引入“谱位置”度量工具，揭示了深度学习扩展定律的本质机制：大模型通过特征学习展现出更强的“谱触达”能力，能够捕捉小模型无法学习的弱谱信号，从而实现更低的损失。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管神经缩放定律（neural scaling laws）在基础模型开发中被广泛应用，但其背后的深层机制尚不明确，主要原因在于缺乏可扩展的分析工具来解释模型规模如何影响性能。作者旨在填补这一空白，探究模型性能提升的本质原因。

Method: 提出了一种名为“谱位置（spectral position）”的可扩展度量工具，用于评估经验神经切线核（eNTK）中哪些特征值对损失下降起主导作用。通过分析训练过程中谱位置的演变，并将其应用于不同规模的模型实验，从而揭示模型大小、特征学习与性能损失之间的内在关联。

Result: 实验发现训练过程中谱位置逐渐下降，学习过程从主导特征模式向谱尾部偏移；大模型相比小模型能触及更深的谱尾部（即更强的“谱触达”能力）；特征学习是实现这一能力的关键，它能通过自适应放大梯度来维持学习进程。

Conclusion: 论文提出“谱触达（spectral reach）”是模型性能扩展的核心机制，大模型通过特征学习动态放大梯度，从而能够学习到小模型无法触及的弱谱信号。该研究为通过架构和优化器设计来进一步提升模型性能提供了理论依据和具体干预方向。

Abstract: Neural scaling laws describe predictable power-law relationships between model size, dataset size, compute, and performance. While these laws guide the development of modern foundation models, the mechanisms underpinning them remain poorly understood, in part due to the absence of scalable analysis tools. To close this gap, we introduce "spectral position": a scalable measure of which eigenvalues of the empirical neural tangent kernel (eNTK) currently drive loss reduction. Applying this measure to scaling experiments, we find that spectral position decreases throughout training: learning shifts from dominant eigenmodes into the spectral tail. Larger models reach further into the tail than smaller models, revealing a size-dependent capacity we call "spectral reach". This suggests why larger models achieve lower losses: they sustain learning on weak spectral signals inaccessible to smaller models. We further identify feature learning as a key enabler of spectral reach. It adaptively amplifies gradient magnitudes as learning advances, sustaining progress where frozen representations stall. This points to concrete interventions through architecture and optimizer design.

### [222] [Lightweight CNN-Based Anomaly Detection for High Voltage Converter Modulators in the Spallation Neutron Source](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31259)
*Alberto D. Cencillo,Leonardo Concepción,Julián Luengo,Isaac Triguero*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型加速器设施中的高压转换调制器（HVCM）故障导致大量停机时间。现有深度学习模型在处理多通道传感器数据时，往往过早地混合了时间和通道信息，无法有效捕捉不同故障类型下特有的先兆模式（如时间结构改变或统计依赖性变化）。

Method: 作者提出了一种新的深度学习架构，通过改变时间特征提取与跨通道信息混合的先后顺序，并引入基于脉冲的自适应通道重加权机制，专门处理多通道传感器信号的时间与空间相关性。该方法在散裂中子源（SNS）的HVCM数据集上进行了广泛评估。

Result: 该模型在SNS四个子系统上实现了0.816的AUC-PR和0.934的AUC-ROC，在大多数子系统和六个故障族中的五个方面均优于现有最优方法；同时识别出三个核心输入通道，并揭示了不同故障类型对通道交互依赖的差异。

Conclusion: 研究证实，通过精心设计的架构归纳偏置（特别是调整时间滤波与跨通道交互的顺序），可以显著提升深度学习模型对高功率脉冲转换器故障先兆的检测能力。这一发现为工业设备故障预测提供了更高效的建模范式。

Abstract: Unscheduled trips of high-power pulsed converters are a leading source of downtime at large accelerator facilities. At the Spallation Neutron Source (SNS), the High Voltage Converter Modulators (HVCMs) are consistently the second-largest contributor to lost beam time. Each HVCM pulse is recorded across sensor channels spanning currents, voltages, and magnetic fluxes, whose mutual interactions encode the operating state of the system. Fault precursors do not manifest uniformly across these channels: depending on fault type, they may alter the temporal structure of individual signals, change the statistical dependencies among channels, or both. Existing deep-learning approaches typically process multi-channel signals with standard convolutional pipelines that entangle temporal and cross-channel operations from the first layer, giving the model no explicit mechanism to represent channel independence or structured inter-channel interaction. We hypothesise that architectural inductive bias, specifically the ordering of temporal filtering and cross-channel mixing, plays a central role in detection performance on this class of data. To test this, we vary the order in which these two operations are applied, and examine whether per-pulse adaptive channel reweighting further improves sensitivity. Evaluated on the public HVCM dataset across all four SNS subsystems (RFQ, DTL, CCL, SCL), our best variant achieves a pooled AUC-PR of 0.816 and AUC-ROC of 0.934, outperforming the state of the art on most subsystems and five of the six fault families. Ablations identify three dominant input channels and link per-fault-family performance to whether precursors manifest as amplitude shifts in individual channels or as subtler patterns requiring joint channel representations to surface.

</details>


### [223] [Algorithmic Recourse of In-Context Learning for Tabular Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31272)
*Wenshuo Dong,Jiaming Zhang,Shaopneg Fu,Hongbin Lin,Di Wang,Lijie Hu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文填补了ICL模型在表格数据领域缺乏算法补救的空白，提出了ASR-ICL框架，通过零阶优化有效生成可解释的补救措施，并从理论与实验层面证明了其有效性与收敛性。

Method: 1. 理论层面：分析了ICL设置下算法补救的定义及收敛性质。2. 实践层面：提出了名为“ASR-ICL”（Adaptive Subspace Recourse for In-Context Learning）的零阶优化框架。该框架通过自适应子空间搜索，在不需要模型梯度的情况下，为黑盒ICL模型生成稀疏且可行的修改建议，并支持多分类任务。

Result: 实验在多个真实世界数据集和模型上表明，ASR-ICL能够以更少的查询次数达到与现有主流方法相当的补救质量，同时其实证结果成功验证了理论推导中关于补救行为随上下文规模增大而收敛的结论。

Abstract: As predictive models are increasingly deployed in high-stakes settings such as credit approval, there is a growing need for post-hoc methods that provide recourse to affected individuals. Many such models operate on tabular data, where features correspond to real-world attributes. Recently, in-context learning (ICL) has enabled large language models to perform tabular prediction by conditioning on labeled examples at inference time, without explicit training. However, algorithmic recourse for tabular decision-making under ICL remains largely unexplored. In this work, we present the first study of algorithmic recourse for tabular data under ICL. We carry out a theoretical analysis, showing that recourse remains well-defined and bounded, and we characterize how recourse converges toward classical solutions as the context size increases. In practice, we propose a novel zeroth-order recourse framework, Adaptive Subspace Recourse for In-Context Learning (ASR-ICL), that efficiently generates actionable and sparse recourse for black-box ICL models. The proposed framework naturally extends to multi-class tabular tasks.   <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种名为“生存强化学习（SRL）”的在线分类框架，通过最大化智能体在目标状态的停留时间来学习价值函数，以此替代传统的对比学习方法，并设计了缓解复杂动力系统中“砰砰”（bang-bang）控制行为的机制。

SRL bypasses the structural constraints of CRL and mitigates the "bang-bang" control solutions inherent to survival frameworks, which often induce undesirable behavior in complex dynamical systems. Evaluated across diverse robotic benchmarks, scaled SRL matches state-of-the-art CRL on manipulation tasks and outperforms it by 2x to 8x on stable, long-horizon locomotion tasks. Our results provide strong additional evidence that classification-based methods may serve as a key primitive in the broader effort to scale reinforcement learning.

### [226] [Non-Asymptotic Convergence of Stochastic Iterative Algorithms: A Lyapunov Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31309)
*Zaiwei Chen,Siva Theja Maguluri*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文综述了随机近似（SA）算法的有限时间分析技术，提出利用广义Moreau包络作为通用Lyapunov函数，为强化学习及相关优化算法提供了一套统一的收敛性分析理论框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有随机近似（SA）算法的分析往往针对特定算法，缺乏通用性和统一性。为了解决这一问题，本文旨在构建一个基于Lyapunov技术的统一框架，以便系统地对解决固定点方程的各类随机迭代算法进行有限时间收敛分析，特别是在强化学习领域。

Method: 本文采用基于Lyapunov函数的理论分析方法。核心在于利用广义Moreau包络（Generalized Moreau Envelopes）作为统一的Lyapunov函数，通过分析其在迭代过程中的单调递减性质，推导出均方收敛界。分析覆盖了从独立同分布（i.i.d.）噪声到马尔可夫噪声、从压缩算子到耗散算子等多种复杂场景。

Result: 本文成功构建了一个以广义Moreau包络为核心的统一分析框架，验证了该框架在随机梯度下降、线性SA、Q-learning及TD学习中的有效性。此外，本文还将该分析推广到了马尔可夫噪声、半范数压缩算子及耗散算子场景下，并推导出了相应的均方收敛界和高概率界。

Conclusion: 该综述为随机近似（SA）算法的有限时间分析提供了一个统一的Lyapunov分析框架。研究表明，通过广义Moreau包络作为通用Lyapunov函数，可以系统地推导出各类强化学习和随机优化算法的收敛性保证，为处理更复杂的噪声和算子特性提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We survey Lyapunov-based techniques for the finite-time analysis of stochastic iterative algorithms, also known as stochastic approximation (SA) algorithms, for solving fixed-point equations $\bar{F}(x)=x$, where the operator $\bar{F}(\cdot)$ can only be accessed through a noisy oracle. We first focus on the standard setting in which $\bar{F}(\cdot)$ is contractive with respect to some norm and the noise is i.i.d., and explain how generalized Moreau envelopes serve as universal Lyapunov functions, regardless of the underlying norm. We then show how this framework yields mean-square convergence guarantees and applies to stochastic gradient descent, linear SA, and value-based reinforcement learning algorithms such as Q-learning and temporal-difference learning. Finally, we discuss extensions to Markovian noise, seminorm-contractive operators, dissipative operators, and high-probability bounds, and conclude with open problems. The goal is to present a unified and self-contained roadmap for the finite-time analysis of SA and its applications, especially in reinforcement learning.

### [227] [Forgetting Has Neighbors: Localized Collateral Forgetting in Machine Unlearning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31317)
*Polina Dolgova,Sebastian U. Stich*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 机器遗忘方法往往会产生非均匀的“局部附带遗忘”现象，即遗忘操作会意外损害邻近样本的预测准确性。本文提出了一种“局部教师蒸馏”策略，通过引入局部化的教师模型来指导遗忘过程，有效减少了该副作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的机器遗忘评估多采用聚合指标（如准确率或遗忘得分），容易掩盖局部区域的遗忘失效。研究者旨在深入探讨遗忘过程中存在的非均匀失效模式（即“局部附带遗忘”），并探索其内在机制。

Method: 本文通过对比遗忘模型与重训练模型在样本级别的预测差异，量化了遗忘过程中的“逐点差异”。研究发现这种差异与样本在特征空间中与遗忘集的几何距离密切相关。基于此机制，作者提出了“局部教师蒸馏”（Local Teacher Distillation）策略，利用仅在遗忘集邻近样本上训练的小型教师模型的软标签来替代随机目标，以缓解局部失真。

Result: 研究发现，现有的遗忘方法（如梯度上升、随机标注）会导致遗忘影响不均匀地扩散，尤其是靠近遗忘集的样本受损最严重。通过采用“局部教师蒸馏”，在CIFAR-100部分类别删除任务中，模型在靠近遗忘集区域的预测表现显著向重训练模型靠拢，同时保持了良好的总体遗忘评估指标。

Conclusion: 本文揭示了机器遗忘过程中的“局部附带遗忘”现象，并证明了通过使用基于保留集邻近样本的“局部教师蒸馏”策略，可以有效缩小遗忘模型与完全重训练模型之间的差距，从而提供了一种更具针对性的遗忘方法。

Abstract: Machine unlearning aims to remove the influence of selected training examples without full retraining. Standard evaluations often summarize unlearning quality with aggregate metrics, such as accuracy- and forgetting-based scores, which can hide localized failures. We study this failure mode at the example level by comparing the predictions of an unlearned model to those of the model retrained after deletion. We show that this pointwise discrepancy can be highly non-uniform: for gradient-ascent and random-labeling methods, with and without retain-set fine-tuning, it grows with geometric proximity to the forget set. We call this phenomenon localized collateral forgetting. Our analysis identifies a mechanism behind the effect: surrogate targets used during unlearning can be inconsistent with the local prediction structure induced by retraining, and this inconsistency propagates through shared representations to nearby examples. Motivated by this mechanism, we propose Local Teacher Distillation, a simple mitigation strategy that replaces random targets with soft labels from a small teacher trained only on retained neighbors of the forget set. On CIFAR-100 partial-class deletion, this local teacher brings the unlearned model substantially closer to retraining, especially near the forget set, while maintaining competitive aggregate unlearning metrics.

Existing opponent modeling methods encode intent using an embedding derived from episode information chosen a priori, such as the opponent's next action or a future environment state, and use this to guide the ego-agent's behavior. These approaches assume that the chosen information is universally representative of intent; however, we show empirically that this is not the case as intentions are often task- and environment-dependent. To address this, we introduce a task-adaptive opponent modeling framework that learns a performance-driven mixture of multiple intent representations. We further introduce a new intention representation that maximizes mutual information with the ego-agent's future returns, thereby capturing opponent information that is most directly relevant to performance. Our approach consistently matches or exceeds the performance of state-of-the-art baselines across diverse tasks and yields insights into when and why different opponent modeling strategies succeed.

### [229] [Softsign: Smooth Sign in Your Optimizer For Better Parameter Heterogeneity Handling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31371)
*Dmitrii Feoktistov,Timofey Belinsky,Andrey Veprikov,Amir Zainullin,Aleksandr Beznosikov*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对符号优化器在收敛末期易震荡的问题，该论文提出了 SoftSignum 和 SoftMuon，通过平滑的温度控制策略实现了符号更新与量级敏感更新的自适应平衡，显著提升了深度学习模型的训练效果与稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于符号（Sign-based）和 LMO 的优化器虽然具有内存占用低等优势，但其固定幅度的更新机制在深度学习的收敛末期会造成参数震荡，无法有效处理参数异质性，从而损害最终的收敛效果。

Method: 1. 提出 SoftSignum：将硬符号映射替换为温度可控的软符号变换，实现参数级从符号更新到量级敏感更新的动态转换；2. 引入基于分位数的自适应温度调度策略；3. 将该原理扩展至矩阵值优化器 SoftMuon；4. 建立基于强凸正则化器和 Fenchel 共轭的广义几何松弛理论框架，并证明了其在随机非凸设置下的收敛性。

Result: 实验表明，SoftSignum 和 SoftMuon 在多种深度学习任务（包括大语言模型预训练）中，不仅克服了硬符号更新的缺陷，而且在性能上始终优于传统的硬符号优化器和标准的 AdamW。

Conclusion: SoftSignum 和 SoftMuon 通过引入温度可控的平滑松弛机制，成功克服了传统符号优化器在收敛末期因固定量级更新导致的震荡问题，在保持低内存占用的同时，实现了优于现有硬符号方法和 AdamW 的性能。此外，该论文提出的几何松弛框架为非凸优化提供了坚实的理论支持。

Abstract: Sign-based and LMO-inspired optimizers have recently attracted substantial attention in deep learning due to their strong performance and low memory footprint. However, their fixed-magnitude updates can hurt terminal convergence: they decouple update mechanisms from gradient magnitudes and fail to account for parameter heterogeneity, often leading to oscillation rather than convergence. We propose SoftSignum, a smooth relaxation of sign-based optimization that replaces the hard sign map with a temperature-controlled soft-sign transformation, enabling a parameter-wise transition from sign-like updates to magnitude-sensitive SGD-like steps. We complement it with an adaptive quantile-based temperature schedule and extend the same principle to matrix-valued optimizers, obtaining SoftMuon. We also develop a generalized geometry-relaxation framework based on strongly convex regularizers and Fenchel conjugates, proving convergence in stochastic non-convex setting. Experiments on diverse deep learning tasks, including LLM pretraining, show that SoftSignum and SoftMuon consistently improve over their hard sign-based counterparts and standard AdamW.

*Giseung Park,Hyunyoung Nam,Woohyeon Byeon,Amir Leshem,Youngchul Sung*

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种集成了最大-最小公平准则与约束满足机制的多目标强化学习新框架，通过理论和实证研究证明了其在解决复杂多目标决策问题中的有效性。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的最大-最小MORL方法在处理带有显式约束的多目标优化问题时适用性有限，无法有效同时平衡公平性与约束条件。

Method: 提出了一种创新的多目标强化学习（MORL）框架，将最大-最小（max-min）公平准则与显式约束满足机制相结合，并提供了相应的理论基础、收敛性分析以及在多种复杂环境下的实验验证。

Result: 实验结果表明，该方法在表格环境、模拟建筑热控制、多目标运动控制以及温室气体排放感知交通管理等多种应用场景中，均能有效实现公平性与约束满足的平衡。

Conclusion: 本文提出的结合最大-最小准则与显式约束满足的MORL框架，在理论上是完备的，在实践中能有效平衡多目标决策中的公平性与约束条件，为处理复杂的多目标任务提供了一种稳健的决策范式。

Abstract: Multi-Objective Reinforcement Learning (MORL) extends standard RL by optimizing policies with respect to multiple, often conflicting, objectives. While max-min MORL has emerged as an effective approach for promoting fairness, its applicability remains limited, particularly when constraints must be incorporated. In this paper, we propose a MORL framework that integrates the max-min criterion with explicit constraint satisfaction. We establish a theoretical foundation for the proposed framework and validate the resulting algorithm through convergence analysis and experiments in tabular settings. We further demonstrate the practical relevance of our approach in simulated building thermal control, multi-objective locomotion control, and greenhouse-gas-emission-aware traffic management. Across these domains, our method effectively balances fairness and constraint satisfaction in multi-objective decision-making.

### [231] [Fixed Universal Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31423)
*Jingwen Liu,Alexandr Andoni,Daniel Hsu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了“通用Transformer”的概念，证明了固定的Transformer权重配合特定的输入嵌入，能够模拟任何同类Transformer模型。这一发现表明模型的表达能力很大程度上蕴含于输入表示之中，而非单纯依赖于权重学习。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索Transformer模型的表达能力边界，探讨是否可以不通过更新权重，而是通过改变输入嵌入（input embedding）来改变模型的功能，以类比图灵机的通用性思想，揭示模型内部参数与输入表示在实现复杂任务中的相对作用。

Method: 1. 构建理论框架：引入“通用Transformer”概念，证明通过适当的输入嵌入，固定的Transformer模型可以模拟给定类别内的任何其他Transformer。
2. 稀疏性构造：提供了具体的稀疏性构造方法，在嵌入维度足够大的情况下实现通用性。
3. 通用性证明：利用概率论证明了随机初始化的Transformer几乎必然具有通用性。
4. 实验验证：在括号平衡（parenthesis balancing）和多跳推理（multi-hop reasoning）等算法任务上对理论进行了实证。

Result: 1. 理论上证明了存在固定的Transformer可以通过特定的输入嵌入模拟该类中的任何Transformer。
2. 证明了随机初始化的Transformer在几乎所有情况下都具备这种通用性。
3. 实验结果证实，即使权重保持不变，通过调整输入表示，模型在特定算法任务上依然具备高性能表现。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，Transformer的强大表达能力在很大程度上可能源于输入表示（input representation）而非仅取决于学习得到的权重。这意味着可以通过设计特定的输入嵌入（input embedding）来使固定的Transformer模型模拟其他模型，为理解模型泛化能力和架构通用性提供了新的视角。

Abstract: We introduce \emph{universal transformers}: fixed transformers that can simulate any transformer in a given class via a suitable input embedding. Analogous to a universal Turing machine, the input embedding encodes a description of the target model while all internal parameters remain fixed. We provide explicit sparse constructions achieving universality when the embedding dimension is sufficiently large, and further show that universality is generic: randomly initialized transformers are universal almost surely, which aligns with recent empirical results of Zhong and Andreas (2024). We empirically validate our theory on the algorithmic tasks of parenthesis balancing and multi-hop reasoning. Our results suggest that much of a transformer's expressive power may reside in its input representation rather than its learned weights.

Abstract: Dynamic graph learning (DGL) is essential for modelling evolving graph data, but existing methods suffer from significant computational overhead due to repeated full-snapshot retraining and are not well-suited for collaborative settings with partitioned data. We propose DG-CoLearn, a client-oblivious collaborative dynamic graph learning framework built on incremental graph snapshot processing, which focuses computation on graph regions affected by temporal updates while preserving historical information through temporal modelling. This incremental design is consistently applied across the entire graph processing pipeline, including a server-mediated embedding exchange mechanism to enable accurate multi-hop message passing without exposing raw cross-client structural information. Extensive experiments demonstrate that DG-CoLearn achieves up to 33.8$\times$ speedup in training time and 27.4$\times$ reduction in communication overhead, while consistently improving predictive performance on both node classification (up to 13.36% F1 improvement) and link prediction (up to 8.27% MAP improvement) tasks. ### [233] [Flow map learning in nonlinear vector autoregressive models: influence of the feature-library structure on the training error](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31438)
*Markus Gross*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过理论分析与实验验证，揭示了非线性向量自回归（NVAR/NG-RC）模型在预测动力系统时的训练误差标度律，阐明了特征库构造与预测性能之间的匹配关系，并指出仅靠增加延迟项无法保证长周期预测的准确性，必须确保模型具备足够的非线性表达能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 时间序列预测通常需要学习非线性与时滞依赖，NVAR（下一代储备池计算）是一类重要的预测模型。尽管其实用性较强，但其学习马尔可夫非线性动力系统的可辨识性问题尚不明确，且训练误差与时间分辨率、模型结构间的量化关系缺乏理论支撑。因此，研究旨在揭示这些模型在逼近Koopman算子时的误差缩放规律及其对泛化性能的影响。

Method: 作者通过将NVAR/NG-RC模型视为Koopman算子在显式特征库上的近似，利用数学分析方法推导了训练误差关于时间分辨率、非线性阶数及延迟项数量的标度律。此外，通过在单项式和傅里叶特征库下的多项式向量场系统进行理论推导，并结合多种混沌动力系统的数值实验验证了上述理论预测。

Result: 研究发现训练误差的标度律取决于特征库对流动映射李级数系数的近似能力。数值实验证实，当模型特征库无法充分匹配真实数据生成过程的非线性结构时，即便能够达到极低的训练误差，长期的预测表现（泛化能力）依然较差，揭示了模型配置与系统动力学特征匹配的重要性。

Conclusion: 研究表明，NVAR/NG-RC模型的训练误差遵循特定的（预）渐近标度律。该标度律由特征库是否能精确表示流动映射的李级数系数决定。尽管增加延迟项可以降低单步训练误差，但若模型特征空间与真实动力系统不匹配，会导致“训练误差小但泛化能力差”的现象。因此，为了提高长周期预测性能，模型必须具备足够的非线性表示能力。

Abstract: Time series forecasting often requires learning nonlinear and time-delayed dependencies. A paradigmatic class of forecasting models are nonlinear vector autoregressive processes (NVAR), also known as next-generation reservoir computers (NG-RCs). These models approximate the Koopman operator on the space spanned by their explicit feature library. We consider the identifiability problem for learning Markovian nonlinear dynamical systems and show that the training error as a function of time resolution follows characteristic (pre-)asymptotic scaling laws. These laws depend on whether the feature library can represent the early Lie-series coefficients of the flow map (propagator) exactly or merely approximately. For dynamical systems governed by polynomial vector fields, we demonstrate the mechanism for NVAR/NG-RC models with monomial and Fourier feature libraries. We determine the dependence of the training error on the temporal resolution, the involved nonlinear degree, and the number of delay terms. While delay terms reduce the optimal one-step training error, they improve long-horizon forecasts only when the library provides sufficient nonlinearity. Thus, small training error coexists with weak generalization as the model class is mismatched to the true data-generating process. Numerical experiments on various chaotic dynamical systems confirm the theoretical predictions.

### [234] [Balanced LoRA: Removing Parameter Invariance to Accelerate Convergence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31484)
*Valérie Castin,Kimia Nadjahi,Pierre Ablin,Gabriel Peyré*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对LoRA过度参数化导致的收敛效率问题，本文提出了BaLoRA（平衡低秩适应）。通过将低秩因子投影到平衡流形上，BaLoRA有效改善了损失地形的条件数，从而在不增加计算负担的情况下，显著提升了微调的收敛速度和模型最终性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LoRA本质上是过度参数化的，即多组低秩因子对可以产生相同的适应权重矩阵。研究发现，这些不同的因子对具有显著不同的条件数，导致训练过程中收敛速度差异巨大。因此，作者旨在通过改善这些参数因子的条件数来提升微调的效率与效果。

Method: 提出了一种名为平衡低秩适应（BaLoRA）的新方法。该方法在LoRA微调过程中引入了一个投影步骤，将迭代点限制在“平衡流形”上。这种投影操作在计算上非常轻量，能够在保持适应权重矩阵不变的前提下，显著改善损失函数的条件数，从而优化优化过程。

Result: 实验结果表明，BaLoRA相比标准LoRA表现出更快的收敛速度。在多种大语言模型微调任务中，BaLoRA均取得了更优的性能，证实了该方法在实际应用中的有效性。

Conclusion: BaLoRA通过引入平衡流形（Balanced Manifold），优化了LoRA在训练过程中的损失地形，不仅提高了计算效率，还通过改善条件数加速了收敛过程，证明了在低秩微调中考虑矩阵因子的平衡性对模型性能和训练速度至关重要。

Abstract: Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA) is the most widely adopted method for fine-tuning large language models. Notably, LoRA is inherently overparameterized: multiple pairs of low-rank factors can yield the same adapted weight matrix. We show--both theoretically and empirically--that these pairs exhibit significantly different condition numbers. As a result, converging to different loss minimizers directly impacts the convergence rate of LoRA. Building on this observation, we introduce Balanced Low-Rank Adaptation (BaLoRA), a variant of LoRA that projects iterates onto a balanced manifold. This manifold improves the conditioning of the loss landscape while preserving the adapted matrix. The projection step is computationally lightweight and integrates seamlessly into existing fine-tuning pipelines. Empirically, BaLoRA converges faster than standard LoRA and achieves superior performance across a range of fine-tuning tasks.

*Brady Exoo,Alberto Bietti,John Sous*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本文采用受控实验方法，设计了包含变量赋值和模加运算的简单任务。通过将训练数据划分为不相交的集合，观察模型在未见组合上的泛化表现；同时结合机械可解释性分析（Mechanistic Analysis）和经验性的训练动力学分析，研究模型如何调用内部组件，并建立理论框架解释组合性的涌现。

Conclusion: 大型语言模型的组合泛化能力源于其内部机制的组合性。训练动力学表现出的阶段性学习过程，促使模型能够利用已有的功能模块（如模加运算）来处理未见过的变量组合。

Abstract: Large language models are able to compose skills in order to perform complex tasks, many of which might not have been seen during training. The details of how exactly this composition occurs remain elusive. In this paper, we study a mechanism for compositional generalization in transformers by considering a simple controlled setting involving variable assignment and modular addition. By partitioning our training data into disjoint sets, we observe that small transformers are able to generalize to previously unseen combinations of variables and numbers. Our mechanistic analysis shows that the same ``modular addition'' MLP module is used whether the inputs are given directly or indirectly through a separate variable assignment mechanism. We also analyze the training dynamics from an empirical lens, which reveals three phases of learning: first, modular addition is learned, then the structure required for variable assignment, and finally a refinement phase where the model generalizes to some hard sequences not seen in training. Finally, we provide a theoretical framework to explain how compositionality emerges from training dynamics. These results suggest that compositional generalization can be a natural consequence of the compositionality of internal mechanisms in~transformers.

### [236] [When Are Multimodal Predictions Biologically Supported? A Diagnostic Evaluation Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31504)
*Dylan Steiner,Gustavo Arango-Argoty,Gerald Sun,Etai Jacob*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: DECAT是一种新型模型评估框架，旨在诊断多模态医疗模型中潜在的“虚假相关性”和混杂偏置，揭示模型是基于真正的生物学规律还是统计学捷径进行预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的多模态医疗模型（尤其是肿瘤学模型）虽然在预测任务上表现出色，但缺乏可解释性，无法确定模型决策的依据是源于真正的生物学关联，还是数据中的混杂因素或虚假相关性。因此，需要一种评估工具来审视模型内部表征的可靠性。

Method: 提出了一种模型无关的后验评估框架（DECAT），利用五个基于空值参考（null-referenced）的指标和一套基于规则的决策程序，对多模态表示进行分类。该方法无需预先知道混杂因素的种类，直接在已学习的表示上进行分析，能够有效识别模型是在捕捉共享生物学特征、单一模态特征，还是虚假相关性。

Conclusion: DECAT框架能够有效揭示多模态模型在肿瘤学预测中是基于真正的生物学关联，还是仅仅依赖于虚假相关性或单模态特征。研究表明，即使是性能优异的模型（如CLIP）也可能存在严重的混杂偏差，且这种问题随模型规模和数据量的增加可能变得更加隐蔽，强调了在多模态医疗AI评估中超越单纯性能指标（如AUROC）的必要性。

Abstract: Multimodal models in oncology can produce accurate predictions, but accurate prediction does not reveal whether the model has learned biology that is shared across modalities, biology confined to one modality, or spurious correlations that reflect confounders rather than genuine biology. We introduce DECAT, a model-agnostic post-hoc evaluation framework that classifies multimodal representations into four diagnostic scenarios for a given task and modality, using five null-referenced metrics and a rule-based decision procedure. The framework operates on learned representations, requires no knowledge of which specific confounder is present, and returns indeterminate when the evidence is insufficient. We validate DECAT on synthetic data across four multimodal model classes (over 2,500 trained representations) and on real data from 8,979 TCGA patients, evaluating both multimodal embeddings and five pretrained pathology foundation models. Entangled models (e.g., CLIP) achieve near-perfect shared biology detection but falsely claim shared biology in the majority of cases where it is absent on real foundation model embeddings. This false claim rate increases with confound strength so that larger cohorts and stronger representations produce more confident but still incorrect diagnoses. Applied to both multimodal TCGA embeddings and five pathology foundation models without paired RNA, DECAT detects confounding invisible to AUROC without requiring the confounder labels, as confirmed by post-hoc stratification.

### [237] [On the Relationship Between Activation Outliers and Feature Death in Sparse Autoencoders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31518)
*Elana Simon,Etowah Adams,James Zou*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文揭示了稀疏自编码器（SAE）中特征死亡现象的根本原因是激活值的均值离群值，并提出通过均值归一化预处理即可有效消除该问题，显著提高特征利用效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 稀疏自编码器（SAE）中广泛存在的“特征死亡”现象（即大量特征从未激活）浪费了模型容量并可能导致叠合（superposition）问题。不同模型间的死亡率差异巨大，研究旨在探究导致这一问题的根源并寻找解决方案。

Method: 研究团队通过对454个不同架构的模型层组合进行大规模分析，将离群值严重程度形式化为γ = ||μ|| / ||σ||，并验证了该指标对特征死亡率的预测能力。同时，通过对比实验证明了减去激活均值的“均值归一化”处理可以消除离群值引起的特征死亡。

Result: 研究发现，维度级的激活离群值会导致初始化时的预激活值偏移，使不匹配的特征永远无法激活。定义的γ值与初始死亡率具有极高的相关性（Spearman ρ高达0.89）。实验证明，均值归一化能够完全消除由离群值导致的特征死亡，是解决该问题的核心手段。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了稀疏自编码器（SAE）中“特征死亡”现象的核心机制是由激活值的均值离群值（outliers）引起的。通过引入均值归一化（mean-centering）预处理步骤，可以有效解决这一问题，从而显著提升特征利用率，为SAE的训练提供了理论基础和实践指导。

Abstract: Sparse autoencoders (SAEs) decompose neural network activations into interpretable features, but many learned features never activate, a problem called feature death that wastes dictionary capacity and can reintroduce superposition. Death rates vary dramatically between models: near-zero on GPT-2, over 70% on AlphaFold3 with identical configurations. We find that dimension-level activation outliers (dimensions whose mean magnitude is large relative to per-token variation) cause this by shifting pre-activations at initialization based on each feature's alignment with the activation mean. Features anti-aligned with the mean receive permanently negative pre-activations and never fire. We formalize outlier severity as $γ= \|μ\|/\|σ\|$; it predicts initial death rates (Spearman $ρ= 0.89$ for dead-by-TopK, $0.82$ for dead-by-ReLU) across 454 model-layer combinations spanning language, vision, protein, and genomic models. Dead features can revive during training, but recovery requires the SAE bias to learn the activation mean, a process that is prohibitively slow at high $γ$. Mean-centering (subtracting the activation mean) sidesteps this and eliminates outlier-induced death across all tested models, confirming the mechanism and providing a principled basis for when and why this preprocessing step is necessary.

</details>


### [238] [Chem-PerturBridge: a harmonized compendium of small molecule perturbation transcriptomic effects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31522)
*Artur Szałata,Olga Novitskaia,Maiia Shulman,Matthew Mella,Altynbek Zhubanchaliyev,Fabian J. Theis*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Chem-PerturBridge 整合了 125 万个异构转录组样本，通过标准化处理解决了数据碎片化问题，并被证明能显著提升化合物表征学习的效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前用于小分子建模的转录组资源高度碎片化，存在技术平台不统一、元数据标注混乱及预处理流程差异大等问题，限制了大规模扰动模型（Large perturbation models）的开发与泛化能力。

Method: 研究人员开发了 Chem-PerturBridge，通过标准化不同技术、元数据、实验条件和预处理流程，整合了来自8种不同检测类型、涵盖3.7万种化合物和136种细胞背景的125万个转录组样本。通过计算匹配条件和重复样本间的一致性，对比了不同数据集的表达谱差异；并利用该资源进行预训练，在化合物表征学习任务（如 OP3 评估）中验证了其性能。

Result: 研究发现：1）跨数据集的细粒度 logFC 数值一致性较弱；2）logFC 的方向性一致性相对稳定；3）基于 Chem-PerturBridge 预训练的模型在化合物表征学习（如 OP3 分割和 molecule-holdout 任务）中，显著优于仅使用 L1000 数据或传统化学描述符的模型。

Conclusion: Chem-PerturBridge 作为一种大规模、标准化的多源转录组数据集，通过整合异构数据弥合了现有资源碎片化的鸿沟。该研究强调了在处理跨数据集转录组数据时，定性的方向性一致性比定量的强度值更可靠，并证实了该资源在提升化合物表征学习能力方面的有效性。

Abstract: Large perturbation models require training data encompassing chemical, cellular, and assay diversity. Current transcriptomic resources for small-molecule modeling, however, are fragmented across technologies, metadata conventions, controls, doses, and preprocessing pipelines. We introduce Chem-PerturBridge, a harmonized multi-dataset resource comprising over 37k compounds, 136 cellular contexts, and 1.25M transcriptomic samples across eight assay types, with standardized identifiers, metadata, and replicate-aware condition-level effects. We use the resource to evaluate matched-condition agreement across datasets and replicate agreement within datasets. Matched same-compound conditions generally show weak agreement in fine-grained logFC rankings and magnitudes across most dataset pairs, often falling below same-context different-compound baselines. In contrast, logFC direction agreement is substantially more stable and usually exceeds these baselines. We further evaluate Chem-PerturBridge as a pretraining resource for compound representation learning. Under a compound-held-out OP3 evaluation split, embeddings pretrained on Chem-PerturBridge improve over L1000-only embeddings, Morgan fingerprints, and the descriptor-free OP3 baseline across metrics. An extensive molecule-holdout evaluation across 11 datasets further shows that models trained on Chem-PerturBridge outperform or match those that are not. Chem-PerturBridge therefore supports both diagnostic evaluation of cross-dataset signature agreement and model-oriented reuse of heterogeneous perturbation transcriptomic data.

</details>


### [239] [Value Functions as Supermartingale Certificates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31524)
*Alessandro Abate,Daniel Contro,Mirco Giacobbe,Agustín Martínez-Suñé,Diptarko Roy*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文建立了一个理论框架，证明了强化学习的价值函数可以作为随机系统满足ω-正则属性的“超鞅证书”，从而为在复杂状态空间中通过强化学习实现具有形式化保证的策略合成提供了理论支持。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随机系统的形式化验证方法（基于超鞅证书）虽能提供强有力的数学保证，但在复杂或无限状态空间中难以合成；而强化学习虽然擅长处理复杂空间下的策略优化，却往往缺乏形式化的合规性保障。本文旨在桥接这两者，通过强化学习自动合成具有形式化证明的验证证书。

Method: 本文提出了一种连接强化学习（RL）与随机系统形式化验证的新框架。核心方法是通过设计特定的奖励函数，将求解满足ω-正则属性的策略问题转化为强化学习问题。研究证明，在最优策略下，该属性的价值函数能够自然地推导出Streett超鞅（supermartingale）证书，从而实现对连续及无限状态空间中系统性质的有效验证。

Result: 研究在理论上确立了强化学习价值函数与Streett超鞅证书之间的映射关系，适用于有限、可数无限及连续状态空间。实验在有限马尔可夫决策过程（MDP）上验证了该方法的有效性，表明强化学习能够被用作一种合成形式化验证证书的原则性手段。

Conclusion: 本文通过建立强化学习与形式化验证之间的理论联系，证明了在特定奖励函数下，满足ω-正则属性的强化学习策略价值函数实质上即为相应的Streett超鞅证书。这一发现为利用强化学习进行形式化证书的自动化合成开辟了新途径，解决了在复杂状态空间中难以通过传统方法直接获取验证证书的难题。

Abstract: Certification methods for stochastic systems provide sufficient proof rules, based on real-valued supermartingale certificates, to determine the almost-sure satisfaction of $ω$-regular properties (and therefore of linear temporal logic) over general state spaces, encompassing both countably infinite and continuous state spaces. Conversely, reinforcement learning (RL) methods for $ω$-regular tasks have received considerable attention, but they typically lack formal guarantees that the learned policy satisfies the specification, except possibly for finite state and action spaces. We bridge these two lines of research by establishing a novel theoretical connection: under an appropriate reward, the value function associated to a policy that almost surely satisfies an $ω$-regular property encodes a Streett supermartingale certificate for that specification. Our results, validated experimentally on finite Markov decision processes, hold for finite, countably infinite, and continuous state spaces, suggesting a principled route to certificate synthesis via RL.

</details>


### [240] [The Dynamic-Probabilistic Consistency Gap in Chaotic Surrogate Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31547)
*Andre Herz,Matthijs Pals,Daniel Durstewitz,Georgia Koppe*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对动态系统重构中预测动力学与不确定性估计不一致的问题（DPC 差距），作者提出了基于可微扩展卡尔曼滤波的 KAFFEE 框架，显著改善了对复杂混沌系统的建模精度与鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在动态系统重构（DSR）中，现有的概率模型在优化有限视界目标时，往往会产生“动态-概率一致性（DPC）差距”，导致动力学特征退化或不确定性估计与系统真实的局部切向动力学脱节。该研究旨在解决这一机制性偏差。

Method: 提出了 KAFFEE（Kalman-Aware Framework For Ergodic Emulation）框架。该方法基于可微扩展卡尔曼滤波（EKF），通过在局部预测残差（新息）上评估似然，并将协方差通过学习到的局部雅可比矩阵进行传播，而非使用传统的开环高斯展开目标。

Result: 在随机超混沌 Lorenz-96 系统上，KAFFEE 有效减少了模型失效模式，显著提升了动力学不变量的重构精度。此外，在跨 13 个混沌系统的基础模型迁移实验中，KAFFEE 在保持零样本动力学建模能力的同时，实现了有效的上下文贝叶斯滤波。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了动态系统重构中概率目标与动力学一致性之间的潜在冲突，通过 KAFFEE 框架验证了利用扩展卡尔曼滤波进行梯度优化能够有效弥合这一差距，从而实现高保真的动力学预测与不确定性量化。

Abstract: Dynamical systems reconstruction (DSR) aims to learn surrogate models that capture the dynamics underlying time-series data. Reliably deploying these surrogates requires uncertainty estimates consistent with the learned dynamics. We expose a dynamic-probabilistic consistency (DPC) gap: the pursuit of finite-horizon probabilistic objectives can degrade dynamics or decouple predictive uncertainty from the local tangent dynamics it ought to reflect. We isolate three mechanisms behind this gap: core collapse, noise masking, and blind uncertainty. Specifically, we show that open-loop Gaussian rollout objectives can penalize Jacobian-generated covariance growth in chaotic systems, encouraging optimization shortcuts that weaken physical expansion or decouple uncertainty from it. To mitigate this gap, we propose KAFFEE (Kalman-Aware Framework For Ergodic Emulation), a differentiable extended Kalman filter-based training framework that evaluates likelihood on local predictive residuals (innovations) while transporting covariance through learned local Jacobians. On stochastic hyperchaotic Lorenz-96, KAFFEE reduces the identified failure modes, improves reconstruction of dynamical invariants relative to open-loop objectives, and maintains competitive predictive scores. We further show that the DPC gap appears when probabilistically adapting a DSR foundation model across 13 chaotic systems, where KAFFEE enables in-context Bayesian filtering while largely preserving zero-shot dynamics.

</details>


### [241] [Functional Attention: From Pairwise Affinities to Functional Correspondences](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31559)
*Jiefang Xiao,Maolin Gao,Simon Weber,Guandao Yang,Daniel Cremers*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种“功能性注意力”机制，将Transformer的注意力重构为自适应基之间的函数映射，从而高效捕捉连续场的全局结构，实现了具有分辨率不变性的高性能算子学习。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前的Transformer算子学习方法通常将连续域上的函数视为离散的Token进行处理，这种离散化方式忽略了底层数据的连续场本质和全局函数结构，导致模型在处理不同分辨率数据时的泛化能力和效率受限。

Method: 该研究提出了“功能性注意力（Functional Attention）”机制。它放弃了传统Transformer中基于Token的Softmax亲和力计算，转而受到几何函数映射（Functional Maps）的启发，利用结构化的线性算子在自适应基之间建立映射，从而在数学上显式捕捉全局函数结构。

Result: 实验结果表明，该方法在求解偏微分方程（PDEs）、3D分割和回归等多种算子学习任务中达到了最先进（SOTA）的性能水平，且对不同的离散化网格表现出极强的鲁棒性和分辨率不变性。

Conclusion: 功能性注意力（Functional Attention）通过将注意力机制重塑为自适应基函数之间的函数对应关系，成功克服了传统基于Token的注意力机制在处理连续场时的局限性，提供了一种更高效、具有分辨率不变性的算子学习新范式。

Abstract: Learning mappings between infinite-dimensional function spaces, or operator learning, is essential for many machine learning applications. Although transformer-based operators are popular, they often rely on token-wise attention. These methods treat continuous fields as discrete tokens and usually ignore the global functional structure. We introduce \emph{Functional Attention}, which reinterprets attention as a functional correspondence between adaptive bases. Inspired by geometric functional maps, our method replaces softmax affinities with structured linear operators. This yields a compact, generalizable, resolution-invariant representation that explicitly captures global dependencies. Experiments demonstrate that \emph{Functional Attention} can match state-of-the-art performance in many operator learning tasks, including solving PDEs, 3D segmentation, and regression, while remaining robust to varying discretizations. Project page is available at https://github.com/xjffff/FUNCATTN.

</details>


### [242] [Effective Biological Representation Learning by Masking Gene Expression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31562)
*Kian Kenyon-Dean,Alina Selega,Ihab Bendidi,Jordan M. Sorokin,Luca Bertinetto,David Errington,Hayley Donnella,Oren Kraus*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的转录组基础模型（FMs）在面对 RNA-seq 数据中的技术噪声和批次效应时，性能往往不及简单的线性基线模型，这引发了对深度表征学习在转录组数据中实际价值的质疑。因此，本文旨在探索如何通过改进模型架构和数据整理来提升深度表示学习的性能。

Method: 提出了一种名为 TxFM 的自监督学习模型，采用针对 RNA-seq 计数数据优化的掩码自编码器（Masked Autoencoder）架构；构建了名为 DiverseRNA-1.4M 的高质量训练语料库，并进行了详尽的消融实验以确定最优架构配置。

Result: TxFM 模型在 DiverseRNA-1.4M 数据集上训练后，产生的基因表示具有高保真度，且性能优于规模大 100 倍以上的地图集规模语料库（atlas-scale corpora）训练的现有模型。

Conclusion: 研究表明，通过精心设计的模型架构与高质量的数据整理，归纳式自监督学习是转录组表示学习的可行且有效的路径，能够生成高质量的基因表示。

Abstract: RNA sequencing produces rich and diverse datasets of gene expression, offering compelling insights into cellular state and function that have many applications in drug discovery. Modeling such data is challenging due to inherent technical noise and experimental batch effects, as evidenced by many existing transcriptomic foundation models (FMs) underperforming relative to linear baselines. Such results raise the question of whether deep representation learning provides a distinct advantage over the direct use of raw transcript counts. Our work explores this by developing a new self-supervised model, TxFM, with a focus on inductive representation learning evaluations. TxFM employs a masked autoencoding approach tailored to diverse RNA-seq count data, and our ablation study empirically identifies crucial architecture configurations required for strong transfer performance. Additionally, we curate a public training corpus, DiverseRNA-1.4M, and find that TxFM trained on this curated dataset yields high-fidelity gene representations that outperform FMs trained on atlas-scale corpora over 100x larger. Overall, our results indicate that inductive self-supervised learning is a viable modeling approach for transcriptomics representation, provided a careful synthesis of model architecture and training data curation.

### [243] [Giving Sensors a Voice: Multimodal JEPA for Semantic Time-Series Embeddings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31580)
*Utsav Dutta,Gerardo Pastrana,Sina Khoshfetrat Pakazad,Henrik Ohlsson*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: CHARM 是一种新型多元时间序列表示学习模型，通过结合通道文本描述、Transformer 编码器和联合嵌入预测架构（JEPA），在无需复杂微调的情况下，实现了跨多种时间序列任务的卓越性能与解释性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前基于 Transformer 的架构在语言和视觉领域已取得显著进展，但针对异构多元时间序列的通用表示学习研究尚不充分。现有的模型往往难以在不同数据集和不同任务间实现良好的泛化。

Method: 1. 架构设计：提出 CHARM 模型，该模型将通道级文本描述集成到对通道顺序等变的 Transformer 编码器中；2. 训练机制：采用联合嵌入预测架构（JEPA），通过潜在空间预测来提升对传感器噪声的鲁棒性；3. 损失函数：引入一种促进信息量大且时间稳定的嵌入损失函数；4. 解释性机制：利用描述感知门控（description-aware gating）来学习通道间的关系。

Result: 在异常检测、分类以及短、长期预测任务中，CHARM 仅使用线性探测器（linear probe）即可获得优异的性能。实验表明，JEPA 目标函数和条件架构是提升性能的关键，而文本描述则有效地充当了跨数据集泛化的通道标识符。

Conclusion: CHARM 证明了通过结合通道文本描述和联合嵌入预测架构（JEPA），可以有效地学习异构多元时间序列的通用表示。这种方法不仅提升了模型在多任务（异常检测、分类、预测）下的性能，还通过描述感知门控机制增强了模型的解释性，为跨数据集泛化提供了有效路径。

Abstract: Transformer-based architectures have advanced sequence modeling in language and vision, yet general-purpose representation learning for heterogeneous multivariate time series remains underexplored. We introduce CHARM (Channel-Aware Representation Model), which incorporates channel-level textual descriptions into a Transformer encoder equivariant to channel order. CHARM is trained with a Joint Embedding Predictive Architecture (JEPA) and a novel loss promoting informative, temporally stable embeddings; latent-space prediction encourages robustness to sensor noise while description-aware gating provides interpretability through learned inter-channel relationships. Across anomaly detection, classification, and short- and long-term forecasting, the learned embeddings achieve strong performance using only a linear probe. Performance is driven primarily by the JEPA objective and conditioning architecture, with text descriptions serving as channel identifiers for cross-dataset generalization.

</details>
